## THH-01 迷途的脚印 / A Trail of Footprints

被雨水润湿的土壤，微微凹陷的脚印。\
Rain-soaked soil. Shallow footprints.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

雇佣兵打扮的女性单膝跪地，她的眼睛正发着灼目的亮光。\
A mercenary in a wide-brimmed hat kneels on one knee, her left eye glowing brightly.

**阿尔古斯**：脚长10.6英寸。\
**Argus**: 10.6 inches long.

脚印下的泥土并不平整，有一侧更深地印进泥土中。\
The soil beneath the footprint is uneven. One side presses deeper into the ground.

**阿尔古斯**：跛足。\
**Argus**: Signs of limping.

步幅大，压痕重，有挖痕。\
Wide stride, heavy indentations, a slight drag.

**阿尔古斯**：男。\
**Argus**: Male.

中前掌压痕重，后跟则较轻。前尖挖痕大，后跟擦痕相对较少。\
Heavy pressure on the forefoot, lighter on the heel. Deep scrapes at the front, fewer at the back.

**阿尔古斯**：……20岁左右。\
**Argus**: Around 20 years old.

运步轻便，脚印前掌压力不均匀。\
Light on his feet, uneven pressure on the forefoot.

**阿尔古斯**：体重低。\
**Argus**: Light-weight.

她感到头皮作痒，用猎枪的枪管用力地戳了戳痒处。\
She scratches her scalp with the barrel of her shotgun.

行得越远，那些脚印愈发的杂乱——更多的线索出现了。\
The further she goes, the more irregular the footprints become—and the more clues emerge.

**阿尔古斯**：……人数变多了。\
**Argus**: More sets of footprints here.

不远处传来了草叶摩擦的沙沙声。随之一并涌入耳中的，还有细微的人语。\
There's a rustling in the grass nearby, along with the faint sound of a conversation.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：老大，那位大人所需要的材料就在这儿吗？\
**"Order" Follower I**: Boss, are you sure this is where the materials for the revered one are?

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：可是……这里没有农宅，更别说是集市了！\
**"Order" Follower I**: There isn't even a single trace of human activity here, let alone a market!

**“启明会”信众Ⅱ**：……\
**"Order" Follower II**: ...

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：所以……只剩下一种可能——材料是这些植物，对吗？\
**"Order" Follower I**: I guess the only possible explanation is we're here for these plants, right?

**“启明会”信众Ⅱ**：蠢货，这当然不是。\
**"Order" Follower II**: Of course not, you idiot.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：哈哈，真可惜！我还想说，割草正是我最擅长的活计之一。您看我掌心的这些茧子……虽然老妈总嫌弃我笨手笨脚。\
**"Order" Follower I**: Haha, that's too bad! I'm great at harvesting plants. I'm a pro, see? Check out these calluses. Although, my mom would probably disagree.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：我想那应该是些需要细致对待的玩意儿。所以，您得告诉我它们长什么样，以免被我当成杂草。\
**"Order" Follower I**: Do you have any idea what these materials look like? They must be important, so we better handle them with care. Don't wanna risk mistaking them for weeds, you know.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：毕竟我的腿伤还没好，路都走不顺，更别说那些精细的活计了。\
**"Order" Follower I**: I hope they're easy enough to find. With my leg messed up like this, I can hardly handle any delicate work.

**阿尔古斯**：是了……一个跛足的男人。\
**Argus**: That's him. The one with the limp.

**“启明会”信众Ⅱ**：抱歉。\
**"Order" Follower II**: Sorry about this, man.

遥远而模糊的上膛声。\
There's a distant sound of a gun being cocked.

**“启明会”信众Ⅱ**：我想，她此刻应当正在天堂等您。\
**"Order" Follower II**: But at least you'll see your mom soon, up there in heaven.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：什、什么……\
**"Order" Follower I**: Wh-What?

“砰——”\
*bang*

雇佣兵果决地按下了扳机，子弹擦伤了施暴者的面颊。\
The mercenary decisively pulls the trigger of her shotgun. The bullet grazes the assailant's cheek.

**“启明会”信众Ⅱ**：——谁？！\
**"Order" Follower II**: Who's there?!

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：……！\
**"Order" Follower I**: ...

**阿尔古斯**：还不走？\
**Argus**: What're you waiting for? Get your ass outta here.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：我……\
**"Order" Follower I**: I ...

那双颤抖的手泄露了他的不安和惊惧。\
His trembling hands betray his fear and panic.

**阿尔古斯**：也是，我想你应该会需要问他一些问题……\
**Argus**: Ah. You got a couple questions for this one too, huh?

**阿尔古斯**：但，抱歉，我先来的。\
**Argus**: Well, first come, first served.

**阿尔古斯**：不介意的话，你可以当第二个。\
**Argus**: I'm afraid you're gonna have to get in line.

她一脚踩住男人的胸膛，把枪管压在了男人的喉咙上。\
She steps on the man's chest and presses the barrel of her gun against his throat.

**阿尔古斯**：听着，老兄。\
**Argus**: Alright, here's how we're gonna do this.

**阿尔古斯**：我有话要问你，有什么就说什么，不然我就会打穿你的喉咙。\
**Argus**: I ask. You answer. If you lie, I'll blow your jaw off.

**阿尔古斯**：你见过一个叫“凯拉”的女孩吗？\
**Argus**: Have you ever met a girl named Kayla?

**“启明会”信众Ⅱ**：凯、凯拉……？\
**"Order" Follower II**: Kayla?

**阿尔古斯**：我换一个问法。\
**Argus**: Let's try that again.

**阿尔古斯**：你是否见过一个女孩，她大概有5英尺3英寸高，栗色头发，翠绿色的眼珠，有德克萨斯的口音……\
**Argus**: A girl, about 5 foot 3, chestnut hair, emerald green eyes, speaks like a Texan.

**阿尔古斯**：你见过吗？是，或者不是。\
**Argus**: Have you seen her? Yes or no?

男人惊恐地以一个小幅度摇头。\
The man shakes his head in terror.

**阿尔古斯**：不是？\
**Argus**: No?

她忽然露出了一个笑容。\
She smirks.

**阿尔古斯**：那你的表袋里怎么会有凯拉的发卡？\
**Argus**: Then why's her hair clip in your pocket?

她压了压枪管，男人在感受到喉咙处紧压着的重量之后，意识到了情况并非自己所想象的那样简单。\
She presses down harder, jamming the shotgun into his throat.

**“启明会”信众Ⅱ**：我知道，有一个和你的描述很相似的人——她5英尺3英寸，栗色头发，总爱挎个小篮子……甚至也叫做凯拉！\
**"Order" Follower II**: I-I remember! There's a girl, 5 foot 3, chestnut hair. She's always carrying a basket. Her name's Kayla, too!

**“启明会”信众Ⅱ**：但唯独有一点——她的眼睛不是翠绿色的，而是另、另外一种颜色……\
**"Order" Follower II**: But her eyes ain't emerald green. They're ... They're ...

男人徒劳地张着嘴巴，他竭力从脑海中搜寻着那位名叫凯拉的少女。她的眼睛到底是什么颜色？\
The man's mouth opens helplessly as he desperately tries to remember the color of the girl's eyes.

一个有关于颜色的词抵在舌尖，但他却无法吐出它——那个他应当记得，但却在此刻被遗忘的关键信息。\
It's on the tip of his tongue, but he can't seem to spit it out—the crucial detail he should remember but has now forgotten.

**阿尔古斯**：继续说，你是怎么拿到这只发卡的——越详细越好。\
**Argus**: Tell me how you got this hair clip—the more detailed, the better.

**“启明会”信众Ⅱ**：那只是一次很短暂的会面……那个姑娘遗失了她的发卡。发卡很漂亮，我想带给我自己的女儿……\
**"Order" Follower II**: We just bumped into each other by chance. She dropped it on the road, and I thought my daughter would like it, so I ...

抛弃了关于颜色的思考，男人从善如流地说道。\
Relieved to have moved on from the color, the man blabbers on obediently.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

她的食指紧扣扳机。\
Her finger tightens on the trigger.

**阿尔古斯**：你还有最后一次机会。\
**Argus**: I'll give you one last chance.

**阿尔古斯**：告诉我，你是在哪里遇见她的？\
**Argus**: Where did you meet?

**“启明会”信众Ⅱ**：……\
**"Order" Follower II**: ...

**“启明会”信众Ⅱ**：我在一个叫蓝手帕旅馆的地方遇见她的……\
**"Order" Follower II**: At a place called Tuesday's Motel.

**阿尔古斯**：早说不就行了。\
**Argus**: There you go. That wasn't so hard, was it?

她掂了掂手中的猎枪，用枪柄砸晕了眼前的男人。\
She hefts the shotgun and knocks the man out with the butt.

**阿尔古斯**：废话真多。\
**Argus**: Next time, just spit it out. Save us all some time.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：……您、您是“基金会”的人吗？\
**"Order" Follower I**: Are-Are you with the Foundation?

**阿尔古斯**：基金会？\
**Argus**: The Foundation?

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：是、是的……他们很讨厌“基金会”……\
**"Order" Follower I**: Yeah. They hate the Foundation, you see.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：但是您救了我！老妈也会需要……\
**"Order" Follower I**: But you saved me! I need some help. My mom ...

雇佣兵强硬地打断了他。\
The mercenary cuts him off harshly.

**阿尔古斯**：我不认识你口中的“基金会”，也不想了解你们之间的矛盾，我还有其他要做的事。\
**Argus**: I ain't never heard of no "Foundation," and I don't give a you-know-what about what's going on between you and them. Got my own matters to deal with.

**阿尔古斯**：他晕在了这里，枪也在这里——现在你能够给他一个结局了，不是吗？\
**Argus**: I'll leave him with you. Keep the gun. You figure the rest out yourself.

稀薄的云遮住了将落未落的太阳，它看起来就像一个被搅碎的蛋黄。\
A thin cloud obscures the setting sun, scattering its light.

她若有所思地望着远方的太阳。\
She looks out into the horizon.

**阿尔古斯**：……告诉我，蓝手帕旅馆在哪？\
**Argus**: Now, where's this motel?

年轻的追随者颤抖地指向更南方，那儿天幕昏黄，远处有着隐约可见的星光。红土地温驯地伏在低处；犁沟起伏，如绵延的脊梁。\
The young follower points a trembling finger southward, where the stars have started to appear in the sky. The red lowlands lie still, their furrows rising and falling gently.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：等等！您救了我的命，我必须得告诉您，那座旅馆……\
**"Order" Follower I**: Listen! You saved my life, so I owe you one. I have to warn you, that motel—

**阿尔古斯**：顺手而已，废话就不必再说了。\
**Argus**: Save your breath. We're done here.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：不！\
**"Order" Follower I**: Wait!

追随者急忙从口袋中翻出几张面额不大的美钞。\
The follower hurriedly pulls out a few dollar bills from his pocket.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：看您的打扮，是一位雇佣兵？我……我很担心我的母亲，如果您在路上见到了我母亲的踪迹……\
**"Order" Follower I**: You're a mercenary, right? I can tell by your gear. I'm, I'm worried about my mother. If you see her on the road, please give me a call.

他犹豫了片刻，从脖子上摘下了一枚金属吊坠。\
He hesitates for a moment before taking off a metal locket from around his neck.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：我母亲长这个样子。\
**"Order" Follower I**: Here's a photo of her.

雇佣兵接过了吊坠，照片中慈祥的妇人正对着她微笑。\
The mercenary opens the locket to reveal an elderly woman with a kind smile.

**阿尔古斯**：我记住了。\
**Argus**: Got it.

她将吊坠回递给了追随者。\
She hands it back to the follower.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：还有……这是我的电话。\
**"Order" Follower I**: And here. My phone number.

追随者在钞票的空白处写下了一串数字。\
He writes a series of numbers on a blank section of one banknote.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：除此以外，我必须得告诉您，那个旅馆有异常……您要小心。\
**"Order" Follower I**: And listen, be careful. Something ain't right about that motel.

**阿尔古斯**：好的。\
**Argus**: Alright.

她收下了钱，将写着电话号码的纸条塞入兜中，转身离开了这个地方。\
She takes the money, slips the dollar bill with the phone number into her pocket, and turns away.

日照的余热散落在公路上，雇佣兵拎着那柄枪，重新回到了她的车旁。\
The afternoon heat lingers on the highway. The mercenary makes her way back to her car, shotgun in hand.

在即将到达之时，她罕见地停下了脚步。\
She comes to a sudden stop.

**？？？**：一只羊，两只羊，三只羊……\
**???**: One sheep, two sheep, three sheep ...

细弱的声音自远方传来，她隐约看到一团雪白的毛绒正围着那辆牧马人越野车打转。\
A soft voice echoes from afar, and she notices a fluffy white figure circling around her car.

**阿尔古斯**：……羊？\
**Argus**: Is that a sheep?

雪白的毛绒赫然地转过了脸——那是一位羊首人身的神秘学家。\
The fluffy creature turns its head. It's a sheep-headed, human-bodied arcanist.

**？？？**：嗯，接下来是两只羊，三只羊……就像所有孩童初学数字那样，大部分人每天都需要重温睡眠这个课题。\
**???**: Hm. Two sheep, three sheep ... Funny how we hit the hay every night, just like kids hit the books every day.

**数羊羔**：很高兴见到您，我是数羊羔。\
**Barbara**: I'm Barbara. Nice to meet you.

羊首人身的神秘学家伸出了一只手——这符合见面的礼节。但她并没有得到期望的结果。\
The sheep-headed arcanist extends a hand—a gesture befitting an introduction. But she doesn't get the expected response.

**阿尔古斯**：让开，我得走了。\
**Argus**: You're in my way, ma'am.

**数羊羔**：挥手法、呼喊法、电话求援法……我尝试了很多方法来搭顺风车。\
**Barbara**: I've tried waving and shouting at the drivers, but none of them stopped for me.

**数羊羔**：现在尝试的是踱步法——它派上了用场，我很高兴。\
**Barbara**: Thankfully, pacing around on the road seems to have done the trick!

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

**阿尔古斯**：真啰嗦，如果你想搭车的话，我现在就可以回答你。\
**Argus**: Listen. If you need a ride, here's my answer.

她关上了车门，望向窗外的搭车客。\
She gets in, closes the door, and looks at the hitchhiker through the open window.

**阿尔古斯**：不行。\
**Argus**: No.

**数羊羔**：原本的司机丢下我离开了。原因大概是在车行至中途的时候，车顶上传来了一些刮擦声——瞧，只是一些摩擦声就能把他吓成那样。\
**Barbara**: My driver left me here. Probably because of that scraping sound on the car roof. That scared him half to death.

**数羊羔**：一切异常都有其成因。所以，我觉得我来对了地方。\
**Barbara**: Everything happens for a reason. Destiny's brought me to the right place, I think.

**数羊羔**：——您能载我一程吗？这是公务行程，价格好谈。\
**Barbara**: Could you give me a ride? I'm on a business trip, so money is no object.

**阿尔古斯**：和钱没关系。\
**Argus**: It ain't about money.

**数羊羔**：噢，令人失望的回答，但我完全理解——保持警惕是好事，小姐。不过……\
**Barbara**: Oh, a disappointing answer, but I understand. One must be vigilant. If you don't mind me asking, Miss ...

**数羊羔**：您的眼睛为什么这样的红？我不建议您在这种情况下继续行驶，这容易导致危险的发生。\
**Barbara**: What happened to your eyes? They're bloodshot. It's best not to drive with your eyes in such a state. You have a much higher chance of getting into an accident.

**阿尔古斯**：这也不是你该关心的事，羊羔小姐。\
**Argus**: That ain't none of your concern, Miss Sheep.

**阿尔古斯**：再见。\
**Argus**: See ya.

雇佣兵关闭了车窗，喋喋不休的噪音终于被中止了。\
The mercenary closes the window, finally blocking out the endless chatter.

她转动钥匙，给车子打上了火。电台启动，喧嚷的迪斯科音乐在车内回荡，发出震耳欲聋的响声。\
She turns the ignition key, and the radio bursts to life, blaring disco music inside the vehicle.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

她恶狠狠地关闭了音响，踩下了油门。\
She shuts it off and stomps on the gas.

发动机震颤着，速度指针不断地攀升。而道路两旁花色的田野上，有牧人正呼唤着羊群。\
The engine roars as the speedometer climbs higher and higher. In the fields on either side of the road, shepherds are herding their sheep.

一些回忆不合时宜地在眼前闪现。\
Unwelcome memories begin to surface.

山脚的土地长满了印第安草，在临近秋天的时候，它的叶子会呈现出晚霞般的红色。\
The land at the foot of the hills is covered in Indian grass, now turning a sunset red as autumn approaches.

**凯拉**：阿尔古斯，你看这只小羊羔……它险些死在了妈妈的肚子里。\
**Kayla**: Argus, come over here. This little lamb almost didn't make it outta her mama's belly.

女孩用剪子割断了羔羊的脐带。母羊卧在草堆中，发出虚弱的呼唤。\
The girl cuts the lamb's umbilical cord with a pair of scissors, while the ewe lies in the hay, baaing weakly.

**阿尔古斯**：那是它命不好。\
**Argus**: That's life.

**凯拉**：别这样，没有什么东西是为了死去而降临在这个世界上的——阿尔古斯，你看，它站起来了。\
**Kayla**: Don't say that. No living thing is born to suffer. Look, it's already standing.

母羊低垂着头颅，舔舐着湿润的胎衣，幼小的羊崽子勉力站稳了脚跟。\
The ewe licks off the afterbirth as the lamb struggles to stand on its shaky legs.

**凯拉**：哈，多可爱的小羊。\
**Kayla**: Hah. What an adorable little thing.

她欣喜地在围裙上擦拭着自己沾满了羊水与血迹的双手。\
She grins as she wipes the blood and fluid from her hands onto her apron.

**凯拉**：天要黑了，我们得带着它们回去——在母羊受伤的情况下，它们一定活不过今晚。\
**Kayla**: It's getting dark. We should take them back. Ain't no way they'll make it through the night out here with their mama hurt.

**凯拉**：更何况，天一黑，你的眼睛就什么都看不见了。\
**Kayla**: And you can't see a thing at night.

**阿尔古斯**：……好。\
**Argus**: You're right. Let's go.

野地的风吹拂着那些遒劲的草叶，那声音随着风的行迹而愈发遥远。\
The wind sweeps through the grass and rustles into the distance.

**阿尔古斯**：该死的——\
**Argus**: Screw it!

阿尔古斯咬了咬牙，将方向盘转到极限。\
Argus grits her teeth and yanks the steering wheel, screeching her car into a U-turn.

她猛踩油门，以最短的时间回到了那个地方，那名形似小羊的神秘学家应该伫立着的地方。\
She slams on the gas, rushing back to where the sheep-like arcanist was.

但路旁空空如也，只有几株棉桃正在随风摇曳。\
But when she arrives, there's nothing but a few cotton plants swaying in the breeze.

**阿尔古斯**：……他*的。\
**Argus**: Should've minded my own damn business.

这是一次失败的尝试。她再次拧动方向盘，比上一次更急，橡胶轮胎发出了不受控制的哀嚎。\
She turns the wheel again, harder this time. The tires screech as she makes another U-turn and drives off.

远方的太阳在此刻回归了群山的怀抱。\
In the distance, the sun dips behind the hills.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

视线正在逐渐变暗，她不抱希望地点亮了车灯。\
Her vision is fading. She switches on the headlights.

然而，车灯的光线微弱。它远不足以照亮因夜盲症而导致的黑暗。\
As expected, the light is too dim to make up for her night blindness. She can hardly see a thing.

**阿尔古斯**：——！\
**Argus**: ...!

一脚刹车。\
A hard brake.

“砰——”\
*bang*

很遗憾，刺耳的脚刹声没能阻止一场车祸的发生。\
Unfortunately, it's too late to stop the crash.

## THH-02 浓雾天 / Fog Descends

**维尔汀**：在此之前，TTT告诉了我一个关于德克萨斯的都市怪谈。\
**Vertin**: Before we left, TTT was telling me an urban myth about Texas.

**红弩箭**：哦？说来听听。\
**Lilya**: Hah. Sounds about right. What's the story about?

故事的开头设计得很典型。\
The story starts off in the typical way.

一个疲惫的司机在德克萨斯的一条公路上开车，偶然遭遇了一个搭便车的女孩。\
A man was driving down a long Texas road when he saw a girl hitch-hiking.

司机让她上了车，并请她吃了一块巧克力。\
He offered her a lift and a piece of chocolate.

女孩在一处墓园下了车，司机继续朝前开——尽管是深夜，但他依然希望能够快些到达目的地。\
The man dropped the girl off at a cemetery and drove on. It was late at night, so he was hoping to reach his destination quickly.

没过多久，马路上却出现了一支送葬的队伍。\
Soon after, he saw a funeral procession going down the road.

那张遗照似曾相识。\
The photo of the dead seemed familiar.

偶然迸发的好奇心驱使着他，于是他随着送葬队伍去了墓园。\
Curiosity came over him, and he followed them to the cemetery.

看，是巧克力。\
Look, a piece of chocolate.

叮铃铃——

一阵骤然的响声打断了她的叙述。\
A sudden beeping interrupts her story.

**维尔汀**：稍等，是基金会的通讯。\
**Vertin**: Give me a moment. I have to take this. It's from the Foundation.

打开通讯器之后，接待员冷淡的声音一如既往。\
The voice on the other side is as calm as ever.

**通讯器**：司辰，我们接到了一则紧急通知——位于美国德克萨斯州的芝诺基地进行了大规模的撤离。\
**Communicator**: Timekeeper, this is an emergency notice. The Zeno Base in Texas, USA, has conducted a large-scale evacuation.

**通讯器**：芝诺方目前尚未给出具体的理由。\
**Communicator**: Zeno has not yet responded regarding their actions.

**通讯器**：如果您在旅途中遇到任何困难，请及时向总部汇报与寻求帮助。\
**Communicator**: Should you encounter any difficulties on your trip there, please contact headquarters immediately.

**维尔汀**：明白了。\
**Vertin**: Understood.

**通讯器**：那么，我再次与您确认一下此次的任务。\
**Communicator**: Despite these developments, your mission remains the same.

**通讯器**：UTTU的编辑数羊羔近日前往77号公路进行取材，基金会需要您尽快与这位编辑接洽，以获取兀尔德的下落——\
**Communicator**: Contact UTTU editor Barbara, who was last seen near Route 77 collecting information, and find Urd's current whereabouts through her.

**通讯器**：UTTU的编辑以特殊的通路传达讯息，基金会仍在调查中，若有进一步的进展，我们将及时与您联系。\
**Communicator**: Since UTTU editors use a special communication channel, her current location is still unknown. We'll be in touch as soon as there's any new information.

**通讯器**：您还有别的疑问吗？\
**Communicator**: Any questions, Timekeeper?

**维尔汀**：没有。\
**Vertin**: No. Thank you.

**通讯器**：那么，祝您一切顺利。\
**Communicator**: All the best, then.

通讯结束了，位于后座的飞行女巫若有所思。\
The communication ends. Lilya looks thoughtful.

**红弩箭**：那群人给了什么新消息吗？\
**Lilya**: What did they say?

**维尔汀**：在德克萨斯州的芝诺基地进行了大规模的撤离。\
**Vertin**: There was a mass evacuation at the Zeno base in Texas.

**红弩箭**：啧——搞什么啊。\
**Lilya**: Tsk. What's that all about?

**红弩箭**：前两天，那些芝诺高层刚告诉我——红色38还在德克萨斯的军备工厂进行检修。\
**Lilya**: They called me two days ago, saying that Red 38 was still under routine maintenance in their armament factory.

**红弩箭**：结果今天就撤离了？见鬼，那我的红色38怎么办？\
**Lilya**: But now, all of a sudden, they're gone? How am I going to get my Red 38 back now, huh?

**红弩箭**：如果没有这次例行检修，我们完全不用花这么多时间在路上……\
**Lilya**: If they hadn't taken her away for inspection, we wouldn't be traveling in this little car, wasting all day on the road.

**维尔汀**：接线员说，这是一次大规模的撤离，也许他们还留有一些人手在维持工厂的正常运转。\
**Vertin**: The operator only mentioned an evacuation. It's still possible that some of them have stayed behind to keep the factory running.

**维尔汀**：如果你担心这些，可以直接去军备工厂看看——它位于奇索斯镇，路途并不算太远。\
**Vertin**: If you're worried about Red 38, we can take a detour there. It's in Chisos. The town isn't far from here.

飞行员蜷缩在座位之上，显然心情并不美妙。\
Lilya squirms in her seat.

**红弩箭**：嘿，司机，能送我们到奇索斯镇吗？只是绕个圈，不远。\
**Lilya**: Hey, mister, can you take us to the Chisos? It's just a little detour.

**司机**：嗯……\
**Driver**: Hmm.

他的双手有节律地叩击着方向盘。\
He taps his fingers rhythmically on the steering wheel.

**司机**：姑娘们，不管你们是什么心血来潮的探险小队，还是确有要务在身。我得提醒你们……那个镇子最近一直在发生怪事。\
**Driver**: Girls, I don't know why y'all are here. But whether it's just for a bit of adventure or for business, I gotta tell you. Something ain't right in that town.

**司机**：像什么车顶上的摩擦声、“钩子”，或者卡在散热格栅上的动物尸体，甚至于身披黑袍的异教徒……这儿的异常已经够多了。\
**Driver**: We've all heard the stories—scratching sounds on car roofs, animal bits stuck to car grilles, and those people in black robes running around. It's all too weird for me.

**红弩箭**：得了吧，那只是一些怪谈故事！\
**Lilya**: Ah, give the ghost stories a rest.

**红弩箭**：你想谈价格，完全能用一个更聪明的方式来谈——而不是拿这些家喻户晓的故事来吓唬人，这太拙劣了。\
**Lilya**: Look, if you're trying to negotiate a higher price, at least be a little smart about it instead of trying to spook us with a few tall tales.

**司机**：……你没理解我的意思，如果不是情势所迫，谁会放弃到手的美钞？\
**Driver**: You got me all wrong. Who in their right mind would throw away the cash in their hand unless they were forced to?

**司机**：富兰克林的头像远没有命重要——给再多的钱也不干。\
**Driver**: Benjamins are good and all, but they ain't worth my life. Ain't no way I'm taking you there, no matter how much cash you throw at me.

**红弩箭**：你就是故事里的那个司机？\
**Lilya**: Why? Were you the driver in that ghost story?

**司机**：……不是。\
**Driver**: N-No.

**红弩箭**：还是说，你亲眼看到了全程？\
**Lilya**: Have you seen these things happen yourself?

**司机**：……\
**Driver**: ...

**红弩箭**：只是绕个弯而已！又费不了多少油。\
**Lilya**: Come on, it's just a little detour! It won't even cost you much fuel!

**司机**：……\
**Driver**: ...

男人的双手紧握着方向盘，指节因用力而泛白。\
He clenches his hands tightly around the steering wheel, his knuckles turning white from the pressure.

**维尔汀**：……先生？\
**Vertin**: Sir?

**司机**：你们看见了吗？这儿……起雾了。\
**Driver**: You see that? It's fogging up.

四周洋溢着白色的雾气，浓稠得如同乳汁。\
Thick, milky fog envelopes the car.

车子在道路旁边停了下来。\
The driver pulls over.

**司机**：这不是天然形成的雾气，我们不能再前进了，必须要停下来……\
**Driver**: Ain't no way this fog is natural. We shouldn't go any further. I'm stopping right here.

**红弩箭**：咱们换个位置。\
**Lilya**: Ugh, fine, I'll drive. Swap seats with me.

**司机**：不……绝不能在现在下车……\
**Driver**: No. Nobody get out of the car.

**红弩箭**：为什么？\
**Lilya**: Why?

**司机**：……该死的！难道你们从来没听过这儿的传说吗？那你们为什么要到这儿来找乐子？\
**Driver**: Are you kidding me?! You haven't heard the stories, have you? Then what in the hell are you even doing here?!

**司机**：当雾气在77号公路翻涌时，一旦下车，就会发生异常的事件……有人说，雾气里有白色的巨型鳄鱼；有人说，远方的树上吊满了尸体。\
**Driver**: When the fog rolls in on Route 77, you should always stay in the car. All kinds of terrible things hide in the fog. Some folks say they saw giant white crocodiles; others say they saw dead bodies hanging from trees.

**司机**：无论如何，我们应该在车里呆着……直到雾气消失。\
**Driver**: Ain't nobody leaving this car. Not until the fog's gone.

哧啦——哧啦——\
*screech*

车顶上的摩擦声让他立刻中止了述说。\
He's interrupted by a drawn-out scraping sound on the roof of the car.

**司机**：……！\
**Driver**: ...!

**司机**：等等，这就是、这就是——\
**Driver**: Is that ... Is that ...?

**红弩箭**：嘿！别告诉我你被这些玩意吓破了胆——\
**Lilya**: Oh, come on! Don't tell me you're scared of this stuff!

没有人回答她。\
No response.

**维尔汀**：……他晕过去了。\
**Vertin**: He's fainted.

狭窄而又安静的车内，诡异的气氛正在蔓延——不过，相较于不久前的绿湖营地来说，这算不了什么。\
A strange atmosphere spreads inside the car as they sit and listen to the scraping on the roof. But this is nothing compared to what happened at Green Lake Campsite.

车顶上的摩擦声消失了，几个黑白相间的小身影在道路外一闪而过。\
Finally, the scraping stops, and a few black-and-white figures dart past the windows.

**维尔汀**：原来是这样……你看，那个是穆姆[Mummu]，一种在美国南部极为常见的魔精。它们在受到惊吓时，会从头部的呼吸角产生一种形似于雾的气体。\
**Vertin**: I see. This looks like the work of a Mummus. It's a critter commonly seen in the southern US. When they're frightened, they produce a fog-like gas from their respiratory trumpet.

**红弩箭**：……只是一些魔精在车顶上瘙痒而已。\
**Lilya**: So that sound is just some critter scratching along on the roof.

飞行员不满地抱怨着，旋即打开了车门。\
Lilya opens the door.

**红弩箭**：照这样下去，一个月都到不了目的地。\
**Lilya**: At this rate, I won't get my Red 38 back for another month!

**红弩箭**：我老早就想试试——我们得先把这个家伙挪走！头儿，你得从副驾驶上下来了。\
**Lilya**: Well, I've always wanted to try this. Help me move this guy! And you'll have to give up your passenger seat, Captain.

**维尔汀**：我明白你想做什么……但是，你有美国驾照，或者国际驾照吗？\
**Vertin**: I know what you're thinking. But do you have a US driver's license? Or any driver's license at all, for that matter?

**红弩箭**：为什么开车一定要有驾照？我会驾驶飞行载具，还能用它们玩特技，这不比开车难多了？\
**Lilya**: What do I need that for? I can fly a broom and even do all those maneuvers. That takes more skill than driving a car, don't you think?

**红弩箭**：哈，驾驶汽车只会比驾驶飞机更简单——你可以从飞行员和司机的数量对比上推知这一点。\
**Lilya**: Ha, compared to flying, driving a car is child's play. Just look at the number of drivers compared to pilots in the world.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

按照飞行员的规划，位置得到了调整。\
Following the pilot's plan, they adjust positions.

**红弩箭**：首先……\
**Lilya**: Now, where do we start?

她望着眼前的仪表盘与操纵杆。\
She glances at the dashboard in front of her.

这和Su-01ве内部结构不尽相似——没关系，小问题。\
This doesn't look like the interior of an Su-01ве. A minor issue.

飞行员开始回忆。\
She thinks back to her training.

**红弩箭**：开启双侧发动机，转速表稳定到70%。\
**Lilya**: Start both engines. Keep the tachometer at 70%.

**红弩箭**：前机轮转向锁、杆位指示器，推杆……噢，襟翼……\
**Lilya**: Here's the nose wheel steering, the position indicator for the joystick, the throttle lever ... ah, and these are for the flaps.

**红弩箭**：不对——这是汽车！该死的！\
**Lilya**: No, no! That's not right! We're in a car, not a flying machine!

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

“咔哒”。\
*click*

后座的乘客沉默地系上了安全带。\
The rear-seat passenger quietly fastens her seatbelt.

**红弩箭**：下车吧，头儿，我得承认我搞不定这铁家伙。\
**Lilya**: Let's just get out, Captain. Can't wrap my head around this hunk of metal.

**维尔汀**：我非常赞同你的决定。\
**Vertin**: Good decision.

**红弩箭**：既然这些雾气的源头是魔精，那也很简单，把它们驱逐出这儿就行了。\
**Lilya**: If these critters are responsible for this fog, our solution is simple. We drive them away.

**红弩箭**：走吧。\
**Lilya**: Let's go.

她伸手打开了车门，外部浓稠的雾气如潮水般扑入车内。\
She opens the door, and the thick fog outside rushes in like a tide.

## THH-03 婴儿电台 / Baby Broadcaster

年轻的乘客们下了车，踩在了沥青的马路上。\
They get out of the car and step onto the asphalt road.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

一丝微不可察的潮湿。乳白色的空气四处蔓延，充塞了鼻腔与耳道。\
A barely perceptible moisture fills the air. The mist is pervasive, even filling their ears and nostrils.

若有似无的风黏在脸上，如同蜘蛛摇曳的丝网。\
A faint breeze runs along their faces, like a spider's web blowing in the wind.

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

一点转瞬即逝的灵光，自遥不可及的远处延伸而来。\
A flash of insight comes to her from some distant, unreachable place.

**红弩箭**：怎么了，头儿？\
**Lilya**: What is it, Captain?

**维尔汀**：有人在使用神秘术。\
**Vertin**: Someone's casting arcane skills nearby.

**？？？**：哇……\
**???**: *baby cries*

婴儿的哭啼宛如虫蚁的咬噬，在耳道的深处隐隐作痛。\
The crying of a baby throbs faintly in her ears like an insect bite.

**维尔汀**：你听到婴儿的哭声了吗？\
**Vertin**: Do you hear that? Sounds like a crying baby.

**红弩箭**：走，去看看。\
**Lilya**: Better go take a look.

静谧的旷野中，响起了急促的草叶摩擦声，仿佛有什么东西正在不远处快速地通行。\
The grass is rustling, as if something is moving nearby.

**红弩箭**：出身于德克萨斯的士兵和我说过，在很多年前，他的故乡出现过一个臭名昭著的抢劫犯。\
**Lilya**: You know, a Texan soldier once told me about a notorious bandit back in his hometown many years ago.

**红弩箭**：他用磁带录下婴儿的声音，在单身母亲的门前播放。一旦有人因为怜悯而开门，立刻会招致不必要的灾祸。\
**Lilya**: He would record the sound of a crying baby and play it outside the homes of single mothers. Then he'd wait, ready to attack them if any of them opened their door to look for the baby.

**维尔汀**：不能因为这个事件而否定所有的求援。\
**Vertin**: Yes, but the actions of one man don't negate all other calls for help.

**红弩箭**：当然，我只是提醒——声源近在眼前，做好战斗的准备。\
**Lilya**: Of course not. It's just a reminder to be ready for anything. We're close now. Prepare yourself.

**维尔汀**：好，我明白。\
**Vertin**: Got it.

草叶飘摇，细弱的哭声戛然而止，随之而来的是骤然加重的雾气。\
The grass sways, and the faint crying stops. The fog grows thicker.

**红弩箭**：不好——！\
**Lilya**: Vertin, over here!

一个破损的手电筒卧在泥土上，伤痕崭新。\
A broken flashlight lies on the ground. The damage looks recent.

不远处是一片灰蓝色的衣角和半截脚踝，其上沾满了新鲜而潮湿的泥土。\
Not far away, they spot a foot in a black shoe, and a pale ankle disappearing under purple fabric.

**侍应生**：噢……孩子们，帮帮我……\
**Maid**: Ah. Hello. Please help.

瘦弱的女性紧紧地怀抱着一个襁褓，身体蜷成一小团，因受惊而轻颤着。\
A frail woman tightly cradles a swaddled infant, her body curled up and trembling with fear.

**维尔汀**：小姐，有什么可以帮助您的吗？\
**Vertin**: Are you alright, Miss?

随着呼唤声，侍应生转过了头，面容苍白，毫无血色。\
The maid turns her head. Her face is pale, as if all the blood has been drained from it.

**侍应生**：终于有人来了……\
**Maid**: Finally, someone ...

**侍应生**：您能帮帮我吗……？这些魔精堵塞了道路，它们不肯让我离开……但凡我想挤出一条路，它们都会跳起来，狠狠撞在我的身上……\
**Maid**: Please, help me. These critters won't let me leave. Every time I try, they knock me back.

**侍应生**：你看，连孩子的肚子都饿了，止不住地哭。要不是你们，我真不知道该怎么办才好……\
**Maid**: My baby's starving and crying. If you hadn't come, I really don't know what I would've done.

**穆姆**：咕呜，咕呜——呜，呜……\
**Mummus**: Cooumm, cooumm ... Urhm, urhm ...

黑白相间的魔精发出了警惕的叫声。\
The critter makes a wary sound.

**维尔汀**：穆姆……？我没有看见过以它为主角的袭击报告，这应该是一种温驯而胆小的魔精……\
**Vertin**: You mean these Mummus? I've never read about them attacking anyone in any reports. In fact, they're known for being rather timid.

**红弩箭**：头儿，报告并不能说明一切。\
**Lilya**: Reports don't necessarily capture the whole story, Captain.

**红弩箭**：你看看这些家伙，它们的眼里可没写着“温驯”两个字。\
**Lilya**: Look at them. They don't seem very "timid" to me.

**穆姆**：咕——\
**Mummus**: Coo ...

眼前的穆姆骤然地张大了嘴，露出口中白森森的牙齿。\
The Mummus before them opens its mouth wide, revealing its sharp white teeth.

**红弩箭**：小心！它要进攻了！\
**Lilya**: Careful! It's going to attack!

喧闹的家伙们四散着逃离了现场，草叶晃动，发出沙沙的响声。\
The creatures scatter, the grass rustling as they flee.

**侍应生**：……噢，它们每次走得都是这样的快。\
**Maid**: Ah. They always run off so quickly.

侍应生打扮的女性慢慢地从泥地里站起了身，拍去了衣角的尘土。\
The woman pulls herself up off the ground and brushes the dirt from her skirt.

**维尔汀**：您还好吗？\
**Vertin**: Are you alright?

**侍应生**：您也看到了，对吗？那种滑溜溜的小生物……和海豹长得太相似了。\
**Maid**: Did you get a good look at them? Those slippery little things look like seals, don't they?

**侍应生**：它们总是喜欢踩着汽车的顶部，用扁平而宽大的后肢摩擦车顶，发出刺耳的刮擦声——\
**Maid**: They always jump on passing cars and rub their flat hind legs on the roof, making that coarse scraping sound.

**侍应生**：多惊人呀，它们也懂得恐惧的好处呢。\
**Maid**: Amazing creatures, aren't they? These little fearmongers.

风吹过原野，雾气渐消，她的面孔潮红，身形随之微微晃动着。\
Wind sweeps across the plains, dispersing the fog. The woman's face flushes red as she sways lightly in the breeze.

**侍应生**：可惜，它们胆子太小，一有动静就要害怕……所以，这儿的雾气从来没有散过，客人也总找不到路。\
**Maid**: But they are, in fact, easily frightened; the slightest movement could startle them. That's why it's foggy all year around here. Many of my guests have trouble finding their way to the motel.

**侍应生**：……姑娘们，你们是旅店的客人吗？\
**Maid**: Are you ladies looking to check in at the motel?

**红弩箭**：旅店？\
**Lilya**: Motel?

**侍应生**：那是一个叫“蓝手帕旅馆”的地方，如果您正感到疲累，去那儿就能好好地睡上一觉……\
**Maid**: Yes, Tuesday's Motel. If you're looking for a comfortable bed for the night, it's the place to go.

**侍应生**：总之，姑娘们，我得好好谢谢你们……\
**Maid**: Anyway, thank you so much for saving us. I owe you one.

她拍了拍怀中的襁褓。\
She pats the swaddled baby.

**维尔汀**：……您是旅馆的侍应生吗？\
**Vertin**: Excuse me, are you the maid at Tuesday's Motel?

**蓝手帕**：噢……险些忘了介绍自己，您也可以叫我蓝手帕——人们常常这么叫我，多亲切的名字。\
**Tuesday**: Ah, I almost forgot to introduce myself. Folks around here call me Tuesday.

**蓝手帕**：嘿，蓝手帕，到这儿来。嘿，蓝手帕，送一份早餐……蓝手帕，蓝手帕，名字就像是一根缰绳，拴在每个人的脖颈儿上。\
**Tuesday**: "Hey, Tuesday, over here. Hey, Tuesday! Breakfast for one, please. Tuesday, Tuesday ..." Ain't we all like horses, and our names like the reins pulling at us?

她打量着两位风尘仆仆的客人。\
She looks the two of them over.

**蓝手帕**：你们需要暂时地歇歇脚吗？姑娘们。\
**Tuesday**: Do you need a place to stay, ladies?

**维尔汀**：……谢谢你的好意。\
**Vertin**: Thank you for your kindness.

**维尔汀**：——我们的司机还在车内，我们不能把他一个人丢在那儿。\
**Vertin**: But our driver's still in the car. We can't just leave him there.

**红弩箭**：证件和行李也都在车里，还有所有的现金——既然雾已经散了，那就赶紧走吧。\
**Lilya**: And our luggage and travel documents are still in the trunk, along with our cash, too. Let's head back now that the fog has cleared.

**蓝手帕**：需要我为你们引路吗？\
**Tuesday**: Shall I lead the way?

**红弩箭**：你？\
**Lilya**: You?

飞行员怀疑地打量着眼前的侍应生。\
She looks the maid up and down suspiciously.

**红弩箭**：你不用做别的事吗？\
**Lilya**: What were you doing out here alone, anyway?

**蓝手帕**：……\
**Tuesday**: ...

**蓝手帕**：我……在这儿等了两个小时了，预定的客人却迟迟未来。\
**Tuesday**: I-I was waiting for a guest. It's been two hours, and they still haven't shown up.

**蓝手帕**：我想，与其在这儿继续等候……不如做一些力所能及的好事。\
**Tuesday**: I thought, rather than waiting here, I would pay you back for helping me.

**蓝手帕**：姑娘们，你们的车是停靠在77号公路的附近吗？让我带你们过去吧。\
**Tuesday**: I assume you parked near Route 77? Let me take you there.

西垂的太阳散发着热力，红土地上的山茱萸与棉桃杂糅地生长于一处。\
The setting sun scatters its light, illuminating the dogwood and cotton plants in the fields.

**红弩箭**：……这胆小的家伙。\
**Lilya**: That coward!

公路边空荡荡的——先前停靠的车辆已不知所踪，路边只留下了少量的行李。\
The car is gone. Nothing remains but a few scattered pieces of luggage.

**红弩箭**：——他把我们的行李丢了下来，自己逃得连影子都不见。\
**Lilya**: He just threw out our luggage and took off! Tsk, how pathetic.

**维尔汀**：……往好处想，至少他没有侵吞我们的财产。\
**Vertin**: At least he didn't take the luggage with him.

**蓝手帕**：嗯……所以，您要拎着这些行李，在公路上等下一辆顺风车吗……？\
**Tuesday**: Mmm. Are you going to thumb a ride with all these bags?

**蓝手帕**：我不会建议你们这么做，尤其是在这儿——您至少应该看过一些公路片，对吗？那就应该知道公路并不是一个安全的地方。\
**Tuesday**: I'd advise against that, especially here. You've seen those movies, right? Bad things can happen on the road out here.

**蓝手帕**：除此以外，还有许多偷渡客来到了这里……\
**Tuesday**: There are a lot of smugglers around these days.

她声音中的担忧显而易见。\
There's a clear concern in her voice.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：您的旅馆就在附近，对吗？\
**Vertin**: Did you say your motel wasn't far from here?

**蓝手帕**：当然，请往这儿走——这里有一条易于行走的小径，别让泥土沾上了你们的鞋子。\
**Tuesday**: Yes. Come this way. There's an easy trail that won't dirty your shoes.

**蓝手帕**：不用担心，路途并不遥远。\
**Tuesday**: Don't worry. It ain't far.

步行的时间并不算长。脚腕还未察觉到疲累，就已经看见了不远处的汽车旅馆。\
The walk isn't far, indeed. Before long, they're standing in front of the motel.

**蓝手帕**：等到天色暗去，悬置的灯牌将会被点亮，每一个迷途的旅人都能得到柔软的床榻。\
**Tuesday**: When night falls and the signs are lit, a weary traveler may find a comfortable place to rest here.

楝树的掩映下，木制门廊于黄昏中静候着它的主人。\
Under the shade of the neem trees, the wooden porch awaits its owner, darkening in the fading sunlight.

**蓝手帕**：孩子们，欢迎来到蓝手帕旅馆。\
**Tuesday**: Welcome to Tuesday's Motel, ladies.

## THH-04 红勋章 / Medal of Honor

旅馆前台，侍应生正为客人们办理入住手续。\
The maid stands behind the front desk in the motel lobby. She's checking in her new guests.

**蓝手帕**：您的房费共计25美金……信用卡还是现金？\
**Tuesday**: That'll be 25 dollars altogether. Will that be on card or cash?

**维尔汀**：现金。\
**Vertin**: Cash, please.

侍应生拿起护照比对着上方的信息。\
The maid holds up the passport, comparing the information on it.

**红弩箭**：嘿，侍应生，附近的小镇上是不是有一个军备工厂？\
**Lilya**: Hey, do you know if there's an armament factory in the town nearby?

**蓝手帕**：军备工厂？\
**Tuesday**: An armament factory?

她打量着红弩箭的装扮，微笑着作出了回应。\
She studies Lilya's outfit and smiles as she responds.

**蓝手帕**：是的，就在附近……我想，也许您需要一份地图。\
**Tuesday**: Yes, there is one. Would you like a map?

她打开抽屉，摸出了一份地图，交至了飞行员的手中。\
She opens a drawer, pulls out a map, and hands it to her.

**蓝手帕**：如果您要去，请务必早些回来，夜里的路会很难走。\
**Tuesday**: If you plan on visiting, make sure to return early. It can be a difficult walk in the dark.

飞行员很快在地图上找到了那个被命名为“奇索斯”的镇子。\
Lilya quickly finds the town labeled "Chisos" on the map.

**红弩箭**：看起来不远。\
**Lilya**: Doesn't seem far from here.

**蓝手帕**：这儿离镇子有将近一小时的步行路程，我会建议您等到明天早晨再出发。\
**Tuesday**: It's about an hour's walk. I'd recommend leaving tomorrow morning.

**蓝手帕**：天已经快黑了，而走夜路总归不是一件好事。\
**Tuesday**: It's getting late. It's best not to be outside at night.

**红弩箭**：多谢你的好心提醒……不过，我现在就得走了。\
**Lilya**: Thanks, but I'm going right now.

飞行员一扫平日的懒散，展现出了绝佳的行动力。\
She moves with swift purpose to the front door.

**红弩箭**：只要红色38在我的身边，所有的事情都会顺利起来！\
**Lilya**: Nothing can go wrong as long as I have the Red 38 by my side.

**维尔汀**：如果有意外，及时联系我。\
**Vertin**: Call me if anything happens.

**红弩箭**：意外？哈，我会把罪魁祸首的头拧下来。\
**Lilya**: Like what? I can handle myself.

平地刮起了一阵骤风，飞行员冲出了旅馆的大门。\
A rush of wind enters as Lilya opens the door and makes her way out of the motel.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：我想，她应该会在稍晚些时候再入住。\
**Vertin**: Don't worry. She'll check in later.

**蓝手帕**：这是您的护照，请收好。\
**Tuesday**: Here's your passport.

**维尔汀**：您一直在这儿当侍应生吗？\
**Vertin**: Have you been working here since the opening of this place?

**蓝手帕**：嗯。\
**Tuesday**: Yes.

**维尔汀**：这儿的生意好吗？\
**Vertin**: How's business?

侍应生轻轻地笑了。\
The maid laughs softly.

**蓝手帕**：现在正是淡季，生意并不怎么好。\
**Tuesday**: Not too great. It's the off-season now.

**蓝手帕**：您不怎么擅长寒暄，是有什么想问的吗？\
**Tuesday**: You don't seem too good at small talk. Is there anything you'd like to ask?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：实际上，我想询问您一个问题。\
**Vertin**: I do have one question.

**维尔汀**：您见过一位羊首人身的神秘学家吗？\
**Vertin**: Have you seen a sheep-headed arcanist around?

她展示了基金会给予的资料。\
She shows the information provided by the Foundation.

**蓝手帕**：噢……很有趣。我想，任何人见过这位小家伙，都会印象深刻的。\
**Tuesday**: Ah, that's not a face you'd easily forget.

**蓝手帕**：您是为什么要找她呢？\
**Tuesday**: And why are you looking for this arcanist?

**蓝手帕**：世界和平……？\
**Tuesday**: World peace?

侍应生略带惊讶地眨巴着眼睛，随后笑出了声。\
The maid blinks in surprise, then laughs.

**蓝手帕**：嗯……这是一个难以拒绝、可爱的理由。\
**Tuesday**: Well, that makes this request simply too adorable to turn down.

**蓝手帕**：《UTTU》……这个名字很亲切，我想我应该在哪里听过。\
**Tuesday**: UTTU ... I think I've heard of that before.

**蓝手帕**：是那本针对神秘学家发行的杂志，对吗？\
**Tuesday**: That's a magazine specially made for arcanists, right?

**蓝手帕**：不过，实在很可惜……我没有见过她。\
**Tuesday**: Well, I'm sorry to say that I've never met an arcanist with the head of a sheep.

**蓝手帕**：如果您需要的话，我可以帮您问问附近的农户……\
**Tuesday**: I can help you ask around if you—

她正要说得更多，天花板却开始颤动，扑簌簌地抖下灰尘。\
Suddenly, the ceiling starts to tremble.

神秘术的涌动从头顶上传来。\
A surge of arcane energy comes from above.

**维尔汀**：这是……\
**Vertin**: What's ...

**蓝手帕**：抱歉，我想是有了一些突发的状况。\
**Tuesday**: Sounds like something's gone wrong upstairs. Sorry about that.

**蓝手帕**：您的房间也在二楼，我先带您过去吧。或许可以一起看看楼上到底发生了什么。\
**Tuesday**: Let's head up. Your room's on the second floor, too. Then we can take a look at what's happened.

**维尔汀**：好。\
**Vertin**: Sounds good.

**蓝手帕**：不过，楼上的客人……\
**Tuesday**: Just so you know, the guests upstairs are a little ...

侍应生欲言又止。\
The maid hesitates.

**蓝手帕**：总之，如果您感到害怕，可以躲在我的身后。\
**Tuesday**: Well, you can stay behind me if you like.

**阿尔古斯**：这个提议怎么样？\
**Argus**: How about it?

走廊的远处传来了交谈的声音。\
A voice echoes from down the hall.

**阿尔古斯**：只是交换房间而已，更何况您还是这样一位慷慨的小姐。\
**Argus**: It's just a simple room swap. I'm sure it won't be no trouble at all for a generous lady such as yourself.

**蓝手帕**：那位是210房间的客人，她是在前天夜里到这儿的。\
**Tuesday**: That's the guest staying in room 210. She arrived here the night before yesterday.

**蓝手帕**：她刚来到这儿的时候受了伤，没想到现在就恢复得差不多了。\
**Tuesday**: She was injured when she came in. Seems it didn't take her long to recover.

**蓝手帕**：噢，但我不知道为什么……她一直执着于与别人交换房间——如果您感到无法应付，请及时给前台打电话，我总会为您提供帮助的……\
**Tuesday**: But I don't quite understand why she insists on swapping rooms with the other guests. If she does the same to you, please call the front desk. I'll do my best to help.

**维尔汀**：也许她比我更需要帮助——你不去问问她为什么要做这些事吗？\
**Vertin**: Why don't you offer her your help? She needs it more than I do.

**蓝手帕**：噢……您果然还是一个孩子。\
**Tuesday**: Oh, things don't work like that here, Miss.

**蓝手帕**：每个人都有自己的秘密，更何况这儿是汽车旅馆。如果人闭不上自己的嘴巴，自然会有别人替他闭上。\
**Tuesday**: Everyone has their own secrets. With the variety of guests we get, it's best to keep your mouth shut, or else somebody will shut it for you.

**蓝手帕**：虽然现在已经不是赏金猎人横行的时代了……但需要提醒您的是，如果不想以身涉险，最好能够保持安静……\
**Tuesday**: Although there are fewer bounty hunters around these days, my advice is to stay quiet if you don't want any trouble.

**蓝手帕**：尤其是面对一位带着猎枪的雇佣兵……噢，您应该知道这在德州意味着什么，对吧？\
**Tuesday**: Especially if you're dealing with an armed mercenary. You know how things like that play out down here in Texas, don't you?

**维尔汀**：……我明白。\
**Vertin**: Understood.

不远处的对话还在继续。\
The voice down the hall continues.

**阿尔古斯**：还是说，你有什么别的条件？\
**Argus**: Or do you have something else in mind?

**女房客**：你的房间会更大、更好吗？\
**Female Guest**: Is your room bigger and better than this one?

一个更雀跃的声音出现了。\
A more lively voice chimes in.

**蓝手帕**：这位是218房间的客人——另一位年轻的小姐。\
**Tuesday**: That's the guest of room 218 speaking. She too is a young lady like you.

**维尔汀**：你能记住所有人的房间号？\
**Vertin**: You remember all the guests and their room numbers?

**蓝手帕**：如果有一位客人在您的旅馆里住了一个月，我相信您也能记住她的名字——这位金伯利女郎就是这样的状况。\
**Tuesday**: You'd remember her too if she'd been staying in your motel for a month. Ms. Kimberly's been here for just over that.

**史蒂文**：我……\
**Stefen**: I ...

**蓝手帕**：……咦？\
**Tuesday**: Hm?

侍应生发出了诧异的声音，快步地走向了声音的发源地。\
The maid quickly moves toward the source of the voice.

眼前的男人面孔憔悴，他的脊背略弓着，眼睛泛黄且浑浊。\
The man before her looks haggard, his back slightly hunched, his eyes yellowed and cloudy.

**史蒂文**：镜子……镜子……\
**Stefen**: Mirror ... The mirror ...

**蓝手帕**：史蒂文先生，您……怎么出来了？\
**Tuesday**: Mr. Stefen, are you coming out for some fresh air?

走廊中的人齐齐地望向了他们。\
Everyone in the hallway turns to look at the maid.

**阿尔古斯**：侍应生？你来得正好。\
**Argus**: Maid! You're just in time.

**阿尔古斯**：我想和这位……嗯，金伯利女郎换一个房间。\
**Argus**: I'd like to swap rooms with this Kimberly lady.

**蓝手帕**：噢，如果你们达成了一致，我当然没有反对的理由……\
**Tuesday**: If Ms. Kimberly and yourself have come to an agreement, then I see no reason why you can't do so.

**史蒂文**：啊……\
**Stefen**: Ah.

男人沉默已久的喉咙发出了干涩的声音，他的声带不自然地震颤着，如同初次学语的婴儿。\
The man makes a dry, rasping sound, his vocal cords trembling unnaturally. It's like he's speaking for the first time in his life.

**史蒂文**：司辰？\
**Stefen**: Timekeeper?

**维尔汀**：……您是？\
**Vertin**: Have we met?

这个回答似乎点燃了男人某根异常的神经，他的表情在一瞬间变得扭曲。\
This response seems to trigger something. His expression twists.

**史蒂文**：维尔汀……？\
**Stefen**: Vertin?

**维尔汀**：是我，先生……？\
**Vertin**: That's me. Do I know you, sir?

**史蒂文**：我看到过你……在那份报纸上……\
**Stefen**: I saw you—in the newspaper.

**史蒂文**：哦……报纸，那颗爆炸的真空弹——您看见了吗？您一定看见了，因为那正是你一手促成的！你们扔下了那颗炸弹，是毋庸置疑的刽子手……\
**Stefen**: Arh, the newspaper, that vacuum bomb—did you see the explosion? You must have, because you made it happen! You dropped the bomb! You murderers!

**史蒂文**：但是你们因此受到审判了吗……？完全没有！你们甚至因为这个而收到了表彰，所有人都在那一刻为您发来贺电……\
**Stefen**: But have any of you been brought to justice? No, not a single one! Instead, you were congratulated and given medals.

**史蒂文**：这个颠倒的世界啊……我想问，人怎么能够因为杀人而被表彰呢？\
**Stefen**: Revolting! Disgusting! Why were you rewarded for murder?!

他神经质地呢喃着。\
He blabbers on, working himself into a frenzy.

**史蒂文**：而我就要待在这个小小的旅馆里……主啊，难道我的人生仅止于此吗？\
**Stefen**: Meanwhile, I'm stuck in this hotel. Lord, is this what my life has come to?

**维尔汀**：可是我从来没有见过你，先生。在这之前我甚至不知道您的名字。\
**Vertin**: But we've never met before. I don't even know your name, sir.

**史蒂文**：你当然不会见过我……因为我将会把你们的罪行公之于众……\
**Stefen**: Of course you don't know me. But I'll get the truth out. I'll expose your crimes to the public!

近似疯癫的男人喋喋不休地说着，他的指关节因用力而泛出白色。\
The man's deranged rant continues, his knuckles turning white as he clenches his fists.

**史蒂文**：浴缸里腐烂的女人，羊头人身的怪物……还有镜子里的……\
**Stefen**: That rotting woman in the tub, that sheep-headed monster, and that one inside the mirror.

**维尔汀**：羊头人身……？\
**Vertin**: Sheep-headed, you say?

**维尔汀**：等等，先生——\
**Vertin**: Wait! Sir—

**阿尔古斯**：嘘，他已经疯了。\
**Argus**: Shh. Don't startle him. He's totally crazy.

**史蒂文**：我早该知道一切都是假的！\
**Stefen**: I should've known it was all fake!

**史蒂文**：如果杀人就能获得勋章……\
**Stefen**: If they're giving out medals for killing people ...

**史蒂文**：哦……我也应该拥有那一枚亮闪闪的勋章啊——那本来就是我的！\
**Stefen**: Ah, then I should have one, too. That shiny medal—it should be mine!

他紧咬着嘴唇，那双浑浊的眼睛如同钩子，直愣愣地望向前方。\
He bites down hard on his lip, his cloudy eyes staring straight ahead.

男人试探性地向前踏出了一步。\
He steps forward.

**阿尔古斯**：退后！\
**Argus**: Stay back!

未等雇佣兵的话音落下，那精瘦的男人赫然扑向了众人。\
But the man has already lunged at them.

失去理智的男人被一枪托打晕在了地上。\
A single blow from the butt of the mercenary's shotgun knocks the man out.

**蓝手帕**：……\
**Tuesday**: ...

侍应生急促地呼吸着，她的面孔微微发热。\
The maid breathes heavily, her face slightly flushed.

**蓝手帕**：抱歉……维尔汀小姐。\
**Tuesday**: I'm ever so sorry about all this, Ms. Vertin.

**蓝手帕**：您刚来不久，就让您卷入了这么大的麻烦……\
**Tuesday**: You've only just arrived, and you've had to deal with so much trouble already.

**维尔汀**：我不认为这是麻烦……甚至我需要感谢您。\
**Vertin**: Oh, it's no trouble. In fact, I'm glad that we came here.

**维尔汀**：他说，他见过一个“羊头人身的怪物”……\
**Vertin**: That man said he'd seen a "sheep-headed monster."

**蓝手帕**：……噢，但我不得不提醒您一句，您真的要相信一个癔病患者的话语吗？\
**Tuesday**: Oh, that ... He's quite delusional. Surely you won't take the ramblings of a madman for a fact, will you?

**蓝手帕**：自他入住旅馆的那一天起，就出现了诸如漫游、痉挛、抽搐的症状……\
**Tuesday**: He's been peculiar since the day he checked in. He spasms and twitches and pays little attention to his surroundings.

**蓝手帕**：我并不建议您与他见面或交谈……因为谁也不知道他下一刻会爆发出什么样的行动。\
**Tuesday**: It's best not to have a face-to-face conversation with him. Who knows what he'll do next.

**金伯利女郎**：嘿，侍应生，别光顾着聊天了！你得处理你的工作。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Hey, you, maid! Enough chatter. You have a job to do.

一边的女郎迫不及待地打断了对话。\
The girl impatiently interrupts their conversation.

**金伯利女郎**：我与这位，呃……阿尔古斯小姐，要交换房间。你知道该怎么做，对吗？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I've accepted the offer this, uh, Ms. Argus made. What's next? What should we do?

**蓝手帕**：……抱歉，金伯利女郎。\
**Tuesday**: Apologies, Ms. Kimberly. I'll be with you in a moment.

**蓝手帕**：不过，在此之前，请二位移步至前台吧……再漂亮的房间，也要收拾之后才能住人。您需要稍等一会儿，在此期间，您可以在前台的椅子上休憩。\
**Tuesday**: Could the both of you wait for me at the front desk? The rooms need a tidy-up before they can be occupied. You may take a rest on the couch in the lobby while you wait.

**蓝手帕**：至于这位维尔汀小姐……非常抱歉，您能够独自前往您的房间吗？\
**Tuesday**: Ms. Vertin, I'm afraid I'll have to leave you here. Do you mind going to your room alone?

**维尔汀**：好。\
**Vertin**: Not at all.

手提箱随着步履的节奏而微微晃动着，将人们抛在身后。\
The suitcase sways with her steps as she heads to her room.

空气中再次传来了神秘术的涌动，令人不自觉地回头望去。\
Once again, the air pulses with the flow of arcane energy, compelling her to look back.

**阿尔古斯**：不——我不需要，侍应生。不如说，你对房间的清理只会干扰我的工作。\
**Argus**: Ma'am, you can just leave the room as it is. If you clean it, it'll interfere with my work.

**阿尔古斯**：去照看那位金伯利女郎吧……她看起来饿得厉害，连身体都在打颤。\
**Argus**: You might wanna check on that Kimberly lady. She looks starved. She wouldn't stop shaking.

雇佣兵的眼中绽放了一簇蓝绿色的光芒，辉光四散，如同鸟类正在舒展它们绚丽的尾羽。\
A cluster of emerald light sparks in the mercenary's left eye, scattering like a bird unfurling its brilliant tail feathers.

**蓝手帕**：噢……金伯利女郎，您需要送餐服务吗？\
**Tuesday**: Oh, Ms. Kimberly. Would you like something to eat?

**金伯利女郎**：不需要！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I'm fine!

女房客的脸色肉眼可见地变得不友善。\
The guest's face visibly sours.

**金伯利女郎**：我同意了你的要求——你怎么还能这样嘲讽我？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I agreed to change rooms, didn't I? Why are you two still mocking me?

女郎如同一只被触发了防御机制的刺猬，恼火地望向了雇佣兵。\
She turns her attention to the mercenary.

**金伯利女郎**：你是一个彻头彻尾的讨厌鬼！我讨厌和你做交易。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: You're not exactly a pleasant person to do business with; you know that, right?

**阿尔古斯**：哦，我不知道我在哪里冒犯了你。\
**Argus**: Well, darn, what got you so riled up?

**阿尔古斯**：但已经晚了，就好像在合同上签下字以后，一切条款都会开始生效——您当然也可以反悔。但你最好不要在德克萨斯招惹一个带枪的人，这是不明智的。\
**Argus**: It's too late now. A deal's a deal. You can backpedal if you like, but it ain't wise to mess with a girl packing heat down here in Texas.

**阿尔古斯**：再见了，金伯利女郎。\
**Argus**: Later, Ms. Kimberly.

雇佣兵的眼中辉光流溢。随后她拧开了门锁，进入了那个她渴望已久的房间。\
The mercenary's eye gleams as she turns the lock and enters her hard-won room.

**维尔汀**：——是她在使用神秘术。\
**Vertin**: Her arcane skill.

## THH-05 临时通讯 / A Sudden Message

吱嘎——

年久失修的房门被推开，空气中散发着地板蜡的清香。\
The door creaks as she opens it, and her nostrils are hit with the distinct scent of floor wax.

摁下开关，在短暂的电流声后，房间里的灯亮了起来。\
She flips the switch, and after a brief hum of electricity, the room lights up.

**维尔汀**：这个名叫史蒂文的住客，他很显然知道些什么。但……他的癔病看上去很严重，并且对我抱有敌意……\
**Vertin**: That man, Stefen. He clearly knows something. But he appears to be rather mentally unstable, and he's hostile towards me.

**维尔汀**：Z女士曾经告诉过我，遇到这种不稳定的对象，需要特别注意沟通的方式、技巧，以及……准备好突发情况的兜底保障。\
**Vertin**: Madam Z cautioned me on this. I must be extra careful when dealing with people like him. Should make sure I have a backup plan in place before proceeding.

**维尔汀**：而现在，红弩箭还不在这儿……\
**Vertin**: Still no sign of Lilya.

思及此，她使用通讯设备联络了飞行女巫。不久之后，彼端传来了通讯失败的忙音。\
She tries contacting her on her communication device, but the line is busy.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

她继续了通讯的尝试，结果并无意外。\
She tries again, but still no luck.

**维尔汀**：她是不是遇到了什么麻烦……？\
**Vertin**: Did she get in trouble?

房间里忽然响起了尖锐的电话声。钴绿色的电话座机正剧烈地震动着。\
Suddenly, the phone on the nightstand rings. It vibrates violently.

**维尔汀**：您好？\
**Vertin**: Hello?

**电话**：哒，哒，哒，哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap, tap, tap, tap*

**维尔汀**：……您好？\
**Vertin**: Hello?!

电话的彼端响起了意义不明的叩击声。\
A series of strange tapping sounds comes from the other end of the line.

**维尔汀**：请问，是蓝手帕小姐吗？\
**Vertin**: Erm, is that Ms. Tuesday?

**电话**：哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap*

**电话**：哒，哒——哒，哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap, tap—tap, tap*

**电话**：哒，哒——哒——哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap, tap—tap—tap*

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

明晰的短音与长音，以一定的节奏交织着。\
The short and long sounds are distinct. They form a certain rhythm.

**维尔汀**：我想，我知道这是什么了。\
**Vertin**: Oh, I think I know what this is.

**电话**：哒，哒——哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap, tap—tap*

**维尔汀**：R。\
**Vertin**: That's an R.

**电话**：哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap*

**维尔汀**：E。\
**Vertin**: E.

**电话**：哒，哒，哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap, tap, tap*

**维尔汀**：S。\
**Vertin**: S.

**电话**：哒，哒——哒——哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap, tap—tap—tap*

**维尔汀**：P。\
**Vertin**: P.

**电话**：哒——哒——哒——\
**Telephone**: *tap—tap—tap—*

**维尔汀**：O。\
**Vertin**: O.

电话被急促地挂断了。——但这无碍于思维的补全。\
The phone is abruptly hung up. But it doesn't matter. The thoughts are complete.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

一份由摩斯电码传达的密电。\
A message conveyed through Morse code.

这是一种为了安全而舍弃效率的信息传达方式，常用于情报的传递，在日常生活中极为少见。\
A means of communication that sacrifices efficiency for safety. It's commonly used in intelligence, but rarely for anything else.

在一个汽车旅馆中，为什么会出现这样的信息？\
Why would there be such a message in a motel?

**电话**：叮铃铃铃铃——\
**Telephone**: *ring-ring-ring—*

铃声再次响起，电话被不假思索地接起。\
The telephone rings again. She picks it up without hesitation.

**蓝手帕**：您好，是维尔汀小姐吗？\
**Tuesday**: Hello, is this Ms. Vertin?

**维尔汀**：……蓝手帕小姐？\
**Vertin**: Ms. Tuesday?

**蓝手帕**：噢，我需要告知您一则通知。\
**Tuesday**: Yes. I have an announcement for you.

**蓝手帕**：附近信号塔的电线遭到了魔精的啃噬，需要进行检修——这会导致通讯上的不便。但旅馆的内线电话始终是接通的。\
**Tuesday**: There's a service outage going on in the area. Some critters nibbled through the cables of a nearby signal tower. But all our internal phone lines are still running well.

**维尔汀**：我明白了。\
**Vertin**: I see.

**蓝手帕**：我想，很快就会检修完毕……毕竟附近那个军备工厂也与旅馆同用一个信号塔——无论如何，对您造成的困扰，我深表歉意。\
**Tuesday**: It should be repaired soon, since we share the signal tower with that armament factory. I apologize for any inconvenience this may cause.

**蓝手帕**：在不久之后，我会为您送上一份晚餐……不必担心费用问题，这是一份完全的馈赠。\
**Tuesday**: I'll bring your dinner up later. It's on the house.

**维尔汀**：事实上，我刚刚接到了一个来源不明的电话……\
**Vertin**: There's something I want to ask you. I received a phone call earlier.

**蓝手帕**：噢……不久前，我也收到过金伯利女郎关于电话的投诉。\
**Tuesday**: Oh, Ms. Kimberly was also prank-called not long ago.

**蓝手帕**：请您无需担心，我想这也是魔精们的捣乱——您也知道，它们总是很调皮，就像一群猴子，有适量的智力用于捉弄他人。\
**Tuesday**: I suppose it's a critter's doing—you know how mischievous they can be, and since they have decent smarts, they can play some pretty nasty tricks.

也许理论上会存在猴子在打字机上撰写莎士比亚全集的概率，但这会在现实世界中出现吗？\
In theory, a group of monkeys could write Shakespeare's complete works on a typewriter if given the time. But would this happen in reality?

**维尔汀**：我认为这不是巧合。\
**Vertin**: I don't think that's what made the phone call.

**蓝手帕**：噢，维尔汀小姐，但这就是我眼见的现实……\
**Tuesday**: Mm, well, Ms. Vertin, this is what I understand to be the truth.

**维尔汀**：有什么样的餐点？\
**Vertin**: May I ask what's on the menu?

**蓝手帕**：噢……我们这儿有每天一顿的免费餐点，是火腿三明治和一杯牛奶。\
**Tuesday**: We have one free meal a day—a ham sandwich and a glass of milk.

**蓝手帕**：如果您有别的需求，我们这儿也能做烤鸡或是鹰嘴豆泥……或者是一些简单的墨西哥菜。\
**Tuesday**: If you'd like to have something else, we've also got roast chicken and hummus and a few simple Mexican dishes.

**维尔汀**：谢谢，等我的同伴回来之后，我会问问她想吃些什么。\
**Vertin**: Thank you. I'll ask my friend what she thinks when she comes back.

**蓝手帕**：噢，还有一点需要提醒您，我们在9点之后就不会再供应餐点了。\
**Tuesday**: Oh, and the kitchen closes at nine. Please take note of that.

**蓝手帕**：您还有别的疑问吗？\
**Tuesday**: Is there anything else I can help you with?

**维尔汀**：暂时没有了。\
**Vertin**: I'm good for now. Thank you.

撂下电话后，脖颈处忽然传来了轻微的触感，如同一片羽毛拂过皮肤。\
As she hangs up, she feels a light touch on her neck, like a feather brushing against her skin.

抬头望去，天花板的角落中，一条若隐若现的细丝垂了下来。\
She reflexively touches her neck. It's a spider's web. She follows it up to the corner of the ceiling.

**维尔汀**：……蜘蛛？\
**Vertin**: Spiders?

节肢动物落在了木柜子的案面上。它挥动细长的足，从一片暗处，爬行到另一片暗处。\
A spider falls onto the surface of the wooden cabinet. It moves its slender legs, crawling from one shadowy spot to another.

它行走时，引燃了空气中的火花。\
As it moves, sparks ignite in the air.

随后，神秘术的辉光显现。借着这一瞬的光芒，她得以看清了一切。\
Then, in the glow of an arcane skill, she can see everything clearly.

**维尔汀**：……奇怪，这是……神秘学术阵？\
**Vertin**: Is that an arcane array?

**维尔汀**：很熟悉的纹路，我曾经在哪里见过它。\
**Vertin**: The pattern's familiar. I've seen it somewhere before.

床头柜的表面，镌刻着几道凹凸不平的痕迹。手指抚上纹路，试图分辨刻痕的纹理与走向。\
The surface of the bedside cabinet has a rough engraving on it. She traces the markings with her fingers, trying to discern their texture and direction.

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

术阵的纹理烫伤了指尖，籍由这一瞬的痛感，过去的回忆从脑海中被唤醒。\
The array burns her fingertips, and in that momentary pain, memories are awakened.

**维尔汀**：我见过这个术阵。\
**Vertin**: Yes, I've definitely seen this before,

**维尔汀**：……在第一防线学校的课堂中。\
**Vertin**: when I was in school.

**教员**：这是一种极其危险的术阵，脱离了固有的范式——这代表着它不受控制。\
**Instructor**: This is an extremely dangerous array—one that you are prohibited from using. It can go easily beyond the caster's control.

**教员**：我们学习神秘术，驯化未知的能量，让它们为我们所用。\
**Instructor**: We study arcanum and tame it for our use.

**教员**：而这力量一旦超过合理的限度，反而会引发自身的毁灭……\
**Instructor**: But once its power surpasses our limits, it is highly likely that it will lead to our own destruction.

**教员**：我需要你们记住这个图案，因为我会在下一次测验中考到它。\
**Instructor**: I need you all to remember that. It'll be in your next exam.

学生们低下稚嫩的脖颈，教室中满溢沙沙的书写声。\
The students put their heads down, and the sound of scribbling fills the classroom.

**十四行诗**：维尔汀，你在听吗？\
**Sonetto**: Vertin? Are you listening?

**十四行诗**：教员说，这是一定会考核的内容。如果你需要笔记的话……\
**Sonetto**: The instructor just said it'd be in the next exam. If you like, you can check my notes.

优等生惴惴不安地攥紧了手中的笔记本。\
The top student nervously clutches her notebook in her hands.

**维尔汀**：……谢谢，不过，我在想另一个问题。\
**Vertin**: Oh, thank you. My mind was somewhere else.

**维尔汀**：为什么学校要把一个学生根本无法用到的术阵，作为考试的重点？\
**Vertin**: Why have they made it a key point of the exam if we can't even use it?

**维尔汀**：……我想，教员的本意并不是让我们学会使用这些术阵。\
**Vertin**: I see. They didn't teach us about arrays so that we could use them.

**维尔汀**：——而是尽快地识别它，好察觉危险的来源。\
**Vertin**: They wanted us to be able to identify them so that we could avoid danger.

她转头望向窗外，暮色沉沉。\
She looks out the window. It's getting dark.

**维尔汀**：如果贸然行动，极有可能引发爆炸，或是其他结果……\
**Vertin**: It's highly likely to cause an explosion or other severe consequences if I act too hastily.

不远处的术阵中，有微弱的光芒正在闪烁。\
The array glows faintly.

**维尔汀**：不能再等下去了，红弩箭不在这儿，我得尽快找到一个帮手。\
**Vertin**: Lilya still hasn't come back. I must find someone else to help.

一个帮手需要具备什么特质？\
What qualities should an ally have?

果决，利落，有一些进攻或自保的手段。\
Decisiveness, efficiency, some means of offense or self-defense ...

笃、笃——

突如其来的敲门声打断了她的思绪。\
A sudden knock on the door interrupts her thoughts.

门扉开启后，一张眼熟的面孔出现了。\
She opens it to a familiar face.

**阿尔古斯**：嘿，小姑娘，我刚刚在走廊见到了你。\
**Argus**: Hey. We met back in the hallway, remember?

**阿尔古斯**：——我得说，现在轮到你了。\
**Argus**: Now, it's your turn.

**维尔汀**：在没有说明前因后果的情况下，我很难对此做出正确的反应，小姐。\
**Vertin**: What exactly do you want from me, Miss?

雇佣兵挑了挑眉毛。\
The mercenary raises an eyebrow.

**阿尔古斯**：很简单，我要找的人就藏在这个旅馆里——为了找到她，我不得不翻遍整座旅馆。\
**Argus**: Well, it's simple. The person I'm looking for is right here in this motel, and I'm scouring every corner of it to find her.

**阿尔古斯**：小姐，我并不是在提一些无礼的要求，你当然可以开出你的价码。\
**Argus**: Look, missy, I don't wanna make things hard for you. Name your price, and we can talk.

**维尔汀**：……如果一个人这样地躲着您，那么她大概是不愿意见您。\
**Vertin**: If this person's gone to such great lengths to avoid you, perhaps she doesn't want to see you at all.

**阿尔古斯**：噢，这不是我该考虑的事情——雇主发布了任务，我只需要完成它，无论是捉奸、跟踪，还是送信……没有差别。\
**Argus**: Well, that ain't my concern, is it? A job's a job. Whether it's catching a cheating spouse, tracking someone down, or delivering a letter, it don't make no difference to me.

**维尔汀**：……好吧，但你的任务目标不在这个房间里——我很确定这里没有其他人。\
**Vertin**: Very well. But you'll have to look elsewhere, I'm afraid. There's no one but me in this room.

**阿尔古斯**：哈。\
**Argus**: Hah.

**阿尔古斯**：我自然有我的用意——您先转过头，看向这个房间。\
**Argus**: Look, I know what I'm doing. How about you turn around and take a good look around the room?

**维尔汀**：……你不会趁我转头的时候敲晕我吧？\
**Vertin**: So you can knock me out as soon as I turn my back to you?

**阿尔古斯**：哈哈哈……\
**Argus**: Hahaha!

雇佣兵发出了爽朗的笑声。\
The mercenary gives a hearty laugh.

**阿尔古斯**：小姑娘，如果我只是想敲晕你，我就不必花这些功夫，和你说上这样多的话。\
**Argus**: Missy, if that were my plan, I wouldn't have spent all this time talking to you.

**阿尔古斯**：非必要的情况下，我还是更愿意用一种合情合理的方式来解决问题——不必让双方闹得太不愉快。\
**Argus**: I much prefer to do my business pleasantly. I don't like to see things get too ugly.

**维尔汀**：……好。\
**Vertin**: I see.

**阿尔古斯**：不转头也没有关系，我会告诉你我看见的一切。\
**Argus**: Fine. If you don't wanna turn around, I'll tell you what I see.

雇佣兵眯起眼睛，眼中辉光流转。\
The mercenary squints, that same emerald light shimmering in her eye.

**阿尔古斯**：您的手指被烫伤了——为什么这样的不小心？\
**Argus**: You've burned your finger there. You should be more careful.

**维尔汀**：这是……\
**Vertin**: This is ...

**阿尔古斯**：真奇怪，这不像是因为靠近火源而造成的灼伤……更像是某种神秘能量？\
**Argus**: Don't look like a fire burn to me. What was it? Some arcane energy?

**阿尔古斯**：看来……和其他的房间一样，这个房间也有它的秘密。\
**Argus**: Looks like this room has a couple secrets, too.

雇佣兵的视线望向了更遥远的方向。\
The mercenary shifts her gaze to the room further away.

**阿尔古斯**：哈，我猜——您刚刚触摸了位于某处的神秘术术阵，而术阵造成的烫伤在您的手上留下了灼痕？我说得对吗？\
**Argus**: So you touched an arcane array, and its power burned you. How's that for a guess? Pretty close, huh?

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

她望向那双正燃烧着蓝绿色的眼睛。\
She examines the mercenary's burning emerald eye.

**阿尔古斯**：小姑娘，这是我的神秘术，能够帮助我看清楚所有的痕迹。这也是那些老板看重我的原因。\
**Argus**: This is my arcane skill. It allows me to see the traces that people leave behind. That's how I get these jobs, you see.

**阿尔古斯**：一件事要不留下痕迹，只有一种可能性——它从未发生。所以，我来到这个房间，只是为了寻找痕迹，而不是寻找人。\
**Argus**: Ain't nothing happening that don't leave a trace. If there ain't no trace, then it never happened. I came to your room to look for evidence, not a person.

**维尔汀**：我明白了，您是想要知道——那位追踪对象是否来过这里，对吗？\
**Vertin**: I see. You want to know whether the person you're tracking has been here, right?

**阿尔古斯**：聪明的小姑娘。\
**Argus**: Now we're talking.

**维尔汀**：在你调查房间之前，我还有一个问题……你是附近的受雇佣者？\
**Vertin**: Before I let you investigate the room, I have one more question. You take jobs from people nearby, don't you?

**阿尔古斯**：很明显，不是吗？\
**Argus**: Of course. It's obvious, ain't it?

她没有等到自己想要的回应。而在这熟悉的沉默中，老道的雇佣兵似乎捕捉到了一线生意即将到来的气息。\
She doesn't get the response she wants. In this familiar silence, the experienced mercenary smells an imminent deal.

那是一种防备与信任，期待与犹疑交杂的情绪。\
It's a mixture of caution and trust, anticipation and doubt.

**阿尔古斯**：相较于我不合常理的请求，您似乎更关注我的身份。\
**Argus**: You seem more intrigued by my profession than my peculiar request.

**阿尔古斯**：——您是遇到麻烦了，是吗？\
**Argus**: You're in trouble, ain't you?

**阿尔古斯**：那么，我再向您坦诚地介绍一下自己。我叫阿尔古斯，26岁，有丰富的受雇佣经验。\
**Argus**: Then let me formally introduce myself. The name's Argus, I'm 26, and I have extensive experience as a mercenary.

**维尔汀**：成交。\
**Vertin**: Let's make a deal.

**维尔汀**：您可以查探这个房间……但在这段时间里，我需要您协助我的调查。\
**Vertin**: You may search this room all you like, and I won't say a thing. But in return, I'd like your assistance in my own investigation.

**阿尔古斯**：调查什么？\
**Argus**: How, exactly?

**维尔汀**：……你能看出柜子上的术阵是什么时候镌刻的吗？\
**Vertin**: Can you tell when that array on the cupboard was drawn?

雇佣兵斜挎着枪支，走入了房间的内部，在床头柜的侧边蹲了下来。在短暂的观察之后，她给出了结论。\
Argus slings her shotgun over her shoulder and crouches down beside the nightstand. After a brief examination, she gives her assessment.

**阿尔古斯**：距离现在不超过24小时。\
**Argus**: Less than 24 hours ago.

**维尔汀**：……也就是说，这些都是上一个住客留下的痕迹。\
**Vertin**: In other words, this was left behind by the last guest who stayed in this room.

面对这个结论，雇佣兵摇了摇头。\
Argus shakes her head.

**阿尔古斯**：未必。\
**Argus**: Can't say for certain.

## THH-06 玻璃酒瓶 / Glass Bottles

空无一人的工厂内，空气潮湿而冰冷。\
The empty factory is cold and damp.

**红弩箭**：哈，希望你别是个空架子。\
**Lilya**: Hah, let's see what you've got in there for me.

她沿着工厂晃了两圈，在收发室里看见了一个硕大的木箱，上面盖满了邮戳。\
She wanders the factory, eventually spotting a large crate covered in postage stamps in the receiving room.

狭长的木箱被钉子紧紧地钉着。她眯着眼睛，借着窗外的月光，看清了木箱上的字迹——\
The crate is nailed tightly shut. She squints, having only the moonlight to help her read the words on the box.

红色38，莉莉娅。\
Red 38, Lilya.

**红弩箭**：哈，老伙计！\
**Lilya**: Hey, buddy!

她蹲下身，细细地检视着木箱。在伸手敲了敲木箱之后，飞行员拧起了眉毛。\
She squats down and inspects the crate. After tapping it a few times, she frowns.

**红弩箭**：只有一层木板——这就是他们的保护措施？\
**Lilya**: They just left her in a wooden box. What kind of safekeeping is this?

**红弩箭**：行吧，时间紧急，这笔账以后再和他们算……\
**Lilya**: Anyway, I don't have much time. I'll settle that with them later.

她伸出双手，托住了木箱的两端。\
She grabs the crate and tries to lift it.

木箱岿然不动——是重力术式。\
It doesn't budge—it's bound by arcanum.

**红弩箭**：……他们至少准备了一个需要特定口令才能解除的重力术式——\
**Lilya**: Alright. At least they bothered to put a gravity ritual on it.

细微的脚步声在身后响起。\
Light footsteps echo behind her.

**？？？**：您也是在准备撤离吗？\
**???**: Are you also preparing to evacuate?

飞行员转过身，一个纤细的身影映入眼帘。\
Lilya turns around. A slender girl stands before her, a basket in her arms.

**红弩箭**：来得好，你是这儿管事的人？\
**Lilya**: Ah, perfect timing. Are you in charge here?

挎着篮子的女孩打量了她一番之后，甜甜地笑了。\
The girl looks her up and down before giving a sweet smile.

**凯拉**：中尉，我当然不是管事的人，也不是什么可疑的人——我只是经过这儿而已，您可以叫我凯拉。\
**Kayla**: No, I'm not in charge of anything, Lieutenant. I'm just passing through. I'm Kayla, by the way.

**凯拉**：我在外面听到了一些响动，还以为是那些不听管教的孩子又来这儿偷军火了……这些东西的价格可不便宜，总有小偷会打上它们的主意。\
**Kayla**: I heard some rattling here and thought some of those kids might've come back to steal weapons again. These things aren't cheap, and the kids know it.

**红弩箭**：偷军火的孩子？有意思，这儿看守的人呢？\
**Lilya**: Kids stealing from the military? Hah, that's a new one. Where are the guards here?

**凯拉**：这位中尉，没有人告诉您吗？\
**Kayla**: Oh. Didn't they tell you, Lieutenant?

女孩略感惊讶地说道。\
The girl sounds surprised.

**凯拉**：早在一个月以前，这儿的军队就已经开始撤离了，他们没有留下多少士兵——连我都知道这些。\
**Kayla**: The army stationed here started evacuating a month ago. There aren't many of them around these days.

**红弩箭**：撤离？\
**Lilya**: Evacuating?

眼前的状况与基金会告知的信息别无二致，飞行员察觉到了一丝危机的预兆。\
The Foundation's report was correct. Lilya senses impending danger.

**红弩箭**：告诉我，哪里能找到那些留下的士兵？\
**Lilya**: Then where can I find the soldiers that are still here?

**凯拉**：嗯……您是从镇子外面来的吧？在路上的时候，您是否有看到路边的酒吧？\
**Kayla**: Hmm. You're new in town, right? Did you see a bar on your way here?

**凯拉**：在闲暇的时候，那些芝诺的士兵最喜欢去那儿喝酒……您尽可以去看看，说不准他正在那儿呢？\
**Kayla**: That's where the Zeno soldiers spend their nights drinking. You might wanna check there first. That's probably where you'll find him.

**红弩箭**：他长什么样子？\
**Lilya**: Him? What does he look like?

**凯拉**：噢，就像所有芝诺士兵那样，您保准一眼就能认出他。\
**Kayla**: Like every other Zeno soldier. They all look the same to me. You'll know when you see him.

她忽然停止了说话，上下打量着飞行员。\
She pauses, looking the pilot up and down.

**凯拉**：但是我得告诉您……酒吧里的人并不欢迎外乡人——您听说过“启明会”吗？\
**Kayla**: But I have to tell you: The bar doesn't like outsiders. Have you heard of the Order of Enlightenment?

**凯拉**：这是一个非常活跃的密教组织……前不久他们一直在镇子上宣教，而今天正是他们做祷告的日子。\
**Kayla**: It's an occult society—very active these days. They were preaching in this town just a few days ago. Today is their day of prayer.

**红弩箭**：这和我有什么关系？\
**Lilya**: And, what does that have to do with me?

**凯拉**：当然与您有关系——因为他们做祷告的地方，正是镇子上的酒吧。\
**Kayla**: The bar you're going to is where they gather to pray.

**凯拉**：再多的，我就不知道了。总之，您如果要去那儿，一定要多加小心。\
**Kayla**: That's all I know. If you're going up there, please be careful.

**红弩箭**：哈……谢了。\
**Lilya**: Hah. Thanks.

飞行员转身离去，而白衣的少女依然立在原地，静静地望着她离去的背影。\
Lilya turns and leaves. The girl watches her as she goes.

**凯拉**：……愿“受苦者”保佑您。\
**Kayla**: May the Sufferer watch over you.

**凯拉**：我们将奉行“受苦者”的意志，让那过去的荣光行于当下……\
**Kayla**: Great Sufferer, by your decree, the glory of former days shall grace our present path.

她低声地祷告着。于她合拢的双手之上，戒指漆黑的刻面正在闪闪发亮。\
She whispers a prayer. As she clasps her hands together, the black facets of her ring shimmer.

**客人Ⅰ**：我们将奉行“受苦者”的意志，让那过去的荣光行于当下。\
**Guest I**: Great Sufferer, by your decree, the glory of former days shall grace our present path.

**客人Ⅱ**：我们将进献心灵中的一切，以信仰换取崇高的福祉。\
**Guest II**: We dedicate our souls and minds to you. We seek the well-being of our people in your name.

肃穆的氛围笼罩着那座小小的酒吧，灯光昏黄地亮着。聚集的人们或披黑袍，或着常服。他们彼此依靠，如兄弟之于兄弟，姊妹之于姊妹。\
A solemn atmosphere fills the bar. A small group has gathered under the dim lights, some in black robes, others in everyday clothes. They lean on each other like brothers and sisters.

为首的一人高举着手中的玻璃酒杯，对着在座的所有人遥相致意。\
The man leading the prayer raises his glass and gives a toast.

**酒吧老板**：愿“受苦者”保佑诸位。\
**Bar Owner**: May the Sufferer watch over you.

**酒吧老板**：祂的恩典必将使我们福杯满溢。\
**Bar Owner**: Under THEIR grace, may our cups overflow.

**酒吧老板**：敬颂“受苦者”。\
**Bar Owner**: To the Sufferer.

**众**：敬颂“受苦者”！\
**Crowd**: To the Sufferer!

酒吧的大门被猛然推开了。\
The bar door flings open.

**客人Ⅰ**：一个外乡人？\
**Guest I**: Hm? Odd time for a stranger to come.

年轻的飞行员望着眼前的一切。\
The young pilot looks around.

**红弩箭**：……真热闹。\
**Lilya**: Not crashing the party, am I?

她径自走向吧台，酒墙上各色的玻璃酒瓶正闪烁着光泽。\
She heads straight to the bar, where the shelves glitter with various bottles.

**红弩箭**：纳帕河谷葡萄酒、加州红酒、肯塔基的威士忌……哈，好货不少。\
**Lilya**: Napa Valley, Californian red, Kentucky whiskey ... Hah, there's a lot of good stuff here.

**红弩箭**：来一杯伏特加纯饮，我要你这儿最好的牌子。\
**Lilya**: One vodka. Straight. The best you got.

**酒吧老板**：现在不是开业的时间，斯拉夫人。\
**Bar Owner**: It ain't business hours, lady.

咔哒。\
*click*

这声音她再熟悉不过——有一把枪，正在数英寸之远的地方上了膛。\
She knows that sound—someone's cocking a gun just inches away from her.

**红弩箭**：嘿，我只是想买酒——这就是你们对待客人的方式吗？\
**Lilya**: Hey, all I did was ask for a drink! Is this how you treat your customers?

**酒吧老板**：我说了，没有。\
**Bar Owner**: As I said, we ain't serving you.

**红弩箭**：开酒吧的没有伏特加？\
**Lilya**: Why? Don't you have vodka?

**红弩箭**：那来一杯威士忌吧，我不挑。\
**Lilya**: Fine, I can settle for whiskey. Have to learn to take what we can get, eh?

**酒吧老板**：——没有。\
**Bar Owner**: You ain't getting that, either.

**红弩箭**：这也没有？\
**Lilya**: Seriously? You don't have any whiskey?

她望向了酒墙上琳琅满目的威士忌。\
She glances at the whiskey bottles lining the shelves.

**红弩箭**：那我知道芝诺为什么要撤离了——那帮家伙嗜酒如命，他们可没有办法在这儿待下去。\
**Lilya**: Pft. I'm starting to understand why Zeno evacuated. What's the point of living in a town where there's no real liquor? Especially for those drunkards.

**酒吧老板**：芝诺的中尉为什么要来这儿喝酒？你们的工厂仓库里没有酒精燃料了吗？\
**Bar Owner**: What's a Zeno lieutenant doing here, anyway? No alcohol fuel in that warehouse of yours?

客人们发出一阵哄笑。\
The patrons laugh.

**红弩箭**：哈，我可不知道当地有喝酒精燃料的习俗。\
**Lilya**: Hah! You sure have some interesting drinking habits down here.

**红弩箭**：——说真的，我很好奇，那个“受苦者”到底给了你们多少好处？\
**Lilya**: But I'm curious. What did this Sufferer promise you to make you all change your faith?

**红弩箭**：让固执的德克萨斯人改变信仰，这不是一件简单的事。\
**Lilya**: I mean, that's quite an achievement, especially here in Texas.

她敏锐地转身，一颗子弹擦过了她的发丝。\
She turns, narrowly avoiding a bullet. It whizzes past her hair.

**红弩箭**：这就忍不住了？\
**Lilya**: Oh, so we're doing this now, are we?

玻璃酒瓶碎了一地，晶亮的酒液浸透了地板。\
Bottles crash to the floor, splashing alcohol all over the bar.

**酒吧老板**：呼……呼……\
**Bar Owner**: *pant*

**红弩箭**：我没有兴趣掺和多余的事。你只要告诉我，那个芝诺的士兵去哪儿了？\
**Lilya**: Look, I don't care what you're doing here. Just tell me where that Zeno soldier went.

飞行员望着趴伏在酒柜上的老板。\
She looks down at the bar owner slumped over the counter.

**酒吧老板**：芝诺士兵……？\
**Bar Owner**: What Zeno soldier?

男人勉力睁大了肿胀的眼睛。\
The man strains to open his swollen eyes.

**红弩箭**：别装傻。\
**Lilya**: Don't play dumb with me.

**酒吧老板**：噢……那个士兵，他是一个十足的蠢货。\
**Bar Owner**: Oh. That soldier. He's a complete idiot, that one.

**酒吧老板**：芝诺已经完全地抛弃他了，他却总觉得是芝诺赏识他，才委派给他看守工厂的任务……\
**Bar Owner**: It's obvious that Zeno's abandoned him. But he insists that they left him here because they believed that only he could keep the warehouse safe.

**酒吧老板**：这就是你们芝诺的作风。既然已经决定抛弃他，为什么现在又要寻找他？\
**Bar Owner**: Why are you looking for him now if you decided to ditch him in the first place?

**红弩箭**：……听着，我知道你们看不惯芝诺。但这和我没关系。\
**Lilya**: Listen, I can tell you guys aren't the biggest fans of Zeno, but that has nothing to do with me.

**红弩箭**：我来这儿只是为了拿回我的东西。\
**Lilya**: I'm just here to get my stuff back.

**酒吧老板**：呼……\
**Bar Owner**: *exhale*

他虚弱地喘了一口气。\
He takes a labored breath.

**酒吧老板**：如果你执意要找他，那他也许在镇子的远郊喝酒。\
**Bar Owner**: Fine. If you insist on finding him, try your luck on the outskirts of town. He might be drinking there.

**红弩箭**：哈，谢了。\
**Lilya**: Hmph. Thanks.

飞行员踩着夜色，离开了这间沉寂的酒吧。\
She steps over the unconscious man beside her and leaves the bar.

## THH-07 羊皮纸 / The Parchment

**阿尔古斯**：这未必是上一位房客留下的痕迹。\
**Argus**: We can't say for sure if this ritual was created by the last guest.

**阿尔古斯**：实际上，在这个旅馆的所有房间中，或多或少地都存在着一些古怪的痕迹——这些痕迹非常新鲜，存续的时间不会超过一个月。\
**Argus**: Fact is, you can find all kinds of unusual markings in this motel—most of them less than a month old. Very recent indeed.

**阿尔古斯**：那名侍应生说，最近并没有大体量的旅客潮——所以，我猜应当是一个精通秘术的团伙，在各个房间之中流窜。\
**Argus**: The maid said that there ain't many tourists these days, so my guess is that a group of skilled arcanists have left their work in every room.

**阿尔古斯**：根据留下的痕迹推断，这个团伙大约有三至五人……\
**Argus**: Based on the markings I've seen so far, there were about three to five people in this group.

**维尔汀**：那么，这些人里，有一位羊首人身的神秘学家吗？\
**Vertin**: And was there a sheep-headed arcanist among them?

**阿尔古斯**：哈，这我可就不知道了。\
**Argus**: Well, that I don't know.

**阿尔古斯**：但我能告诉您的是……这儿确实有羊存在过的痕迹——我曾在走廊上看到过几只小小的羊蹄印。\
**Argus**: What I can say, though, is that there was a sheep living in here. I saw some hoofprints on the hallway floor.

**阿尔古斯**：这里曾有人牵着羊来住宿，多么奇怪——但是，这儿是德州，附近多是农户，这样的事情似乎又没有那么奇怪了。\
**Argus**: It looked like someone had stayed in this motel with a sheep—sounds pretty odd, but I suppose it ain't too strange given the local farmland.

**阿尔古斯**：不过，我保证，有一个信息是您一定感兴趣的。\
**Argus**: But I'm sure this will catch your attention.

**维尔汀**：……什么？\
**Vertin**: What?

**阿尔古斯**：我们都知道，羊用四个蹄子来走路。\
**Argus**: We all know that sheep walk on four hooves.

**阿尔古斯**：但是我看到的足迹显然并不符合这个特征——它小巧而精致。最重要的是，脚印主人的行走方式更接近于人，而且……\
**Argus**: But the hoofprints I saw were different. They were small and delicate and, most importantly, followed the movement pattern of a human. Judging by the trail ...

**阿尔古斯**：我能看出来，脚印的主人是个瘦弱的孩子，身高约为5英尺。\
**Argus**: The owner of the hoofprints was about the size of a slender kid, maybe 5 feet tall.

雇佣兵口述的数据与基金会的报告如出一辙。\
This description exactly matches the Foundation's report.

**维尔汀**：……你说得没有错。\
**Vertin**: That's it. That's the one I'm looking for.

**阿尔古斯**：当然——您可以质疑我的为人，但绝不能质疑我的专业水准。\
**Argus**: Don't I know it—they can question my morals, but nobody can question my competence.

**阿尔古斯**：现在，我可以开始对房间的探查了吗？维尔汀小姐。\
**Argus**: So, may I enter your room now, Ms. Vertin?

**维尔汀**：请。\
**Vertin**: Please.

**阿尔古斯**：那么……首先来看看这个。\
**Argus**: Now, let's start with this little thing.

**阿尔古斯**：这些刻痕非常新鲜，没有被虫蚁咬噬，也没有遭到水雾的侵蚀。\
**Argus**: The carvings are new. No sign of woodworm damage or moisture absorption.

**阿尔古斯**：断口的木刺非常锐利，连……嗯？\
**Argus**: These splinters along the edge are extremely sharp. Mm?

痕迹中有一些暗红色的脆质结晶，她伸手蘸取。\
She dips her finger into a dark red, crumbly residue.

**阿尔古斯**：这是……血痂？\
**Argus**: Is this dried blood?

她揉搓着那些细碎的结晶，它们随着雇佣兵的动作化为更细碎的粉末。\
She rubs the granules between her finger and her thumb, reducing them to a fine powder.

**维尔汀**：它在术阵中作为触媒而使用。\
**Vertin**: Blood was used as the medium for this array.

**维尔汀**：这儿，未闭口的圆，用力不匀的线条。从作画方式来看——不是精于此道的专家。\
**Vertin**: The circle isn't fully closed here, and the lines are a bit uneven. Whoever drew this doesn't seem to be an expert.

**维尔汀**：您的身手不错，对吗？\
**Vertin**: You know how to deal with this, right?

**阿尔古斯**：老板，别小瞧我。\
**Argus**: All you have to do is ask, boss. You might be surprised.

**维尔汀**：我们需要尽可能快地摧毁这个术阵……我想这是一个危险的密教团体所篆刻的……\
**Vertin**: We need to destroy it as quickly as possible. I think it's been left by a dangerous occult group.

**阿尔古斯**：稍等。\
**Argus**: Hold on.

雇佣兵将枕头垫在了木板之上，随后扣下扳机。\
She places a pillow over the wood and pulls the trigger.

微弱的枪击声之后，残余的亮光熄灭了。\
After a faint gunshot, the lingering light goes out.

哗啦——\
*squelch*

新鲜的血液自术阵中涌出，浸湿了发白的刻痕。\
Fresh blood oozes from the array, settling in the faded carvings.

**维尔汀**：……血？\
**Vertin**: Is that blood?

雇佣兵恍若未闻，在错愕的目光中，她用手指蘸取了红色的液体，放在鼻端之下嗅闻着。\
The mercenary, unfazed, dips her finger into the red liquid and sniffs it.

**阿尔古斯**：这是一个神秘学家的血——不是凯拉。\
**Argus**: Yup. The blood of an arcanist. So it can't be Kayla's.

**维尔汀**：……你能看出这位神秘学家的身份吗？\
**Vertin**: Can you discern the owner's identity?

**阿尔古斯**：老板，你未免有些太高估我了——我并不能通过血的气味定位到某个具体的人。\
**Argus**: Hah, I ain't all-knowing. I can't identify people by their blood.

**阿尔古斯**：——还需要更多的线索。\
**Argus**: No, I'll need more than just blood to find out who was here.

**阿尔古斯**：……嗯？\
**Argus**: Mm?

雇佣兵从柜子与墙面的缝隙处，摸出了一本遍布灰尘的羊皮手册。\
She fishes out a dusty sheepskin journal from the gap between the cabinet and the wall.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

她翻开了手册。\
She flips through the pages.

**阿尔古斯**：我等乃金属之第一本质，以及唯一源泉。\
**Argus**: "We are the beginning and the original source of metals."

**阿尔古斯**：经由我等，伟大艺术之最高酊剂得以酿造。\
**Argus**: "Through us, the highest tincture of art is brewed."

**阿尔古斯**：无泉无水能似我，我成全贫者和富者，或让他们罹患病灾。\
**Argus**: "There is neither a spring nor water like mine. I heal and help both the rich and the poor."

**阿尔古斯**：因我可为良药，可为鸩酒。\
**Argus**: "Yet I am full of hurtful poison."

**阿尔古斯**：……什么意思？\
**Argus**: What the hell does that mean?

**维尔汀**：这是一段有关于炼金术的引文。\
**Vertin**: It's a quote from a text on alchemy.

**阿尔古斯**：只需要准备足量且优质的材料，画出足够准确的术阵，一切问题都能够被解决。\
**Argus**: "All challenges will be resolved with the provision of sufficient and high quality materials and the precise execution of the array."

**阿尔古斯**：那么——从哪里可以找到优质的材料？\
**Argus**: "But where do we find these materials?"

她快速地翻动着陈旧的手册，缝隙中堆积的炼金产物飘扬在空气之中。\
She continues to flick through the journal, releasing the accumulated alchemical residue on its pages into the air.

最后一页中，形态抽搐的文字如同遭受火刑的罪者，于书页上写满了孤独的呓语。\
On the last page, tortured words are scrawled on the paper. It looks like something a criminal would write in their final moments before their death sentence.

**阿尔古斯**：存在的，分裂的，终将走向极一。\
**Argus**: "What was once sundered shall reunite."

**维尔汀**：咳、咳……\
**Vertin**: *cough*

鼻腔滚烫，细不可察的火花在空气中涌动。\
Her nose burns as barely visible sparks heat the air.

**阿尔古斯**：我看见过这个笔迹。\
**Argus**: I've seen this handwriting before.

**“启明会”信众Ⅰ**：还有……这是我的电话。\
**"Order" Follower I**: And here. My phone number.

追随者随之递过来一张美钞，上面潦草地写着一串数字。\
He hands over a dollar bill with a string of numbers scrawled along the blank space.

雇佣兵从口袋中掏出了那张皱巴巴的钞票，将上面的字迹与羊皮手册进行比对。\
The mercenary pulls out the crumpled bill from her pocket, comparing the handwriting with that in the journal.

**阿尔古斯**：……是了，两份笔迹的书写特征完全吻合。\
**Argus**: Yup. This is definitely the same.

砰——\
*bang*

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

**阿尔古斯**：……飞矢M1903式手枪。\
**Argus**: That sound. It's a Flying Arrow M1903 pistol.

**？？？**：啊啊啊啊——\
**???**: Ahhh.

**阿尔古斯**：……金伯利？怎么哪里都有她？\
**Argus**: Kimberly? What's wrong with her now?

**阿尔古斯**：老板，外面出岔子了。我得过去看看，你要和我来吗？\
**Argus**: I better go check it out, boss. Something don't seem right. You coming?

**阿尔古斯**：那个金伯利可能看见了什么。\
**Argus**: That Kimberly must've run into something.

## THH-08 纪实文学 / Face Reality

长绒的厚地毯本应具备绝佳的隔音效果。\
The thick carpet in the hallway is usually enough to dampen any sounds.

但人们急切的情绪让这份本应具有的功能无限地趋近于无。\
But no amount of soundproofing could stop the sound of a gunshot from echoing through the place.

枪响之处，毫无生机的史蒂文躺在地上。他的头上被开了一个大洞，孱弱的神经末梢在一片红色中颤动。\
At its source, Stefen's limp, twitching body lies on the floor. There's a gaping hole in his head.

**金伯利女郎**：啊……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Ah.

女房客失去了全身的力气，正惊魂未定地战栗着。\
She's trembling in fear.

**金伯利女郎**：他、他还活着吗……？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Is-Is he still alive?

**阿尔古斯**：蠢问题。\
**Argus**: Just when I thought you couldn't get any dumber.

**金伯利女郎**：……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...

**维尔汀**：这是自杀？\
**Vertin**: Is this a suicide?

**金伯利女郎**：他掏出枪，对着自己的太阳穴来了一枪……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: He pulled out the gun and shot himself in the head.

**金伯利女郎**：那些脑子里的东西，全部流到了地板和墙壁上……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: His brains splattered on the walls and flowed onto the floor.

她的喃喃自语近乎于告解。\
Her muttering is almost a confession.

雇佣兵俯下身，查看现场的狼藉。\
Argus kneels down to examine the body.

**阿尔古斯**：嗯……伤口附近存在灼伤与烟垢。\
**Argus**: Mm. There's gunshot residue and powder burns near the wound.

**阿尔古斯**：手上有火药粒。\
**Argus**: Gunpowder particles on his fingers.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**阿尔古斯**：他死于枪伤，子弹由飞矢M1903式手枪发出，贯穿了他的脑部。\
**Argus**: There's no doubt. He died from a gunshot wound. The bullet was fired from the pistol in his hand and went straight through his skull.

**阿尔古斯**：这把枪的来头可不小，是芝诺那边配发的军备用品——你惹上大麻烦了。\
**Argus**: But this ain't just any pistol. It's a Zeno pistol. You've got yourself in some serious trouble, missy.

**金伯利女郎**：不是我……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: It wasn't me.

她面色苍白，勉强地镇定了下来。\
Her face is still pale, but she manages to stop her shaking.

**金伯利女郎**：我只是一个路过的、可怜的、被牵连进来的普通人。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I'm just an innocent, sad, terrified girl who just happened to pass by.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

**阿尔古斯**：好吧，这位路过的、可怜的、被牵连进来的小姐。\
**Argus**: Well, Ms. Innocent-Sad-and-Terrified ...

**阿尔古斯**：如果你想完全摆脱自身的嫌疑，就告诉我们刚刚发生了什么。\
**Argus**: If you wanna prove your innocence, start by telling us what happened here.

**阿尔古斯**：——你说的谎言都会被我识破，因为这儿的痕迹不会骗人。\
**Argus**: And mind you, I will call you out if you lie. The evidence here will tell me what's true and what ain't.

她指了指自己的眼睛。\
She points to her eye.

**金伯利女郎**：……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...

**金伯利女郎**：既然你心里已经有了答案，那为什么还要问我！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: If you're so clever, then why are you asking me? Just figure it out yourself!

惊魂未定的女郎虚弱地申辩着。\
Her protestation is weak. She quickly gives in.

**金伯利女郎**：好吧，好吧——我告诉你们，这个疯子在这段时间里是怎么纠缠我的。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Ugh! Alright, alright! I'll tell you. This madman has been harassing me.

**金伯利女郎**：……自从我住进来之后，这个男人时常会在走廊中踱步。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Ever since I moved into this place, I'd often seen him pacing around in the hallway.

**金伯利女郎**：无论白天还是黑夜，他总是踩着重重的步子，一步一步踩在走廊上——他从来不会考虑别的人是不是要休息！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Day and night, he'd stomp around out here. He didn't care if anyone else was trying to sleep!

**金伯利女郎**：但也许他正因为什么事而困扰着呢？出于好心，我决定问问他，发生了什么事……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I thought he must have had a lot on his mind, like he was troubled or something. So I asked him what happened.

**史蒂文**：……\
**Stefen**: ...

他眼窝深陷，眼睛里布满了血丝，整个人呈现出一种神经质的特征。\
His deep, sunken eyes were bloodshot. Every fiber of his being screamed that something was wrong with him.

**金伯利女郎**：先生，如果您遇到了困难，可以寻找更合理的方式去解决——在走廊上踱步不仅不管用，还会影响到其他人的休息。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Sir, if you're having any problems, there are many ways to solve them, but pacing in the hallway isn't one of them. Plus, it disrupts everyone's sleep.

我敢打赌，我没有说任何过激的言语——但他接下来的反应却相当的无礼！\
I swear I didn't say anything too harsh, but he was just downright rude!

**史蒂文**：滚、滚开——离我远点！\
**Stefen**: Get the hell away! Get out of my face!

**金伯利女郎**：……什么？没礼貌的家伙。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Excuse me? That's pretty rude, you know.

我不想和疯子吵架，还好侍应生及时地过来，帮我解了围。\
I had no desire to argue with a madman. Thankfully, the maid intervened when she heard what was going on.

我不知道她是怎么劝说了史蒂文……总之他们最后达成了一致。史蒂文从此不再出现在走廊中，这对其他旅客而言是一件好事。\
I have no idea what she said to him, but eventually they came to terms. He stopped pacing the hallway from then on. That was a relief. I'm sure the other guests would agree.

这些话，那个侍应生都可以为我作证，你们大可去问问她。\
That maid can vouch for what I've said. Ask her yourselves.

不久之后，史蒂文写了一封信，通过门缝，塞到了我的房间里。\
Not long after, I found a letter from Stefen on the floor of my room. It'd been slid under my door.

信上说，他为他的鲁莽感到抱歉。\
In the letter, he apologized for his behavior.

……\
...

要不要原谅他呢？\
"Should I make peace with him?" I thought.

这么想着，我鬼使神差地往猫眼望去——奇怪的是，那里漆黑一片。\
As I wondered, I took a look through the peephole. It was strange. I couldn't see a thing. It was pitch black out there.

——这是猫眼坏了吗？\
"Is it broken?" I wondered.

没等我想得太多，房间里的电话铃声忽然叮铃铃地响了起来——吓了我一跳呢，还好那是侍应生的电话。\
Before I could dwell on it too much, the phone rang. I was startled, but it was just the front desk calling.

**蓝手帕**：您好，金伯利女郎。\
**Tuesday**: Hello, Ms. Kimberly.

**金伯利女郎**：是到了晚餐的时间吗？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Is it dinner time already?

**蓝手帕**：……不是。\
**Tuesday**: No.

**蓝手帕**：您与史蒂文先生有什么……\
**Tuesday**: Is there an issue between Mr. Stefen and yourself?

她欲言又止。\
She seemed hesitant to speak.

**金伯利女郎**：……嗯？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Mm?

**蓝手帕**：抱歉，也许我并不该问您这些，但目前的状况实在令人担心。\
**Tuesday**: I know it's not my place to ask, but the situation is a little concerning.

**蓝手帕**：史蒂文先生的整张脸都贴在了您的门板上……他应该正通过猫眼在看您。\
**Tuesday**: Mr. Stefen is standing at your door, his face pressed up against it.

**蓝手帕**：……我需要与您确认一个问题——您确定与他没有任何矛盾吗？\
**Tuesday**: So I just wanna confirm that everything's alright between you two.

**金伯利女郎**：……这就是我所遭遇的一切！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: And that's what happened!

**维尔汀**：不要太紧张，小姐。至少现在，一切都已经过去了。\
**Vertin**: Calm down, Miss. It's all over now.

**维尔汀**：那封信你还保存着吗？\
**Vertin**: Do you still have that letter with you?

女房客露出了嫌恶的表情，用下巴指了指脚边的垃圾桶。\
A look of disgust comes across Ms. Kimberly's face as she gestures to the trash can nearby.

**金伯利女郎**：谁会留着这种恶心的东西，当然是扔了——如果你们有兴趣，就在这儿找吧。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Who'd hold onto that? I threw it out right away. It's somewhere in that bin.

垃圾桶里只有一个被揉皱的纸团，雇佣兵拾起了它。\
Argus quickly retrieves the crumpled piece of paper from the trash can.

她尽力将纸抚平，阅读着上方的内容。\
