She smooths it out on her palm and reads its contents.

**阿尔古斯**：“亲爱的金伯利女郎……”\
**Argus**: "Dear Ms. Kimberly ..."

**阿尔古斯**：噢，小姐，我也没想到第一个疑问来得居然如此之快。\
**Argus**: I've got a question already.

**阿尔古斯**：——他为什么知道你叫金伯利？你们在之前可没有熟络到互通姓名的程度。\
**Argus**: How did he know your name? You didn't know each other well enough to have exchanged them, did you?

**金伯利女郎**：见鬼了……我才是那个受害者！你为什么要像审一个犯人一样来审我！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I'm the victim here, damn it! You can't interrogate me like this!

**金伯利女郎**：如果你非要知道这其中的原因……那我告诉你！因为我的同伴总会叫我的名字……谁知道是不是被史蒂文听见了。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Ugh, but if you must know, maybe he heard it when my friend called me.

**阿尔古斯**：你的同伴？\
**Argus**: Your friend?

**金伯利女郎**：当然得有同伴，一位像我这样高贵的小姐，怎么可能孤身来到这个地方……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Why, what's so odd about that? A young girl like myself should never travel alone to places like this!

窈窕的女郎愤愤不平地控诉着。\
She continues in her indignation.

**金伯利女郎**：我总得有柔软的床榻、美丽的衣饰，还有……最重要的粮食！要不是为了找东西，我才不会……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I need someone to make my bed and prepare my clothes, and, most importantly, I need to eat! I wouldn't even be here if I weren't looking for ...

**金伯利女郎**：——！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...!

她倒吸了一口凉气，用手捂住了自己的嘴。\
She gasps, covering her mouth with her hand.

雇佣兵无暇理会女郎聒噪的声音。她眯着眼睛，继续念诵着书信的内容。\
But Argus isn't listening. She continues to read the letter aloud.

**阿尔古斯**：“我对我在走廊上的行为深感歉意……”\
**Argus**: "I wanna apologize for my behavior earlier in the hallway."

**维尔汀**：嗯……这封信的措辞从头到尾都很正常，几乎看不出笔者是一位濒临崩溃的人。\
**Vertin**: Hmm. Looks like a perfectly normal letter to me. No hints that this is from a man on the verge of a mental breakdown.

**金伯利女郎**：如果你不相信我说的话，你大可去询问那位侍应生……她看见了一切，她可以为我作证！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: If you won't take my word for it, go ahead and ask the maid. She was there! She can vouch for me!

**维尔汀**：……请您冷静，我们没有冒犯您的意思。\
**Vertin**: Please. We aren't accusing you of anything.

雇佣兵用指尖夹住了那张信纸，发出了一声嗤笑。\
Argus lets out a laugh.

**阿尔古斯**：虽然笔迹学已经被证实为一种可信度极低的学问……但我还是不得不说一句。\
**Argus**: Though graphology has been criticized a lot these days, I gotta say ...

**阿尔古斯**：这个字迹更像是女人的字迹。\
**Argus**: This looks more like a woman's handwriting to me.

**金伯利女郎**：……史蒂文是女人？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: So you mean Stefen was a woman?

原本张牙舞爪的女郎微张着嘴，愣在了原地——\
Her aggression seems to dissipate as her eyes widen and her mouth drops.

**阿尔古斯**：哈哈……小姐，您想到哪儿去了？\
**Argus**: Hah! You still with us, missy?

**阿尔古斯**：我的意思是，这封信有可能不是由史蒂文先生书写的，而是由一位女性所书写。\
**Argus**: What I'm suggesting is that Mr. Stefen didn't write this letter, but a woman did.

**阿尔古斯**：……当然，这也只是一种猜测，也许史蒂文先生本人的字迹就是如此纤细呢？\
**Argus**: But that's just speculation. Chances are Mr. Stefen's handwriting was just a little feminine.

**阿尔古斯**：我会暂时保留这张纸条。现在，让我们继续之前的问题。\
**Argus**: I'll keep this letter for now. Back to my questions.

**阿尔古斯**：既然如此，你为什么要继续接近史蒂文？你明明知道他曾做过不合常理的行为。\
**Argus**: If the story you told is true, then why are you at the scene of his death? Did you go looking for him, even after all the weird things he'd done?

**金伯利女郎**：……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...

**金伯利女郎**：因为我饿了！我总不能饿着肚子干活！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I was hungry, okay?! That a good enough answer for you?! I can't just starve myself!

**阿尔古斯**：……饿了？我记得旅馆中有送餐服务。\
**Argus**: Hungry? If I remember correctly, the motel offers room service.

**阿尔古斯**：而旅馆每天会有一份免费的餐点——所以即使您没有钱，也可以维持基本的温饱。\
**Argus**: And you get one free meal a day, so even if you ain't got no money, you have enough food to get by.

**金伯利女郎**：你、你不懂——！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: What-what do you know?!

女房客有些气急败坏了。\
She looks flustered.

**金伯利女郎**：我怎么能吃那些东西……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I'm not eating one of those ham sandwiches.

**阿尔古斯**：好吧，您是一位对生活品质有所追求的小姐。\
**Argus**: Alright, so you've got some standards when it comes to food.

**阿尔古斯**：现在让我们回到正题，在他开枪前一刻，您也在场，对吗？那时发生了什么？\
**Argus**: Let's drop that. You were there when he fired the shot, right? What happened then?

**阿尔古斯**：不要慌张，您可以慢慢地讲述。\
**Argus**: Take your time and think it through. There's no rush.

**金伯利女郎**：……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...

一刻钟以前，史蒂文按响了我的门铃。\
About fifteen minutes ago, he rang my doorbell.

我以为是我的同伴从镇子上回来了，每次她一回来，就会带来一些好东西。于是我打开了门——谁能知道史蒂文挨了那样一顿打，还能这么快地出门。\
I thought my friend had returned from town. She always brings something amazing with her. So I opened the door. The last thing I expected was to see Stefen standing there—who'd have thought that he could get back on his feet so quickly after the beating he took?

看到他的脸之后，我吓坏了，用力地砸上门，原本以为他会放手。\
I was terrified when I saw him there. He towered over me, one hand on the doorframe and the other pushing against the door. I slammed the door shut. I thought he'd let go.

——但是他没有。\
But he didn't. The door closed on his fingers.

**史蒂文**：哈哈……我明白，我全都搞懂了！你就是芝诺派来的人，对不对！\
**Stefen**: Hahaha, I understand now. I understand it all! You're with Zeno, aren't you?!

他的手指因骨折而扭曲成奇异的角度，但他却对此毫不在意……就像骨折对于他而言，只是虱子的咬噬。\
His fingers were bent at a peculiar angle. It must've been painful, but he didn't seem to feel the pain at all. The fracturing of his fingers was no more painful than a mosquito bite to him.

**史蒂文**：所有的接近行为，最终的目的都只是为了拿我去换赏金……天哪，我真是搞不懂你们为什么要这么做。\
**Stefen**: You came to me and made me drop my guard so that one day you could turn me in for a bounty. But why me? Why are you doing this to me?!

**史蒂文**：提出计划的不是我，执行计划的人不是我，按下那个发射按钮的人……更不是我！\
**Stefen**: It wasn't me who made the plan. It wasn't me who executed it. It wasn't me who pressed that damn button!

**史蒂文**：我只是向世人揭露了这段罪行——你说，要不是心虚，他们为什么要发布这么多的通缉令呢？\
**Stefen**: All I did was expose their crime to the rest of the world. Tell me. Why else would they want my head so desperately if they didn't believe they were guilty?

**史蒂文**：那些杀人的人饱受赞誉，这不正常——而我原本应该是个英雄！却只能龟缩在这个肮脏的小旅馆里，这更不正常！\
**Stefen**: In the meantime, the actual killers are treated as heroes. But I'm the hero! Me! ME! But, but all my sorry ass gets is a lifetime of hiding out in some random motel in the middle of nowhere! This world is sick!

**金伯利女郎**：……天啊，你在说些什么？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: What the hell are you talking about?

**史蒂文**：得了吧，小姐，不要再装腔作势了。你一和我说话，维尔汀就来了——世界上哪里会有这么巧的事。\
**Stefen**: Come on. Drop the act. Right after you spoke to me, Vertin showed up at my door. Are you trying to tell me that that was just by chance?

**金伯利女郎**：维尔汀？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Vertin?

他没有理会我的疑问。\
He totally ignored my question.

**史蒂文**：这个世界生病了。\
**Stefen**: The world has fallen ill.

**史蒂文**：我想明白了……那天上的国是确实存在着的。要不然，我们的脑子里为何会拥有一个关于“完美的天国”的概念呢？\
**Stefen**: I can see that now. The, the realm above truly does exist. How else would we have gotten the idea of a perfect heavenly realm?

**史蒂文**：明明它不存在于现实世界里啊……\
**Stefen**: Obviously, it doesn't exist in this world.

**金伯利女郎**：别再发癔症了。就算那天上的国确实存在，和现在的你也没关系——你松手，我要关门了。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I don't care. Even if that place does exist, it has nothing to do with you. Get out of the way. I'm closing the door.

**史蒂文**：但至少，我可以决定在什么时候踏入那道窄门，对吗？\
**Stefen**: But at least I get to decide when I step through that door, right?

我不知道他在说什么。\
I had no idea what he was talking about.

而他也没有继续给我说话的机会。\
And he didn't give me much chance to figure it out, either.

**史蒂文**：小姐，恐怕你得带着“任务失败”的消息回去咯。\
**Stefen**: I'm afraid your mission is doomed to fail, young lady.

他在那一瞬间露出从未有过的释然笑容。\
In that moment, a smile of relief came over his face.

随后，他毫不犹豫地将手枪抵在了太阳穴上，扣下了扳机。\
Then, without a moment's hesitation, he pressed the pistol against his temple and pulled the trigger.

砰——！\
*bang*

**金伯利女郎**：……后来的事，你们都知道了。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: And you know the rest.

渐近的足音在这一刻停止，众人望向了声音的来源。\
The approaching footsteps stop abruptly. They turn to the source.

身着蓝灰色裙装的侍应生停在了众人的面前。望着眼前的尸体，她展露出恰到好处的惊讶。\
The maid stands before the group, showing just the right amount of surprise as her eyes fall upon the body.

**蓝手帕**：这儿刚刚发生了什么……？\
**Tuesday**: What's going on in here?

**阿尔古斯**：他自杀了，就是这么简单。\
**Argus**: This man killed himself.

**蓝手帕**：……您看看，他的血流了一地。\
**Tuesday**: Oh, dear. There's blood everywhere.

**蓝手帕**：这打扫起来会多么麻烦……天气又这样的热，也许残留的血迹和油脂很快就会发出腐败的臭味……\
**Tuesday**: It'll be a lot of work to clean it all up, and with the weather being so hot, the room will soon start to smell.

**蓝手帕**：我得把这些地毯全换了……\
**Tuesday**: All the carpets have to go.

侍应生发出一声长叹，语气中略带苦恼。\
The maid lets out a long sigh, her tone tinged with annoyance.

**维尔汀**：……蓝手帕小姐，有一个问题我想与您确认。\
**Vertin**: Ms. Tuesday, can I ask you a question?

**蓝手帕**：什么？\
**Tuesday**: Yes?

**维尔汀**：在您这里，是否有一些来自于重塑之手的客人？\
**Vertin**: Have you ever had any guests who looked like or claimed themselves to be Manus Vindictae?

**蓝手帕**：……重塑之手？\
**Tuesday**: Manus Vindictae?

她的面孔红润，似笑非笑地伫立着。\
Her face flushes as she smiles faintly.

**蓝手帕**：我不明白这些，您能替我讲讲吗？\
**Tuesday**: I'm not entirely sure what you mean. Could you explain in more detail?

**维尔汀**：他们总喜欢穿着蓝黑色的衣物，有部分信徒时常口角流涎，无法说出完整的语句。\
**Vertin**: Most of them dress in blue and black, some drool a fair bit, and most of them can't speak in full sentences.

**维尔汀**：最重要的特征是，他们总会戴着手状的面具——您见过吗？\
**Vertin**: The most notable feature is that they all wear masks shaped like hands. Have you seen any before?

**蓝手帕**：手状的面具……\
**Tuesday**: Masks shaped like hands ...

她像是开始了回忆。\
She taps her finger on her chin.

**蓝手帕**：我所接待的客人，没有一位曾经戴过手状的面具——他们也不曾穿着蓝黑色的衣物。\
**Tuesday**: No, I've never had a guest who wore a hand-shaped mask. Never seen anyone in blue and black, either.

**蓝手帕**：但如果一个组织要秘密地做些什么，我想他们也不会太过张扬。\
**Tuesday**: But if an organization was going to do something in secret, I don't think they'd be too public about it.

**阿尔古斯**：嘿，侍应生。\
**Argus**: Hey, lady.

雇佣兵毫不客气地打断了对话。\
Argus doesn't hesitate to interrupt the conversation.

**阿尔古斯**：告诉我这个男人住在哪儿。\
**Argus**: Take me to his room.

她的枪管指向史蒂文的尸体。\
She points the barrel of her gun at Stefen's corpse.

**蓝手帕**：您不是顶擅长这些追踪吗？阿尔古斯小姐。\
**Tuesday**: Oh, it shouldn't be too hard for you to find the room yourself, right, Ms. Argus? After all, that's how you make a living.

**蓝手帕**：我可以告诉您他的房间号码——214，您应该也想去那个房间。\
**Tuesday**: But I can just tell it to you. It's 214. You must be curious about that room.

**蓝手帕**：……我很惊讶，您竟然在短短的两天内，就快要查遍整座旅馆了……充沛的行动力，就像一个饱含好奇心的孩子。\
**Tuesday**: I'm surprised. You've been in almost every room in the motel, and you've been here for two days. You're like a child in your curiosity.

**蓝手帕**：……嗯，如果您是一位州际警察，我相信附近的治安会得到很大的改善。\
**Tuesday**: This place would be much safer if you were the sheriff here.

**蓝手帕**：……哈，祝愿您能找到那位小姑娘。\
**Tuesday**: Anyway, I hope you can find that girl soon.

血肉模糊的尸体近在眼前，而她垂下头，轻轻地掖了掖怀中的襁褓。\
Standing before the bloody corpse, she looks down and gently adjusts the baby in her arms.

## THH-09 丝与线 / Spider Silk

**维尔汀**：……为什么要去那个军官的房间？这和我们的目的有什么关系吗？\
**Vertin**: Why do you want to go to Stefen's room exactly? Is it related to our investigation?

**阿尔古斯**：当然有关系，老板。\
**Argus**: Of course, boss.

**阿尔古斯**：就像我在这儿寻找凯拉一样，您也在这儿寻找那位羊首人身的神秘……\
**Argus**: I'm here looking for Kayla, just as you're looking for that sheep-headed ...

雇佣兵罕见地陷入了沉默。\
She falls into an unusual silence.

**维尔汀**：怎么了？\
**Vertin**: What is it?

**阿尔古斯**：……您要找的那位神秘学家，她的名字是叫做数羊羔吗？\
**Argus**: That arcanist you're looking for, is her name Barbara?

**维尔汀**：——你知道她？\
**Vertin**: You know her?

**阿尔古斯**：……我见过她。\
**Argus**: Yup, we met.

**阿尔古斯**：就在77号公路的一侧。\
**Argus**: On Route 77.

**阿尔古斯**：我刚刚在两个男人嘴里问到了凯拉的下落，那时天已经快黑了。\
**Argus**: I'd just got done asking two men about Kayla's whereabouts, and saw that it was getting dark.

**阿尔古斯**：每到晚上，我的视线就会受到影响——这个季节，天又总是黑得很快。\
**Argus**: My sight ain't so good at night. And the nights are long these days.

**阿尔古斯**：我要赶紧发动车子，到达一个足够明亮的地方。\
**Argus**: So I was in a bit of a hurry, hoping to get somewhere with proper lights as fast as I could.

**阿尔古斯**：这时候，那个名叫数羊羔的神秘学家找上了我——司机把她丢在了公路边，她希望我能够带她一程。\
**Argus**: That's when I saw her, Barbara—all alone by the road. Some jerk of a driver dumped her there, and she asked me for a ride.

**阿尔古斯**：我拒绝了，因为我的眼睛已经快看不清了——这样疲惫的状态下，路上有大概率会出事。\
**Argus**: I turned her down. Heck, I could hardly see. She'd have been better off waiting for the next driver than riding with a blind bat like me, you know?

**阿尔古斯**：但在不久之后，我还是反悔了——那样小的一个孩子，怎么能让她一个人留在路边呢？\
**Argus**: But as I drove away, I changed my mind. She was too young to be left out there all by herself.

**阿尔古斯**：当我再次到达那个地方的时候，小东西已经不见了，地上只留下了一串小小的羊蹄印。\
**Argus**: So I turned back to get her. But when I arrived, she was already gone. There was nothing but a trail of hoofprints in the dirt.

**阿尔古斯**：后来，我也在旅馆里见到了一模一样的、形似羊蹄的脚印——她最后还是来到了这座旅馆，我很庆幸。\
**Argus**: When I got to the motel, I saw those hoofprints again. I gotta say, I was kinda relieved to see them. At least she made it here safely.

**维尔汀**：她现在还在这座旅馆中吗？\
**Vertin**: And is she still here?

**阿尔古斯**：当然，因为没有离去的脚印。\
**Argus**: Well, I've never seen any hoofprints leaving the motel.

**阿尔古斯**：不过，从结果去推导原因，无异于射出了箭再画靶子。痕迹只能作为一种辅助手段——这就是所有痕迹追踪的局限。\
**Argus**: But that don't mean she's still here. You gotta be mindful of what your mind picks up and what might slip you by. It's easy to ignore other evidence when what you've seen already fits your hypothesis.

**阿尔古斯**：但我依然认为她有很大的可能性在这座旅馆之中。\
**Argus**: That being said, it's still likely that she's somewhere in the motel.

**维尔汀**：……好，我和你一起找。\
**Vertin**: Alright. Then let's look for her.

**阿尔古斯**：很高兴与您达成了一致——下一个房间是214。\
**Argus**: It seems we're in agreement. To room 214.

**维尔汀**：202，203……\
**Vertin**: 202, 203 ...

沿着走廊，一扇一扇地数过门扉。\
She counts the doors as they walk down the hallway.

**维尔汀**：……嗯？\
**Vertin**: Mm?

恍惚间，有一抹红色自眼前闪过。\
Out of the corner of her eye, a flash of red catches her attention.

**阿尔古斯**：这两个房间我都查过了，没有相关的痕迹。\
**Argus**: I've checked those two. Ain't much in them.

**维尔汀**：……阿尔古斯，你有没有看到一扇红色的门扉？\
**Vertin**: Argus, did you see a red door just now?

**阿尔古斯**：红色的门扉？\
**Argus**: A red door?

**维尔汀**：……没什么，也许是我看错了。\
**Vertin**: Nothing. Must've been my imagination.

214号房间位于走廊的尽头，房门半阖着——房间的主人显然走得很匆忙。\
As they approach the end of the hallway, they spot room 214. The door is slightly ajar—clearly Stefen left in a hurry.

她们进入了史蒂文的房间，厚重的窗帘紧封着窗户。室内昏沉而寂静，房间里飘浮着一种醉酒后的酸臭味。\
They enter. The thick curtains are pulled shut, blocking out almost all the light from outside. They're hit with the stale, sour smell of old alcohol.

阿尔古斯眼中的辉光不断地闪烁着，如同接触不良的电路。\
The glow in Argus's eye flickers like a light with a faulty circuit.

**维尔汀**：你的眼睛还好吗？\
**Vertin**: Are you alright? Can you still see?

**阿尔古斯**：噢，不用担心，常有的事。\
**Argus**: Don't worry about it. Ain't the first time this has happened.

**阿尔古斯**：我们这一支的神秘学家都是这样，靠眼睛为生，自然会存在用眼过度的问题。\
**Argus**: This eye issue runs in the family. It's the price we pay for having our arcane power.

雇佣兵简单地环顾了四周，室内的凌乱令她微微皱起了眉毛。\
The mercenary glances around the room, a slight frown on her face.

**阿尔古斯**：老板，你想让我找什么？\
**Argus**: Now, what are we looking for, boss?

**阿尔古斯**：一个人留下的痕迹有很多种，如果像无头苍蝇一样没有方向，就什么都找不到。\
**Argus**: People leave all kinds of evidence behind all the time. It'll be like wandering around in the woods without a compass if we don't know what we're looking for.

**阿尔古斯**：如果不想被毫无意义的线索淹没，你得给我一个方向。\
**Argus**: So, if you don't wanna be inundated with meaningless clues, you need to give me some directions.

**维尔汀**：我希望能找到有关于数羊羔的线索。\
**Vertin**: Alright. First, I'd like to know what happened to Barbara.

**维尔汀**：还有……\
**Vertin**: Second ...

似是而非的线索在脑海中浮现。\
Fleeting images surface in her mind.

**维尔汀**：这里是否有重塑之手……或者是自称“启明会”的人来过，以及……\
**Vertin**: Whether Manus Vindictae has been here, or anyone from that Order of Enlightenment. And last ...

**维尔汀**：史蒂文先生使用的是飞矢M1903式手枪，并且知道我与“真空弹”的关系——他应该是一名来自于芝诺的军官，军衔应当不低。\
**Vertin**: About Mr. Stefen. The pistol he used was a Zeno military weapon, and he seemed to know about my relation to the vacuum bomb operation. It's likely that he once held a high rank within the Zeno military.

**维尔汀**：我想要知道，他为什么会来到这里，又为什么会在这里罹患癔症。\
**Vertin**: I want to know why he came to this motel and what happened to make him lose his mind here.

**阿尔古斯**：在这里患上癔症？老板，或许他原本就是个精神病人呢？\
**Argus**: "Lose his mind here"? What makes you think he wasn't crazy already?

**维尔汀**：……实际上，相较于人类的军事机构，芝诺会更加重视军士的精神问题。\
**Vertin**: Zeno pays much more attention to its soldiers' mental well-being than any conventional military organization.

**维尔汀**：——毕竟有相当一部分的军士有着神秘学家的血统，这既是超凡的根源，也是不稳定的因素。\
**Vertin**: It's because quite a few of them are arcanists. They're both Zeno's strength and weakness.

**维尔汀**：所以，我更倾向于认为，史蒂文先生是在进入旅馆之后，才患上了癔症。\
**Vertin**: So I'm inclined to think Mr. Stefen developed these mental health issues after entering the motel.

**阿尔古斯**：行吧，我得承认我不了解这些军事机构。\
**Argus**: Huh, is that so? I gotta say, I don't know much about all this military institution stuff.

**阿尔古斯**：一，搜寻数羊羔的下落；二，是否有重塑之手，或者启明会的人来过；三，史蒂文是如何来到这里，又如何罹患病症……\
**Argus**: Right, so here's the plan: first, locate Barbara; second, look for any signs of Manus Vindictae or the Order of Enlightenment; and third, find out how poor old Stefen lost his marbles.

**阿尔古斯**：当然，还有一件我自己的事……找到凯拉的下落。\
**Argus**: And, of course, I've got my own business to deal with—tracking down Kayla.

雇佣兵开始对室内的痕迹进行逐一排查。\
She starts to meticulously search the room.

**阿尔古斯**：噢，老板，有新发现。\
**Argus**: Hey, boss! I've got something.

一道明晰的行迹，嵌于灰尘之中。\
There's a series of small but clear traces imprinted in the dust.

**阿尔古斯**：这是蜘蛛的足迹，它来回地徘徊于一侧，对于当下的情景来说没什么价值，但也是个异常的线索——您觉得，蜘蛛会打电话吗？\
**Argus**: These footprints are from a spider. Looks like the little guy went back and forth along here quite a few times. I know this might not seem pertinent to our investigation, but it is worth noting. You ever seen a spider make a phone call?

**维尔汀**：……阿尔古斯，我现在并不想了解蜘蛛的习性。\
**Vertin**: I'm afraid I'm not interested in the movements of spiders right now.

雇佣兵耸了耸肩。\
Argus shrugs.

**阿尔古斯**：好吧，老板——你看起来有些过于紧张了。\
**Argus**: Come on, boss, loosen up a little.

滴答，滴答……\
*drip-drip*

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

回荡的水滴声在不远处响起。\
The sound of dripping water echoes nearby.

**维尔汀**：你听到了响声吗？\
**Vertin**: Do you hear that? Sounds like dripping water.

滴答，滴答，滴答……\
*drip-drip-drip*

伴随着水滴的声响，一片洇湿的水渍正于墙纸上扩散。\
With every drip, a water stain grows larger and larger on the wallpaper.

**阿尔古斯**：只是水而已，这家旅馆的管道系统就是这样，不是什么值得惊讶的事。\
**Argus**: I'm sure it's just the motel plumbing.

**维尔汀**：可是……\
**Vertin**: But ...

墙上的水渍逐渐洇成了手掌的形状，五指俱全。\
The stain gradually takes the form of a hand, its five fingers all clearly defined.

**维尔汀**：——小心！\
**Vertin**: Watch out!

那只手掌赫然地拍了下来——\
Suddenly, the hand pulls itself from the wall and slams down.

**维尔汀**：……这座旅馆没有那么简单。\
**Vertin**: This place is definitely more than meets the eye.

**阿尔古斯**：实际上我在之前也发现了这一点……\
**Argus**: I'm with you on that.

**阿尔古斯**：这儿有着过于浓厚的神秘学氛围，我从来没有在别的旅馆中看到过这样多的术阵。\
**Argus**: There's just too much arcanum-related weirdness going on here. Never seen so many arrays in a motel before.

**维尔汀**：……可是我们只看到了一个术阵。\
**Vertin**: But we've only found one.

**阿尔古斯**：那只是您的房间。\
**Argus**: In your room, yeah.

**阿尔古斯**：在其他房间中，术阵并不少见……最多的一间房，它从地板到天花板，都刻满了密密麻麻的术阵。\
**Argus**: But there are a load more. One room has them drawn from floor to ceiling.

**阿尔古斯**：看起来像是……转化方面的用途？我并不了解术阵，也不清楚它们的用途。\
**Argus**: Looked like some kinda transformation array to me. I ain't no expert, so, I can't say for sure.

**维尔汀**：……他们想要获得什么？\
**Vertin**: What are they trying to do, I wonder?

**阿尔古斯**：谁知道呢。\
**Argus**: Who knows.

雇佣兵简单地结束了对话，随即继续开始对房间的探查。\
She brings the conversation to an abrupt end and continues searching the room.

**阿尔古斯**：噢，老板，你可能对这个感兴趣。\
**Argus**: Oh, boss, you might be interested in this.

雇佣兵望向了床底。\
She peers under the bed.

**阿尔古斯**：就是这样的图案。\
**Argus**: It's another one. Just like the others.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

一个巨大的术阵横卧于眼前，周围散落着一些暗色的结晶。\
A huge array lies beneath the bed. It's scattered with dark crystals.

似曾相识的图案。\
The design is familiar.

**维尔汀**：我看过这个，就在那本羊皮手册上……\
**Vertin**: I've seen this before. It was also drawn in that parchment notebook.

**维尔汀**：这的确是一个有关于转化的术阵……但它残破不堪。\
**Vertin**: This is indeed a transformation array. But it's not in its full form.

**阿尔古斯**：他们在尝试什么东西，您瞧。\
**Argus**: They were trying something. Check it out.

雇佣兵捻起了旁边的一根毛发。\
She plucks a hair from the carpet.

**阿尔古斯**：这是吼狮的鬃毛……旁边还有许多神秘学的材料，但它们被磨得太细碎，我无法判断具体是什么。\
**Argus**: This is hair from the mane of a howler lion, and there are some other materials around it, too. Not exactly sure what they are, though. They're too finely ground.

**阿尔古斯**：但毋庸置疑的一点是——有人在这里进行某种神秘学仪式，不知道出于什么原因，仪式并未成功。\
**Argus**: But one thing's for sure: Someone held a ceremony here, and for some reason, it didn't work out for them.

**维尔汀**：这很重要……得及时上报基金会。\
**Vertin**: This is important. The Foundation needs to know about this.

空气中一片寂静。\
The air is silent.

**维尔汀**：……阿尔古斯？\
**Vertin**: Argus?

雇佣兵并未对这声呼唤作出反应，她正紧盯着自己的掌心——其上有一根栗色的发丝。\
The mercenary doesn't respond. She's still staring at the strand of hair between her fingers. It's chestnut colored.

**阿尔古斯**：还有凯拉的头发，她来过这儿！\
**Argus**: This is Kayla's hair. She was here! In this room!

**阿尔古斯**：……至少，有一位和她打过交道的人，来过这儿。\
**Argus**: Or at least someone who came into contact with her.

还未等雇佣兵说得更多，房间里的电话忽然急促地响了起来。\
The phone rings, cutting her off.

**电话**：叮铃铃铃铃铃——

## THH-10 嘿，万圣节！ / It's Spooky Time!

辽阔的远郊，有人在野地里弹起了吉他，哼起了二部曲式的调子。\
A man lies in the grass just outside of town. He's strumming a guitar and humming to himself.

**士兵**：哦，这样美丽且悠闲的夜晚，最适合在微醺之后，坐在原野之上吹风……如果能就此睡到明天……\
**Zeno Soldier**: Ah, this is the life. A warm, beautiful night, a cold drink, and no one but me and the stars in the sky. Eh, maybe I'll just lie here till morning.

年轻的芝诺士兵醉眼迷蒙地躺在镇外的原野上，他对着闪烁的星空，高高地举起了手中的酒壶。\
It's a young Zeno soldier, his eyes hazy from intoxication. He raises his flask to the twinkling stars above.

**士兵**：多么好的酒，多么美妙的夜晚！噢，如果每天都能这样……\
**Zeno Soldier**: A good night with good drinks! I wish every day could be like this.

一片人形的阴影笼罩在他的脸上——士兵虚焦的眼睛并不能分辨出那是谁。\
A dark figure looms over him, but in his blurred vision, he can't make out who it is.

**士兵**：嘿，你挡住我看星星了。\
**Zeno Soldier**: Hey, buddy, you're blocking my view.

**红弩箭**：哈……看星星？\
**Lilya**: Huh? Are you stargazing?

听到了熟悉的声音，士兵眨了眨眼睛。\
The soldier blinks. He knows that voice.

**士兵**：……唔，小姐，有没有人和你说过……你的声音很像红弩箭中尉？\
**Zeno Soldier**: Has anyone ever told you that you sound awfully like Lieutenant Lilya?

**士兵**：就是那个驾驶着红色38的飞行女巫……你应该认得她吧？没有人能做出比她更好的飞行了。\
**Zeno Soldier**: The rider of Red 38. Heard of her? No one can fly like her.

**红弩箭**：当然。\
**Lilya**: Of course.

士兵勉强聚焦了视线，一张似曾相识的脸庞出现在了他的面前。\
The soldier concentrates, getting the figure's face a little more into focus.

**士兵**：天哪——您就连长相都和中尉相似……\
**Zeno Soldier**: Oh, my! You even look like her.

**红弩箭**：你如果再装疯卖傻，我就会让你知道红弩箭揍起人来是什么样子。\
**Lilya**: Keep playing dumb, and I'll show you what it's like to have her kick your ass.

因酒醉而迟缓的眼睛终于在这一刻对上了焦，一张满是不爽的面孔赫然现于眼前。\
The soldier's drunken eyes finally focus to see Lilya herself, a look of displeasure on her face.

**士兵**：——！\
**Zeno Soldier**: ...!

年轻的士兵手忙脚乱地扔下了酒壶。\
He stumbles to his feet, dropping the flask in his hand on the way up.

他试图用无力的手行个标准的军礼，但虚浮的步伐使他险些摔了一个倒栽葱。\
He tries to salute, but almost falls flat on his face in the attempt.

**士兵**：红弩箭中尉，一等列兵安德烈向您致敬！\
**Zeno Soldier**: Lieutenant Lilya! Airman First Class Andreas at your service!

所幸，他最后还是完成了那个七倒八歪的军礼。\
Luckily, he manages to complete the wobbly salute.

**红弩箭**：你就是那个看守军备工厂的人？\
**Lilya**: Are you the warehouse guard?

飞行员充满怀疑的目光在士兵的身上游移。\
She looks at the soldier doubtfully.

**士兵**：是的！红弩箭中尉！\
**Zeno Soldier**: Yes, ma'am!

**红弩箭**：……\
**Lilya**: ...

很少有人会如此兴奋地承认自己的渎职，某种程度上，他的确拥有出类拔萃的勇气。\
Few would so eagerly admit to the dereliction of their duties. In a way, he possesses exceptional courage.

**红弩箭**：那么，现在到你干活的时候了——我的红色38被寄到了这儿的军备工厂，我需要你帮我解开包裹上附着的重力术式。\
**Lilya**: On your feet, soldier. My Red 38 is in your warehouse for maintenance, and I need you to remove the gravity ritual from it.

**士兵**：……重力术式？\
**Zeno Soldier**: Gravity ritual?

**红弩箭**：如果你不明白我在说什么，就去找负责人过来——我必须得在今天拿到红色38。\
**Lilya**: If you don't understand what I'm saying, go get someone who does. I need it today.

他被酒精麻痹的神经滞涩地转动着。在飞行员即将爆发的前一刻，士兵终于露出了恍然大悟的表情。\
The soldier ponders, slowed by his inebriation. Just as Lilya is about to lose her patience, the soldier's eyes light up.

**士兵**：……噢，重力术式！\
**Zeno Soldier**: Oh, right, the gravity ritual!

**士兵**：我知道您在说什么了，请和我一起去军备工厂吧！\
**Zeno Soldier**: Yes, yes, I know! Please, come with me. I'll take you to the warehouse!

**红弩箭**：……你真的能解开那个术式吗？\
**Lilya**: Are you certain you can undo the ritual?

**士兵**：当然！军官们在撤离之前，特地培训了我好几次——您就放心吧！\
**Zeno Soldier**: Yes, ma'am! They made sure I got the hang of it before they took off. Leave it to me!

**红弩箭**：带路吧，士兵。\
**Lilya**: Lead the way, soldier.

他们再次来到了那个工厂，巨大的木箱横亘于二人的面前。\
They stand side by side in the factory, the wooden crate before them.

**红弩箭**：打开它。\
**Lilya**: Open it.

**士兵**：噢——这个包裹。\
**Zeno Soldier**: Oh, I remember this package.

**士兵**：我拿到的时候，还以为是什么玩笑，或者是同名的军士——谁也想不到，您居然会到德克萨斯来！\
**Zeno Soldier**: I thought it was some kind of joke, or someone with the same name as you sent the package. Who would've thought that you'd come to Texas yourself?

他喋喋不休地说着，飞行员的耐心正在飞速下滑。\
He rambles on. Lilya's patience is coming to an end.

**红弩箭**：士兵，我没空和你废话。\
**Lilya**: Hurry it up, soldier.

**红弩箭**：打开它，现在。\
**Lilya**: Open the crate. Now.

**士兵**：嗯，中尉，我理解您的心情，但是……嗝。\
**Zeno Soldier**: Ma'am, I know you want to do this quick, but ... *burp*

**士兵**：我没有解开这个术式的权限。\
**Zeno Soldier**: I haven't been authorized to undo this incantation.

**红弩箭**：如果你不能解决这个问题，那就找能解决的人来——不要让我重复第三次。\
**Lilya**: If you can't do it, find me someone who can. I won't say it a third time.

**士兵**：实话告诉您，除了我以外，您找不到别的人了。现在驻守在军备工厂的人，只剩下我了——\
**Zeno Soldier**: Truth be told, there's no one else to turn to. I'm the only one left.

**士兵**：为了让我干这活，他们还特地给我升了军衔——现在，我是个一等列兵了！\
**Zeno Soldier**: I was made an Airman First Class to do this job. I was still in training before this, you see.

他骄傲地拍了拍胸口。\
He proudly pats his chest.

**士兵**：其他人要么接到了调令，回到了总部，要么就离开了这里……\
**Zeno Soldier**: The others were either transferred back to headquarters or just left.

**士兵**：我也不知道他们去了哪里。\
**Zeno Soldier**: I don't know where they are now.

**士兵**：不过，他们把这么重要的任务交给我，我相信以后一定还有更好的未来在等着我……\
**Zeno Soldier**: But since they entrusted me with such an important task, I'm sure I have a bright future ahead of me.

在士兵连篇累牍的废话之下，飞行员的耐心正式宣布告罄。\
Lilya's patience has officially run out.

**红弩箭**：士兵，你只是没有解开术式的权限，而并不是没有解开术式的能力，对吗？\
**Lilya**: You just said you aren't authorized, not that you don't have the ability, right?

**红弩箭**：我现在给你两个选择。\
**Lilya**: I have two options for you.

**红弩箭**：第一，现在帮我解开术式。\
**Lilya**: One, remove the ritual now.

**红弩箭**：第二，被我狠狠揍一顿后，解开这个术式。\
**Lilya**: Or, two, I beat your ass, and then you remove the ritual.

**士兵**：其实……\
**Zeno Soldier**: Well ...

**红弩箭**：别废话。\
**Lilya**: Choose. No more gibbering.

她晃了晃自己的拳头。\
She readies her fist.

**士兵**：……我选第二个。\
**Zeno Soldier**: I pick the second one.

**红弩箭**：……？\
**Lilya**: Huh?

她发自内心地困惑了。\
She is genuinely confused.

**士兵**：哈哈……嗝，我可以帮您解开术式，但是这个行为不能是我主动、自愿发起的……\
**Zeno Soldier**: Haha. *burp* You see, I'm happy to get rid of the ritual for you, but I can't do it on my own initiative.

**士兵**：因为我现在还只是一个一等列兵……\
**Zeno Soldier**: I'm only an Airman First Class. I can't make decisions about this stuff.

**士兵**：所以，您的确得揍我一顿……以避免后续的审查——\
**Zeno Soldier**: So, you have to beat me up to avoid future inquiries.

**士兵**：不过——！等我以后得到了更高的军衔，我就能更好地帮助您了！红弩箭中尉！\
**Zeno Soldier**: One day, after I'm promoted, I'll be able to better assist you, ma'am!

**士兵**：您的飞行真是太棒了，我还特意做了剪报，贴在了我的……\
**Zeno Soldier**: I mean, you're the best pilot I've ever seen! I even made a scrapbook of the reports on your flights.

话音未落，他的右脸颊已重重地挨了一拳。\
Before he can finish what he's saying, Lilya has already clocked him.

**红弩箭**：放心，我会掌握分寸的。\
**Lilya**: Alright, no screaming, soldier. Let's do this.

显然，疼痛有助于醒酒。\
Each hit seems to clear his head a little more.

当士兵的面孔无限地接近于猪头的时候，他的脑子忽然地清醒了。\
By the time his face is completely swollen, he has snapped back to reality.

**士兵**：慢着……我相信这已经达到了他们的标准！\
**Zeno Soldier**: Stop! Stop! This is plenty to prove my innocence!

**士兵**：现在，我来帮您解开这个术式。\
**Zeno Soldier**: I'll undo the ritual now.

他蹲下了身，在木箱的周围进行了相应的动作——辉光流溢，木箱被打开了。\
He squats down and performs the necessary movements around the crate. There's a flash of light, and the crate opens.

**红弩箭**：这亮得像个闪光弹。\
**Lilya**: Oof. You almost blinded me there.

她迫不及待地拿起了红色38，金属冰凉的触感一如既往。\
She eagerly grabs the Red 38 and feels the familiar touch of the cold metal in her palm.

**红弩箭**：——谢了，一等列兵。\
**Lilya**: Thanks, soldier.

**红弩箭**：在走之前，有一件事情需要再向你确认。\
**Lilya**: There's one more thing.

**士兵**：请说，中尉！\
**Zeno Soldier**: Yes, ma'am!

**红弩箭**：这儿的人为什么全部撤离了？\
**Lilya**: Do you know why Zeno pulled out of here so suddenly?

**士兵**：唔……\
**Zeno Soldier**: Hmm.

他眯起了眼睛，开始回忆。\
He squints, trying to remember.

**士兵**：听说是“上面”的指示。\
**Zeno Soldier**: They said it was an order from "the top."

**红弩箭**：“上面”？\
**Lilya**: "The top"?

**士兵**：这就不是我能知道的了……据说是那个轰炸视频被泄露，伊戈尔上将发了大火——有人说和这件事有关。\
**Zeno Soldier**: That's all I was told. But word is, it was because Admiral Igor got real mad about the video leak of the vacuum bomb.

**士兵**：但这也只是传言。大部队还是撤离了，人少了以后，这儿逐渐变得奇怪……\
**Zeno Soldier**: But that's just a rumor. Ever since the evacuation, strange things have started to happen.

**红弩箭**：怎样的奇怪？\
**Lilya**: Such as?

**士兵**：最开始只是几个外乡人前来传教，说是一个名叫“启明会”的新兴密教……\
**Zeno Soldier**: We started getting visitors from this group called the Order of Enlightenment.

**士兵**：农民们不再去耕种田地，牧民也不再放牧牛羊。他们每日参加各种集会，期盼“受苦者”能够给予永恒的安乐。\
**Zeno Soldier**: And now, the farmers have stopped tending their fields. The cattle and sheep have been abandoned in the wilderness. All the townsfolk do now is go to these gatherings, hoping that the Sufferer will bring them eternal joy.

**士兵**：我不知道“受苦者”是谁，但想来应该不是一个好人。\
**Zeno Soldier**: I don't know who this Sufferer is, but he ain't doing any good here.

**红弩箭**：那些人驻扎在哪里？镇子的中心吗？\
**Lilya**: Where do those people stay? In the town?

**士兵**：嗯……并不是在镇子里，离这儿有些距离，好像是……\
**Zeno Soldier**: Mm. It's a ways away, I think.

士兵费力地回想着。\
The soldier struggles to recall.

**士兵**：……是一个叫做蓝手帕旅馆的地方。\
**Zeno Soldier**: A place called Tuesday's Motel.

**红弩箭**：该死的！维尔汀有危险——我得回去找她！\
**Lilya**: Damn! Vertin! I have to go back!

流线型的金属机身泛着微微的凉意，一切都一如往昔。\
She clasps the Red 38 with both hands, the cool grooves of the metal settling into her grasp.

**红弩箭**：好伙计，得出发了。\
**Lilya**: Let's get out of here, girl!

说着，她以一个胜利者的姿态，骑上了红色38。\
With a victorious stance, she mounts the Red 38.

银白色的光芒划出一道弧线，如同一枚贴地飞行的流星。飞行员驾驶它离开了工厂，随后消失在了漆黑的天幕中。\
A silver light traces an arc in the sky as the pilot leaves the factory and disappears into the night.

**士兵**：中尉，请小心——\
**Zeno Soldier**: Safe travels, ma'am!

年轻的士兵在她的身后遥遥呼喊，那声音很快被夜色吞没。\
The young soldier calls out after her, his voice soon swallowed by the night.

短途飞行对她而言并非难事。\
Short-distance flights are no challenge for Lilya.

在黑夜中，远处亮起的灯牌显得尤为清晰。远处树影憧憧，如同佝偻着的人形。\
She lands near the motel, guided by its glowing sign. The shadows of the trees around it look like hunched human figures.

**红弩箭**：蓝手帕旅馆。\
**Lilya**: Tuesday's Motel.

飞行员锁定了目标，准备向前走去，忽然有什么东西，在后面轻轻地拍了拍她的肩膀。\
She locks onto her destination and is about to proceed when she feels something tap her on the shoulder from behind.

**？？？**：您好，请问可以搭便车吗？\
**???**: Hello, can you give me a ride?

**红弩箭**：我载不了你，找别人吧。\
**Lilya**: I can't help you. Ask someone else.

**？？？**：……我可以搭便车吗？\
**???**: Can you give me a ride?

**红弩箭**：——我说了，我载不了你！\
**Lilya**: I said I can't help you!

重复的问题让飞行员不耐烦了起来，她转过头，却当场愣在了原地。\
The repeated questions are getting on her nerves. She swivels around, ready to give the questioner a piece of her mind, but freezes on the spot.

面前的人——她应当是一个姑娘，穿着数年前流行的裙子，整张脸却像水泥一样被抹平了。\
There's a girl wearing an out-dated outfit. Her face has no discernible features, like it's been smoothed over with cement.

**？？？**：噢……那您可以给我一块儿巧克力吗？\
**???**: Oh, can I have some chocolate?

无脸的女孩展示着一张糖果的包装纸。\
The faceless girl holds out a candy wrapper.

**？？？**：不久前，我遇到了一位好心人……他请我吃了一颗巧克力，我从来没有吃过这样美味的糖果……\
**???**: I met a kind man who gave me some chocolate. I've never tasted anything so sweet.

**红弩箭**：见鬼了！你离我远点！\
**Lilya**: The hell—stay away from me!

**？？？**：给我，给我……把那颗糖果……给我……我要更多……\
**???**: Can I? Can I have that candy? More. I want more.

无脸的女孩忽然裂开了嘴，露出了口中如同剃刀一样锋利的牙齿。\
She opens her mouth wide, revealing a row of razorsharp teeth.

**红弩箭**：*的，别找我要糖了，我可不想过万圣节！\
**Lilya**: Stop asking me for candy. This isn't Halloween, idiot!

**红弩箭**：呼……呼……\
**Lilya**: *pant*

**蓝手帕**：……嘿。\
**Tuesday**: Hey.

**红弩箭**：——！\
**Lilya**: ...!

飞行员在看清了来人的面孔之后，骤然放松了蓄势待发的拳头。\
The pilot relaxes her poised fists when she recognizes the person in front of her.

**红弩箭**：原来是你。\
**Lilya**: It's you.

**蓝手帕**：您刚刚是看见什么了吗？脸色这样的白。\
**Tuesday**: Are you alright? You look pale.

**红弩箭**：……不要在别人的背后突然出声，我有时会来不及收手。\
**Lilya**: You shouldn't sneak up on people like that. I could've hurt you.

**蓝手帕**：噢，抱歉……不过，既然已经到了旅馆，您现在可以不必这么紧绷着了。\
**Tuesday**: My apologies. But you're safe now that you're at the motel. No need to be frightened.

## THH-11 “请勿打扰” / "Please Do Not Disturb"

雇佣兵按下了免提键。\
Argus presses the speaker button on the telephone.

电话彼端传来熟悉的敲击声。\
A familiar tapping sound comes from the other end of the line.

**电话**：哒，哒，哒，哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap, tap, tap, tap*

**电话**：哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap*

**电话**：哒，哒——哒，哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap, tap—tap, tap*

**电话**：哒，哒——哒——哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap, tap—tap—tap*

**维尔汀**：求救。\
**Vertin**: HELP.

**电话**：哒——哒，哒。\
**Telephone**: *tap—tap, tap*

**电话**：哒，哒——\
**Telephone**: *tap, tap—*

**维尔汀**：Baa……羊的叫声？\
**Vertin**: BAA. Is that the sound of a sheep?

**阿尔古斯**：老板，你听出来了吗？\
**Argus**: You noticed it, too, huh?

**阿尔古斯**：这的确不是人打出来的电话——而是某种动物，或是昆虫。\
**Argus**: Ain't no way that's a human on the other end. It's gotta be some kind of animal.

**维尔汀**：……动物或昆虫？\
**Vertin**: Animal?

**阿尔古斯**：根据电话座机上爬行的声音，以及灰尘中的足迹——我想它的体型不会太大。\
**Argus**: Based on those sounds and the tracks in the dust, I figure it's something small like a—

雇佣兵忽然停止了说话。\
She stops.

**阿尔古斯**：稍等，老板。\
**Argus**: One sec, boss.

雇佣兵从口袋中摸出了一些东西，塞入了嘴中。\
She fishes something out of her pocket and pops it into her mouth.

**维尔汀**：苦目糖？\
**Vertin**: Picrasma candy?

**维尔汀**：如果使用神秘术已经让你感到负担，我们可以暂时休息一下。\
**Vertin**: Using your arcane skill so frequently must be tiring. You should take a break.

**阿尔古斯**：任务还没完成——远远没到休息的时候呢。\
**Argus**: The job ain't done yet. Far too early to rest.

**阿尔古斯**：不用担心，老板，这是代代相传的病症，从老阿尔古斯到小阿尔古斯，没有一个人能够逃脱。\
**Argus**: Don't worry, boss. It's just a condition that runs in my family, no biggie.

**维尔汀**：它的副作用是什么？\
**Vertin**: What are its side effects?

**阿尔古斯**：哈，老板，让一个雇佣兵把自己的弱点告诉你……我们还没有熟到这种地步吧？\
**Argus**: Ha, boss. You expect a merc to reveal her weakness? We ain't that close yet.

**阿尔古斯**：不过，可以告诉您的是，只要眼睛还在使用，这些副作用就会如影随形——所幸如今的科技足够发达，您瞧瞧。\
**Argus**: One thing I can tell you, though, is that I suffer the side effects as long as my eyes are open. Luckily, I've got cutting-edge technology at my disposal.

她展示了手中的糖块。\
She holds up the candy between her fingers.

**阿尔古斯**：安全、高效——最重要的是，很甜。\
**Argus**: They're safe, efficient, and, most importantly, satisfy my sweet tooth.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：它不是糖，而是一种药剂——它应当在合乎医嘱的情况下使用，这一点你应该比我更清楚。\
**Vertin**: They may be called candy, but they're actually medicine and ought to be used following medical instructions. You should know that.

**阿尔古斯**：得了吧，老板，危险可不会在医生的预料之内发生。\
**Argus**: Gimme a break, boss. What do doctors know about my life?

**阿尔古斯**：它作为药剂，很合理地发挥了身为药剂的作用，一次次地救人们于险境，这还不够吗？\
**Argus**: I use these candies whenever I need them. Ain't that the whole point?

**维尔汀**：可是……\
**Vertin**: But ...

她还想再说些什么，但雇佣兵却示意她噤声。\
Argus motions for her to be quiet.

**阿尔古斯**：嘘——你听见了吗？\
**Argus**: Shh! Did you hear that?

**维尔汀**：……什么？\
**Vertin**: Hear what?

雇佣兵将话音放得很轻。\
Argus lowers her voice.

**阿尔古斯**：是心跳。门外，有人在偷听。\
**Argus**: A heartbeat, right outside the door. Someone's eavesdropping on us.

咚、咚、咚。\
Thump, thump, thump.

雇佣兵悄无声息地蹲下了身。\
She crouches down.

咚咚、咚咚、咚咚……\
Thump, thump, thump …

子弹被塞入枪中，发出了轻微的响声。\
With a faint clink, she loads her shotgun.

咚咚咚咚咚咚咚咚咚咚……\
Thump, thump, thump, thump, thump …

雇佣兵一把拧开了门把手。\
Then she swiftly turns the door handle.

**？？？**：——！\
**???**: *gasp*

偷听的女孩儿差点随着敞开的门跌滚进来。\
The eavesdropping girl nearly falls forward into the room as the door swings open.

**阿尔古斯**：也许你需要花点时间解释——你为什么会在这里，金伯利女郎？\
**Argus**: Care to explain why you're here, Ms. Kimberly?

**阿尔古斯**：对你而言，这位史蒂文先生真的有这么大的魅力吗？即使在他已经死了之后？\
**Argus**: Just how obsessed are you with Mr. Stefen, huh? Even now, after his death?

**金伯利女郎**：啊……不，不是的！我只是在找我的玩具……它只是恰好，可能在……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Oh, n-no, it's not what you think! I was just looking for my toy, and it just so happens—

**阿尔古斯**：玩具？\
**Argus**: Toy?

**阿尔古斯**：我不希望把枪口对准手无寸铁的人。但有时这种行为是很有必要的——因为人总是不见棺材不落泪。\
**Argus**: You know, it ain't my style to point a gun at an unarmed person, but sometimes you gotta do what you gotta do. Especially when they're speaking with a forked tongue.

**阿尔古斯**：五。\
**Argus**: Five.

**金伯利女郎**：我说了，我就是在找东西……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I told you, I was just looking for something.

**阿尔古斯**：四。\
**Argus**: Four.

**金伯利女郎**：……天啊！你为什么不肯信我！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Are you joking?! Why won't you believe me?!

女房客急切地跺起了脚，地板咚咚地震颤着。\
She stomps her feet anxiously, making the floor tremble a little.

**阿尔古斯**：三。\
**Argus**: Three.

**金伯利女郎**：我、我没有……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I-I didn't ...

她闭上了眼睛，像是下定了决心。\
She closes her eyes as if she has made a decision.

**阿尔古斯**：二。\
**Argus**: Two.

**金伯利女郎**：……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...

**阿尔古斯**：一。\
**Argus**: One.

雇佣兵毫不犹豫地扣下了扳机。\
She pulls the trigger.

巨大的响声在耳边炸开，金伯利的面孔一瞬间褪去了血色，她蜷缩起来，竭力让自己变成一个更小的东西。\
The bullet flies past Ms. Kimberly's ear. Her face turns pale. She curls up, desperately trying to make herself smaller.

**金伯利女郎**：不要杀我，不要杀我……我什么都没有做……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Don't kill me. D-Don't kill me, please. I didn't do anything.

她的手指不受控制地颤抖着，黑色的趾爪从指尖伸出。\
Her fingers tremble uncontrollably as black claws extend from her fingertips.

**金伯利女郎**：——！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: —!

她惊讶地望着自己漆黑而锐利的指尖，急忙将它揣进怀里——随后惴惴不安地望向二人。\
She looks at the claws in shock, quickly tucking them into her chest, then looks nervously at the two of them.

**维尔汀**：……在玛蒂尔达传回的报告中，也出现过“金伯利”这个名字。\
**Vertin**: I saw the name "Kimberly" in Matilda's report.

**维尔汀**：我原本以为只是巧合。\
**Vertin**: I'd thought it was just a coincidence. But now I realize it wasn't.

**维尔汀**：——你就是那位隶属于重塑之手的成员，金伯利女郎，对吗？\
**Vertin**: Ms. Kimberly, you're a member of Manus Vindictae, aren't you?

**金伯利女郎**：我、我真的什么都没有做……那帮穿黑衣服的人只是告诉我，要我和一个同伴一起行动……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I swear, I didn't do anything wrong! All I did was follow my partner like the people in black told me to.

**维尔汀**：告诉我，那个同伴是谁？\
**Vertin**: Who's your partner?

**金伯利女郎**：……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...

**金伯利女郎**：我饿了，我一直很饿……我好羡慕你们，只要把食物储存起来，你们就可以在很长的一段时间里填饱肚子……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I'm hungry all the time, so hungry. Oh, how I envy the likes of you. You can store your food in so many ways.

**金伯利女郎**：木桶可以储存面包和水，谷仓可以储存粮食，牧场里则是正在奔跑的肉类和奶制品……而我的粮食却……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: You have enough bread and water in your barns to last an entire winter, and your pastures are full of meat and dairy products. But my food ...

**金伯利女郎**：我保证，我只是想快点找到我的失物……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I promise, all I'm trying to do is get back what I lost.

**维尔汀**：别害怕，我们不会伤害你……只要你把那个名字告诉我。\
**Vertin**: There's no need to be afraid. We won't hurt you, as long as you tell me the name of your partner.

女郎转了转眼珠。\
Ms. Kimberly's eyes dart around.

**金伯利女郎**：如果我把她的名字告诉你，那你是不是会放我一马？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Um. If I tell you her name, will you let me go?

**阿尔古斯**：看你诚意咯。\
**Argus**: That depends on your sincerity.

**金伯利女郎**：她……叫淑女格蕾丝……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Sh-She's called Ms. Grace.

**维尔汀**：你们来这里的目的是什么？\
**Vertin**: What's your purpose here?

**金伯利女郎**：我当然不知道！那群穿黑衣服的家伙只是让我听格蕾丝的话……但来到这里以后，她也没让我做过什么事儿……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I don't know! Those people in black told me to follow Ms. Grace's orders, but she hasn't asked me to do anything since we got here.

**金伯利女郎**：那个小气鬼，肯定是背着我在做什么——不过我不在乎！我只想吃饭！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: She must be hiding something from me, but I couldn't care less! I just want to eat!

女郎言辞恳切，另一只手却从口袋里掏出了什么。\
She speaks earnestly, but her other hand pulls something out of her pocket.

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

**金伯利女郎**：嘿嘿。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Heh heh.

女郎露出了狡黠的笑容，抬手捏爆了手中的道具，漆黑的烟雾四处蔓延。\
She gives a sly smile and crushes the item in her hand, releasing a veil of thick black smoke.

**金伯利女郎**：讨厌鬼，你们连我的衣角都抓不住！还想抓住我呢，做白日梦！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: You annoying little brats can catch me in your dreams!

**维尔汀**：是传送仪式——阿尔古斯，帮帮我！不能让她逃走！\
**Vertin**: She's casting a teleport ritual. Argus, your assistance! We can't let her get away!

砰——\
*bang*

随着一阵散开的烟雾，金伯利女郎消失了。\
In a final burst of smoke, Ms. Kimberly vanishes.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**阿尔古斯**：跑得倒挺快。\
**Argus**: Tsk, she disappeared fast.

**维尔汀**：至少现在我们可以得出一些结论。\
**Vertin**: At least now we can draw some conclusions.

**维尔汀**：是重塑之手盯上了这座旅馆——我想，也许“启明会”正是他们的化名。\
**Vertin**: Manus Vindictae has set their eyes on this motel.

**维尔汀**：有一段时间，他们把这里当成了据点，并且进行了一些失败的术式尝试，但最终撤离了。\
**Vertin**: Under the name of the Order of Enlightenment, they used this place as a base and conducted some failed ritual experiments before they left.

**阿尔古斯**：重塑之手，我听说过他们的名字，那个臭名昭著的神秘学家团体……\
**Argus**: Manus Vindictae. I've heard of them. That infamous group of arcanists.

雇佣兵在此刻显得忧心忡忡。\
She looks worried.

**阿尔古斯**：如果凯拉落到他们的手里……\
**Argus**: If Kayla falls into their hands ...

**阿尔古斯**：——一定不会有什么好结果，对吗？\
**Argus**: Things won't turn out well, will they?

**维尔汀**：别担心，他们一般只招徕纯血神秘学家。\
**Vertin**: I wouldn't worry too much. They usually only target pure-blooded arcanists.

**阿尔古斯**：……噢，那就太好了。我敢保证，凯拉的父母都是纯得不能再纯的人类。\
**Argus**: Alright, that's a relief. Kayla's bloodline is a hundred percent human.

**维尔汀**：不过，既然是重塑之手来到了这儿……\
**Vertin**: But why would Manus Vindictae choose to come here specifically?

**维尔汀**：——他们的目的是什么？\
**Vertin**: What are they trying to do?

夜幕中的原野，对话还在继续。\
The conversation continues under the neon lights of the motel.

**蓝手帕**：我担心您夜里找不到路，特意点了门廊的灯。您瞧瞧，灯一亮，这些蛾子都飞了过来，真是讨厌……\
**Tuesday**: I was worried you wouldn't be able to make your way back, so I lit the porch light for you. Oh, but how annoying that these moths keep fluttering around.

**红弩箭**：少废话。\
**Lilya**: Cut the crap, lady.

**红弩箭**：维尔汀呢？带我过去找她。\
**Lilya**: Where's Vertin? Take me to her.

**蓝手帕**：平时我不怎么点燃这盏灯……因为我的孩子从不迷路。\
**Tuesday**: I rarely turn on this light. My baby never gets lost, you see.

侍应生淡淡地微笑着。\
She gives a faint smile.

**蓝手帕**：但像您这样年轻又活泼的孩子，总是需要前方有一盏亮着的灯，对吗？\
**Tuesday**: But a young, spirited child such as yourself always needs a light to lead the way. Am I right?

**蓝手帕**：对于疲累的旅客而言，这盏灯意味着一家旅馆；对于孩子而言，这盏灯意味着母亲；而对于您而言……这盏灯又意味着什么？\
**Tuesday**: To the weary traveler, this light is a shelter; to a child, it's a mother; and to you? What does this light mean to you?

侍应生的面孔泛着潮红。\
The maid's face flushes red.

**蓝手帕**：无论如何，人们都需要这样的一盏灯，以摆脱身后紧追不舍的恐惧，对吗？\
**Tuesday**: No matter who they are, people need a light to shine through the darkness—to chase away their fears. Don't you agree?

**红弩箭**：你是“启明会”的人？\
**Lilya**: Are you a member of the Order of Enlightenment?

**蓝手帕**：“启明会”？\
**Tuesday**: Order of Enlightenment?

**蓝手帕**：……噢，你在说那些讨人厌的客人。\
**Tuesday**: Oh, you mean those troublesome guests.

**红弩箭**：客人？\
**Lilya**: Guests?

侍应生并未理会她的疑问，只是自顾自地说了下去。\
The maid ignores her question and continues talking to herself.

**蓝手帕**：我不喜欢他们，他们总是到处写写画画，把布置好的房间弄得一团乱麻——甚至还弄疼了我的孩子……\
**Tuesday**: I don't like them one bit. They've scribbled all over the place and made a mess of the rooms. They hurt my baby!

**蓝手帕**：噢……别怕，别怕，我的孩子……\
**Tuesday**: Oh, my poor baby. Shh. Don't be scared. Everything's alright now.

她轻声地抚慰着襁褓里的孩子，用手舒缓地拍打着。\
She gently comforts the child in her arms, patting the swaddling cloth softly.

**红弩箭**：他们还在这里吗？\
**Lilya**: Are they still here?

**蓝手帕**：噢……当然，他们付出了我无法拒绝的报酬……\
**Tuesday**: Oh, of course. They made an offer that I couldn't refuse, after all.

**红弩箭**：多少钱？\
**Lilya**: How much did they pay you?

**蓝手帕**：哦呀，您果然还是小孩子。世界上当然存在着许多无法用金钱买到的东西……\
**Tuesday**: Oh, you are naive, my sweet child. There are countless things in this world that money can't buy.

**蓝手帕**：就像旅客无法在恰到好处的时候买到旅馆的出现，哭泣的孩子无法买到母亲的怀抱……\
**Tuesday**: A traveler can't buy the sudden appearance of a hotel at just the right time. A crying child can't buy the comforting embrace of their mother.

**蓝手帕**：哈……我也无法买到黑暗之中的那一份甜蜜与稠醇……\
**Tuesday**: Ha. And I can't buy that thrilling satisfaction brought by sweet darkness.

侍应生近似于神经质的喃喃自语令她感到无比烦躁。\
The maid's near-neurotic muttering is getting on Lilya's nerves.

**红弩箭**：——够了，我不想再听你说话。\
**Lilya**: Enough of your endless rambling!

**红弩箭**：我不能再和你说下去……不能……\
**Lilya**: I can't waste any more time talking to you. I can't ...

眼前的一切变得模糊，她隐约看见了侍应生似有若无的笑容。\
With every blink, Lilya's sight becomes increasingly blurred. She can just about make out the maid's smile.

**蓝手帕**：……哈。\
**Tuesday**: Aha.

**蓝手帕**：……♪\
**Tuesday**: …♪

她柔声安抚着眼神涣散的飞行员。\
She gently soothes the dazed pilot.

**蓝手帕**：睡在床里，不要再想参与那些大人的事……这才是孩子该做的……\
**Tuesday**: Sleep tight. Just leave everything to the adults. Yes, what a good child you are.

侍应生翻转了门口的告示牌，“请勿打扰”赫然其上。\
She flips the sign on the door to "Do Not Disturb."

## THH-12 猎犬与姑娘 / The Girl and the Hound

**阿尔古斯**：他的药物清单也在这儿……噢，这应该是他的笔记？\
**Argus**: Found his medication prescription, and, oh, is this his notebook?

雇佣兵从口袋中掏出了皱巴巴的纸条儿。\
She pulls a crumpled piece of paper from her pocket.

**阿尔古斯**：……哈，果然，老板。这个旅馆没那么简单，你看这封信，根本不是史蒂文写的。\
**Argus**: Ha, just as expected, boss. This motel ain't what it seems to be. Ain't no way that letter was written by Stefen.

**阿尔古斯**：这两种字迹，一种细长纤瘦，另一种活像个大老粗。瞎子都能看出来这是两个人。\
**Argus**: Take a look. The writing in this letter is delicate and slender, while the writing in this notebook is total chicken scratch. Even a blind person could tell they're written by two different people.

**维尔汀**：写信的人，并不是史蒂文——那么，塞信的人，也极有可能不是史蒂文。\
**Vertin**: Stefen didn't write the letter. So it's very likely that the person who sent it wasn't Stefen either.

脑海中不期然地浮现出了侍应生的身影。\
The maid suddenly comes to mind.

**阿尔古斯**：还有……\
**Argus**: And this ...

桌子旁有一沓装订在一起的纸张，她拿起了它。\
She picks up a stack of bound papers from the table.

**阿尔古斯**：……该死的，我讨厌数字。\
**Argus**: Ugh, I hate numbers.

**阿尔古斯**：维尔汀，你来看看这个——里面到底说了什么。\
**Argus**: I'll leave this one to you, boss.

**维尔汀**：这是一些账单，史蒂文先生把日常的花销全部都记在了这里。\
**Vertin**: It appears to be Mr. Stefen's records of his daily expenses, along with some notes.

**维尔汀**：包括香烟、酒精……还有大剂量的精神药物。\
**Vertin**: Cigarettes, alcohol, and a significant amount of psychiatric medication.

**维尔汀**：他认为自己的病情在恶化，每天都有幻象和幻听在折磨他，于是他不得不加大了药物的剂量。\
**Vertin**: It says he was tormented by his hallucinations day after day, so he had to increase his dosage.

**维尔汀**：……他说，他在这儿，看到了一个编号为707的房间。\
**Vertin**: Hm. And it says he saw a room numbered 707 here.

**阿尔古斯**：整个汽车旅馆只有两层，不可能有开头为7的房间——他有具体地描述这个房间吗？\
**Argus**: The motel only has two floors. There can't be a room starting with seven. Did he describe it at all?

**维尔汀**：他说……那是一扇鲜红的门扉，与周遭的一切都格格不入。\
**Vertin**: He said the room had a bright red door that seemed completely out of place.

**阿尔古斯**：也许是他的癔症又发作了。\
**Argus**: Maybe it was just one of his hallucinations.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

走廊上一抹一闪而过的红色。\
There's a flash of red in the hallway.

**维尔汀**：不，这不是癔症。\
**Vertin**: No, it's not that.

**维尔汀**：除了707房间之外，他还看见了许多无法解释的怪象……例如走廊中的双胞胎、天花板上倒悬而下的头发……以及一个……\
**Vertin**: He also saw all kinds of things: a pair of twins in the hallway, long hair hanging from the ceiling, and ...

**维尔汀**：果然，他看见了数羊羔，却以为那是自己的幻觉。\
**Vertin**: He saw Barbara but assumed she was another hallucination.

纸张上画着一只小小的羊头。\
A small sheep's head is sketched on the paper.

**维尔汀**：……这也说明了，数羊羔的确来过这个旅馆。\
**Vertin**: This proves that Barbara's been to the motel.

**维尔汀**：既然这样……\
**Vertin**: Which means ...

**蓝手帕**：不过，实在很可惜……我没有见过她。\
**Tuesday**: Well, I'm sorry to say that I've never met an arcanist with the head of a sheep.

**蓝手帕**：如果您需要的话，我可以帮您问问附近的农户……\
**Tuesday**: I can help you ask around if you—

**维尔汀**：她为什么要对我隐瞒这个消息……\
**Vertin**: Why did she lie to me?

雇佣兵的声音打断了思绪。\
Argus interrupts her thoughts.

**阿尔古斯**：老板，这本账单里有你想要的东西吗？\
**Argus**: So, did you find anything useful from the expense record?

**维尔汀**：……我得去找那个侍应生。\
**Vertin**: I need to talk to the maid.

**阿尔古斯**：别急，我们还没搜查盥洗室。\
**Argus**: Hold your horses. We haven't searched the washroom yet.

**阿尔古斯**：这个地方通常藏了最多的信息——您看过《教父》这部电影吗？迈克·柯里昂就是在马桶的水箱里找到了那把手枪。\
**Argus**: You should never skip the bathroom. Ain't you seen the Godfather? Michael Corleone grabs his gun from behind a toilet tank.

雇佣兵一边说着，一边推开了盥洗室的房门。\
She pushes open the bathroom door as she speaks.

盥洗室的镜子前，摆满了燃烧未尽的蜡烛。\
The bathroom mirror is surrounded by half-burned candles.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

雇佣兵伸出手，拦住了他人前进的脚步。\
She holds out a hand to signal a stop.

随后，她凑上前去，敲了敲镜面，铜制的镜框发出了铮然的回音。\
She moves closer and knocks on the mirror. The copper frame gives a hollow echo.

艳如猛毒的浓绿在镜面中一闪而过，一张象牙般的面孔浮现在了镜面上。\
A vivid, venomous green flashes across the mirror, and an ivory face appears in its reflection.

**？？？**：阿尔古斯，阿尔古斯，你来找我了……\
**???**: Argus, Argus. You've come to me.

**阿尔古斯**：——！\
**Argus**: —!

**维尔汀**：……她认识你？\
**Vertin**: Do you know her?

雇佣兵没有对这个问题作出反应，她的双目直视镜面，整个人似乎陷入了巨大的茫然之中。\
Argus doesn't respond. Her eyes are locked on the mirror, as if lost in a daze.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

**？？？**：阿尔古斯……\
**???**: Argus ...

**？？？**：阿尔古斯……阿尔古斯……\
**???**: Argus ... Argus ...

似有若无的声音在狭小的空间中回荡，如同一浪又一浪的海潮。\
The faint voice echoes around the bathroom, like waves crashing repeatedly against the shore.

**阿尔古斯**：这不可能……\
**Argus**: It-It's not possible.

雇佣兵的沉默，令人衍生了一个大胆的猜测。\
Argus's silence gives rise to a bold speculation.

**维尔汀**：——她是凯拉？\
**Vertin**: Is that Kayla?

**阿尔古斯**：不，绝不是。老板，如果您亲眼见过凯拉，就能明白这绝不是她——这只是一个丑陋的幽灵，我想它的出现也许与这座旅馆浓厚的神秘学氛围有关。\
**Argus**: No, there's no way that's her. If you knew Kayla like I do, you'd say the same. This distorted reflection in the mirror is probably a result of the excessive arcanum in this motel.

**阿尔古斯**：一种类似于“血腥玛丽”的怪谈……这曾在当地很流行。\
**Argus**: A ritual similar to Bloody Mary used to be quite popular among the kids in this town.

**阿尔古斯**：如果在午夜照镜子，里面的幽灵会变成你朝思暮想的人——只要你回应了幽灵的话语，就会被它夺去灵魂。\
**Argus**: If you look into a mirror at exactly midnight, the spirit within will morph into the shape of the person you desire most. But if you respond to the spirit's call, it will drain your soul from your body.

**维尔汀**：我从未想过这是真的。\
**Vertin**: I always thought those were just myths.

**阿尔古斯**：噢，曾经的我也是这样，见得多了就不觉得奇怪了。\
**Argus**: So did I. But after all the strange things I've seen, I've become less surprised.

**阿尔古斯**：这些幽灵以此为生，它们需要一种灵魂中的能量来维生。所以这东西很能诱骗人——要当心。\
**Argus**: These spirits feed on the energy of our souls. That's why you should never trust a word they say.

**阿尔古斯**：而那些被骗的人就没有那么好运了……他们会因此恍惚好一阵子，有的人甚至患上了癔症——您看看，史蒂文先生就是最典型的例子。\
**Argus**: The people who are tricked by them fall into a kind of trance, and, some, like Mr. Stefen, go crazy.

**阿尔古斯**：……不知道他在镜子里看到什么了呢？\
**Argus**: I wonder what he saw in the mirror.

**阿尔古斯**：不过，我与他不同。\
**Argus**: Anyway, I won't repeat his mistake.

雇佣兵举起了猎枪，蓄势待发。\
She raises her shotgun, ready to fire.

**阿尔古斯**：对我们来说，最绝望的险境不是多么危险的场景，而是内心的动摇。\
**Argus**: For mercs like me, the deepest despair ain't external danger; it's internal hesitation.

**阿尔古斯**：如果面对这种幽灵，就会轻易地动摇——那我又有什么资格去保护别人呢？我们必须相信自己的判断……\
**Argus**: If some pale imitation makes me hesitate so easily, then how can I claim to be able to protect others? You've gotta be able to stand your ground.

**阿尔古斯**：罪犯会在获知死刑判决后，想尽方法地为自己辩白；间谍为了获取情报，披上一层又一层的皮……\
**Argus**: A cunning criminal would use every excuse to defend themselves in court. And a scheming spy would wear all kinds of disguises to gather information on the enemy.

**阿尔古斯**：所以我们只能相信自己……\
**Argus**: That's why we've gotta stay sharp. When it comes down to it, we only have our own two legs to stand on.

**阿尔古斯**：一个合格的雇佣兵，不需要对所谓的道德、善良、伦理去进行思考，那是学者们的工作。一旦我们对这些东西产生了怀疑，那也就离死不远了。\
**Argus**: Mercs ain't philosophers. Once a merc starts pondering morals, justice, and ethics, they're digging their own grave.

**阿尔古斯**：对我们而言，目标就是唯一的意义；过度的思考，只会毁了一个雇佣兵。\
**Argus**: For a merc, the mission objective is the only thing that matters. Overthinking don't bring nothing but disaster and destruction.

**阿尔古斯**：所以，她……它骗不到我。\
**Argus**: That's why she—no, it—won't fool me.

她目光平静。\
Her gaze is steady.

眼前似乎闪过了一幕幕久远的回忆。\
Memories flash by, distant and playful.

在原野中的，嬉戏着的，追逐着的。\
Laughing and running in those grassy fields.

**阿尔古斯**：小凯拉是农场里的珍宝，每个人都那样地爱她。\
**Argus**: The folks on the ranch adored little Kayla.

**阿尔古斯**：他们爱她，如同爱护自己的眼珠子。\
**Argus**: She was the apple of all their eyes.

**阿尔古斯**：这样一个丑陋的东西，它怎么能……\
**Argus**: How dare this ugly imitation!

她用力地给猎枪上了子弹。\
<speed=9>She forcefully loads the shotgun.

**阿尔古斯**：所以……\
**Argus**: So ...

她站在了维尔汀的身前，将枪管对准了那面镜子。\
She aims her gun squarely at the mirror.

**阿尔古斯**：这就是我的回答。\
**Argus**: Here's my response.

**？？？**：好、好痛……\
**???**: Urgh, i-it hurts.

**？？？**：阿尔古斯，阿尔古斯，你来找我了……\
**???**: Argus, Argus. You've come to me.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

**阿尔古斯**：所以说，干这一行的必须多长点心眼——您瞧瞧，这次就差点被骗了。如果幽灵们有业务能力的评选，我想它保准能拿个第一。\
**Argus**: Let this serve as a reminder to remain vigilant. If there were a "Deceitful Spirit of the Year" award, I'm sure that would win.

## THH-13 反刍的胃袋 / The Churning Stomach

**维尔汀**：史蒂文·加西亚，芝诺上尉，36岁。\
**Vertin**: Stefen Garcia, a Zeno captain, 36 years old.

**维尔汀**：出于一些我们所不知道的原因——极有可能与重塑之手有关，他入住了这个旅馆。\
**Vertin**: For unknown reasons—likely connected to Manus Vindictae—he moved into this motel.

**维尔汀**：在住进旅馆之后，他曾数次尝试和芝诺联络，这些联络无一例外，没有成功。\
**Vertin**: He attempted to make contact with Zeno several times, all of which failed.

**维尔汀**：这期间，他的谵妄与惊厥愈发严重，饱受幻象与恐惧的折磨。\
**Vertin**: During his stay, he was tortured by increasingly intense hallucinations, delusion, and fear.

**维尔汀**：所以……\
**Vertin**: And as a result ...

**阿尔古斯**：所以，他就在刚刚自杀了。\
**Argus**: As a result, he committed suicide.

**阿尔古斯**：这就是线索告诉我们的内容。\
**Argus**: And that's everything the evidence shows.

混沌的线索在脑中翻涌，如同一个正在反刍的胃袋。\
Chaotic clues are rolling in the mind, like a churning stomach.

**维尔汀**：……不对。\
**Vertin**: No.

**维尔汀**：我们一定忽略了什么重要的信息……\
**Vertin**: We must've overlooked something.

**维尔汀**：自杀的军官、用摩斯电码传递的求救信息。\
**Vertin**: A military officer killing himself; a phone call asking for help in Morse code.

**维尔汀**：还有……重塑之手和……\
**Vertin**: Not to mention Manus Vindictae.

**阿尔古斯**：老板，你有什么结论吗？\
**Argus**: Where's this going, boss?

**维尔汀**：……我们前来这家旅店，遭遇了许多无法用常理解释的事件。\
**Vertin**: We've encountered a series of bizarre events, one after another, ever since we arrived at this motel.

**维尔汀**：房间里的术阵、发疯的军官、镜子里的幽灵、藏匿其中的重塑之手成员……\
**Vertin**: The rituals in the rooms, the officer that went mad, the spirit in the mirror, and Manus Vindictae.

**维尔汀**：唯独有一个人置身事外。\
**Vertin**: Only one person remains uninvolved.

**阿尔古斯**：你是想说，她是位于幕后的始作俑者？\
**Argus**: Are you tryna say that she's the mastermind behind all this?

**维尔汀**：她理应是那个了解事件全貌的人，却处处显得一无所知——这本来就很奇怪。\
**Vertin**: She should know more about all this than anyone, yet she feigns ignorance at every turn, which is suspicious in its own right.

**阿尔古斯**：但这不会让她因此获得更多的利益。很显然，不会有客人因为撞鬼而赞扬她。\
**Argus**: But what's there for a motel housekeeper to gain from all this? It's not like these spooky scandals would attract more guests.

**阿尔古斯**：除非在她的幕后有其他的人……可这也说不通，不是吗？\
**Argus**: Unless someone else is pulling the strings, but that don't make much sense either, does it?

**阿尔古斯**：她任由这位军官在这儿发疯，也不去管重塑之手在这儿的行为……您觉得她是得到了谁的授意呢？某个更为庞大、更为神秘的组织吗？\
**Argus**: When all these unusual things happened, she was happy to stand by and watch, but by whose orders? Some larger, more mysterious organization?

**阿尔古斯**：得了吧。\
**Argus**: Gimme a break.

**维尔汀**：……假设她并不需要这些东西呢？\
**Vertin**: What if she doesn't desire money or power?

**阿尔古斯**：好吧，老板，那么接下来您是去找那位侍应生吗？\
**Argus**: So what you're saying is that you need to ask Little Miss Maid a couple more questions.

**维尔汀**：我得再去问问她。\
**Vertin**: Precisely.

雇佣兵叹了一口气。\
Argus sighs.

**阿尔古斯**：这个幽灵既然能变化成凯拉的样子……我想它一定在某个时候见过凯拉——或者说，凯拉在某个时候来过这个房间。\
**Argus**: That spirit morphed into Kayla, so it must've seen her face at some point. Which means that, at one time, Kayla was in this room.

**阿尔古斯**：我得承认您的猜测有些道理，她的确不是一位符合常理的侍应生。您贸然前去并不是一个明智的选择。\
**Argus**: And you're right. Tuesday's definitely not a run-of-the-mill motel maid. It wouldn't be wise to approach her rashly.

**阿尔古斯**：因此，我建议，您最好等我查验完这儿的情况，咱们再一起去向那位侍应生问话。\
**Argus**: Let me finish up here first, then we can go question her together.

**维尔汀**：……好。\
**Vertin**: Alright.

短暂的等待之后，雇佣兵失望地摇了摇头。\
After a moment, Argus shakes her head in disappointment.

**阿尔古斯**：什么也没有，老板。\
**Argus**: Nope. I got nothing.

**阿尔古斯**：去找那位侍应生吧……恰好，我也有一些问题想要问问她。\
**Argus**: Let's go find that maid. I have a few questions for her myself.

她打开了门，随即愣在原地。\
She makes her way across the room and opens the door. She freezes.

**阿尔古斯**：尸体……不见了。\
**Argus**: Where'd the body go?

原本横亘在走廊中的尸体不翼而飞，仅留下一摊飞溅的血迹。\
The corpse that had been lying in the hallway has vanished, leaving only a pool of blood on the floor.

**阿尔古斯**：这里没有拖拽和运输的痕迹，到底是谁……\
**Argus**: Ain't no signs of dragging, neither. Who, and how?

**电话**：叮铃铃铃铃——\
**Telephone**: *ring-ring-ring—*

模糊的铃声再次从尚未合拢的门扉中传来。\
The ringing echoes through the doorway.

**阿尔古斯**：……又是电话。\
**Argus**: The phone again.

**阿尔古斯**：还去吗？老板，我猜那八成又是那些古怪的电话……\
**Argus**: What do you think? Should we answer it? I bet it's another one of those prank calls.

**维尔汀**：那不是恶作剧，是有人在使用摩斯电码求救。\
**Vertin**: Those weren't prank calls. Someone was sending a distress signal in Morse code.

她拎起了听筒，按下了免提键。\
She picks up the receiver and presses the speaker button.

**？？？**：……您能告诉我，现在是什么时间吗？\
**???**: Could you tell me what year it is now?

一个细细的声音从电话的彼端传来。\
A soft voice plays through the speaker.

**维尔汀**：哪位？\
**Vertin**: Who's this?

**？？？**：……我是数羊羔。\
**???**: This is Barbara.

## THH-14 保佑她 / May They Be Blessed

电话彼端的声音还在继续。\
The voice on the other end continues.

**数羊羔**：太好了，既然电话能够被使用，我想风的步伐也许还在附近游荡……\
**Barbara**: Wonderful, I can talk over the phone now. The wind must still be wandering nearby.

**维尔汀**：……别担心。\
**Vertin**: That's good to hear.

**维尔汀**：你是《UTTU》的编辑？\
**Vertin**: Are you an editor for UTTU?

电话彼端的人松了一口气。\
There's a sigh of relief.

**数羊羔**：……是的，小姐，正如您所说。\
**Barbara**: Yes, Miss, I am.

**数羊羔**：不过，在对话开始前，您能告诉我现在是哪一年吗？\
**Barbara**: But before we continue our conversation, could you please tell me what year it is now?

**维尔汀**：……1990年。\
**Vertin**: ... 1990.

**数羊羔**：噢……我明白了。\
**Barbara**: I see.

细弱的声音镇定了下来。\
The frail voice steadies.

**维尔汀**：……数羊羔小姐，我要怎样才能见到您？\
**Vertin**: Ms. Barbara, can I meet you in person?

**数羊羔**：见到我……？\
**Barbara**: You want to meet me?

**维尔汀**：是的，我是隶属于圣洛夫基金会的司辰——基金会希望能够得知兀尔德的下落，故而派我来寻找您。\
**Vertin**: Yes, I'm Vertin, the Timekeeper of the St. Pavlov Foundation. I was sent to ask you about Urd's whereabouts.

**维尔汀**：但目前，您的安全状况似乎不容乐观。\
**Vertin**: But you don't seem to be in a favorable situation right now.

**数羊羔**：维尔汀小姐，这个房间隔绝了所有的联络，我听不到风的声音，无法得知兀尔德的下落。\
**Barbara**: Ms. Vertin, I couldn't possibly locate Urd's whereabouts. The whispers of the wind can't reach this room.

**维尔汀**：……风的声音？\
**Vertin**: The whispers of the wind?

**数羊羔**：是的，您可以理解为一种特殊的联络方式。\
**Barbara**: Yes, it's a special form of communication.

**维尔汀**：我要怎样才能帮助您？\
**Vertin**: Right. Well, is there anything I can do to help you rebuild this line of communication?

**数羊羔**：嗯……我先为您讲述一下当前的情况。现在，我能够确定的有以下几件事。\
**Barbara**: Hmm. Let me first explain the situation to you. Here are a few things I'm certain of:

**数羊羔**：首先，这个旅馆并不是普通的旅馆，而是某种特殊的、具备超自然者般的生命力的存在。\
**Barbara**: First, this isn't an ordinary motel. It possesses some kind of supernatural life force.

**数羊羔**：在入住旅馆前，我对附近的居民做过访谈，他们无一不提到了近几个月以来，在附近出现的都市怪谈。\
**Barbara**: Before checking in, I interviewed some of the residents nearby. They all mentioned eerie rumors centered around the motel these past few months.

**维尔汀**：确实，我们在旅馆中也遇到了类似的情况——这是一个怪谈泛滥的地方。\
**Vertin**: Yes, we've encountered some bizarre events here. Like real-life urban legends.

**数羊羔**：第二，我现在被困在一个红色的房间里。\
**Barbara**: Second, I'm now trapped in a red room.

**数羊羔**：这个房间与你们同样地处于旅馆之中……但与你们的房间不同，它隔绝了一切信息。\
**Barbara**: This room is in the same motel as yours. What's different is that it blocks all forms of communication.

**数羊羔**：我没有办法打开那扇门，也没有办法呼出电话。\
**Barbara**: I couldn't get the room to open, and my voice didn't reach through the phone.

**数羊羔**：不过，一声枪响打破了这份无形的桎梏……在枪响之后，这个小房间猛烈地进行了一次收缩。随后，一切线路畅通无阻。\
**Barbara**: That was until a gunshot broke this intangible restraint. This small room contracted violently, and now I can communicate with the outside world.

**数羊羔**：我最初还以为是某种地震，但随后，被压缩的空间又恢复了原状——我想这应该不能用“地震”来解释。\
**Barbara**: At first, I thought it was an earthquake, but the contracted space soon returned to normal. Earthquakes can't do that, can they?

**维尔汀**：在这之前，您依靠蜘蛛来传递信息吗？\
**Vertin**: Before this happened, were you using spiders to communicate with the world outside?

**数羊羔**：嗯，所幸这里有很多蜘蛛……我想，这应该与蜘蛛在都市怪谈中的泛滥有关。\
**Barbara**: Yes, I was. As luck would have it, there are many spiders here. Thanks to the prevalence of spiders in urban legends, I assume.

电话彼端传来了翻书页的声音。\
They can hear the sound of pages being turned from the other end of the telephone.

**数羊羔**：譬如说有许多人会忧虑“在头发中生存的蜘蛛”……实际上这是一个来源于13世纪英国的说教故事。\
**Barbara**: There's some paranoia about "spiders living in hair." It originated in a sermon from 13th-century England.

**数羊羔**：“一位爱慕虚荣的信众总是在做弥撒的时候迟到，因为她花了太多时间来整理她的头发，结果魔鬼以蜘蛛的形式附着在了她的头发中。”\
**Barbara**: A woman was always late to mass because she spent too much time styling her hair. Eventually, a devil attached itself to her hair in the form of a spider.

**数羊羔**：……是的，这些小家伙以它们的方式替我传递信息。\
**Barbara**: Yes, they delivered messages for me in their own peculiar way.

**数羊羔**：我很担忧自己处于一个与外界隔绝的空间中，这会令我联想到某些不好的事……\
**Barbara**: Being completely isolated from the outside world greatly unsettled me. It reminded me of that terrible phenomenon.

她轻轻地喘了几口气。\
She takes a few light breaths.

**数羊羔**：所幸并不如此。\
**Barbara**: Fortunately, that wasn't the case.

**维尔汀**：您并没有办法离开那个房间对吗？\
**Vertin**: But you're still trapped in that room, right?

**数羊羔**：是的，它没有门，我无法离开。\
**Barbara**: Yes. The door's gone. I can't get out from the inside.

**维尔汀**：那么，您当初是如何进去的呢……或者说，是谁带你进入这个房间的？\
**Vertin**: How did you get in there in the first place? Or rather, who brought you into that room?

**数羊羔**：噢，还能有谁呢？\
**Barbara**: Well, who else could it be?

**数羊羔**：是那个名叫蓝……蓝手帕的侍应生。\
**Barbara**: The maid named Tuesday.

**维尔汀**：果然。\
**Vertin**: Just as I expected.

**阿尔古斯**：……等等。\
**Argus**: Wait.

久未出声的雇佣兵打断了对话。\
The mercenary cuts in.

**数羊羔**：您是阿尔古斯，对吗？我还记得您的声音。\
**Barbara**: You're that driver who left me on the road, right? I remember your voice.

**阿尔古斯**：……对，是我。\
**Argus**: Yeah, it's me.

**阿尔古斯**：那之后我又折返去了你所停驻的地方，但你那时已经不见了。\
**Argus**: I actually changed my mind and turned back to get you, but you were gone by the time I arrived.

**阿尔古斯**：——你在那时就到达了这家旅店吗？\
**Argus**: I guess that's when you came to this motel, right?

**数羊羔**：嗯，蓝手帕看见了我，她邀请我前往这个旅馆。\
**Barbara**: Yes, Tuesday saw me and invited me here.

**阿尔古斯**：噢……\
**Argus**: Oh.

**数羊羔**：您想问些什么？\
**Barbara**: Did you wanna ask me something?

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

**阿尔古斯**：您在这里，看见一个高约5英尺3英寸的女孩了吗？\
**Argus**: Have you seen a girl of about 5 foot 3 here?

**阿尔古斯**：她穿着白裙子，一头栗色的卷发，眼珠子则是翠绿色的，手很小。\
**Argus**: In a white dress. Curly chestnut-colored hair. Green eyes. Small hands.

**数羊羔**：……\
**Barbara**: ...

**数羊羔**：也许我见过她。\
**Barbara**: I may have seen her.

**数羊羔**：在我刚刚到达的时候，有这样的一个女孩从楼道上走了下来——\
**Barbara**: When I first arrived, I saw a girl who matched your description coming down the hallway.

**数羊羔**：她挎着一个空空的篮子，我想她也许是去附近的镇子上购物了？\
**Barbara**: She was carrying an empty basket. I presumed that she'd been shopping in the town nearby.

**数羊羔**：我记得她并没有退房。\
**Barbara**: If I recall correctly, she didn't check out.

**阿尔古斯**：……谢谢。\
**Argus**: Thank you.

她脱力地耷拉着肩膀，眼中的辉光虚弱地熄灭。\
She slumps her shoulders, and the light in her eye dims.

她不再说话了。\
She says no more.

**维尔汀**：我们该怎么找到那个房间呢……\
**Vertin**: How can we find this room?

**数羊羔**：它很好找，就在走廊的一侧，编号为707。\
**Barbara**: It's just in the hallway, number 707.

**数羊羔**：那是一扇红色的门……\
**Barbara**: Look for a door covered in red—

滴滴滴——\
*beep—beep—beep*

**阿尔古斯**：……电话断了？\
**Argus**: Looks like the phone got disconnected.

**维尔汀**：阿尔古斯，我知道了，数羊羔就在那个名为707的房间。\
**Vertin**: So Barbara's in that room that Stefen saw. Number 707.

**维尔汀**：那么，接下来，你要去镇子上找你的凯拉吗？\
**Vertin**: I'm going to find it. What about you? Heading into town for Kayla?

短暂的沉默之后，她再次开口了。\
After a brief silence, Argus speaks.

**阿尔古斯**：我曾在走廊上见过一个奇怪的地方……侍应生的脚印围绕着它——那应该是一个被频繁出入的地方。\
**Argus**: I did notice a weird spot in the hallway earlier. The maid's footprints were going back and forth, like there was an entrance there.

**阿尔古斯**：但我却没有看到任何的门。\
**Argus**: But I didn't see no signs of a door.

雇佣兵用已上膛的枪管戳了戳头上的痒处。\
She scratches her head with the barrel of her gun.

**维尔汀**：如果有一天你死在了你自己的枪口之下，我也并不会意外。\
**Vertin**: I wouldn't be surprised if you died by your own gun one day.

**阿尔古斯**：哈，那可真是帮了我大忙。\
**Argus**: Haha, that'd be a memorable way to go.

**阿尔古斯**：……开玩笑。\
**Argus**: Alright, enough kidding around.

雇佣兵振作了精神。\
She perks up.

**阿尔古斯**：那个侍应生并不想让我们知道数羊羔在这座旅馆之中——哈，可惜，百密一疏。\
**Argus**: Our Little Miss Maid tried so very hard to hide Barbara from us, but I guess the lamb's out of the bag now.

**维尔汀**：情况已经非常明晰——走吧。\
**Vertin**: Yes. It's all crystal clear now. Let's go.

**阿尔古斯**：等一下，老板。\
**Argus**: Hold up a sec, boss.

她咬着嘴唇，露出了一副为难的样子。\
She bites her lip.

**阿尔古斯**：你那儿还有多余的糖果吗？我的糖已经快要吃完了，这儿没有什么补给的手段。\
**Argus**: Do you have any candies? I'm running on fumes here, and I ain't got no way to replenish my stash.

发出请求对她而言似乎是一件很困难的事。\
Asking for help seems very difficult for her.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

她从口袋里掏出了几枚糖果，塞在了阿尔古斯的掌心。\
She pulls a few pieces of candy from her pocket and places them in Argus's palm.

**维尔汀**：很快我们就能从这里出去了。\
**Vertin**: Us and Barbara will be out of here soon.

**维尔汀**：我找到数羊羔，你也能找到凯拉。\
**Vertin**: And you'll find some candy and Kayla in town.

## THH-15 服务热线 / The Front Desk Call

红房间的中心，摆放着一张雪白的婴儿床。\
In the center of the red room stands a snow-white crib.

垂下的布帘微微摇晃着，如同正在跃动的血管。\
The hanging curtains sway slightly, like pulsating veins.

羊首人身的神秘学家伫立于此，她正面对着那模糊透光的薄布，不发一言。\
An arcanist with the head of a sheep stands there, silently observing the translucent fabric.

脚步声渐近，她没有回头。\
Footsteps draw closer, but she doesn't turn to face them.

**蓝手帕**：是我的招待还不够周到吗？\
**Tuesday**: Are you not satisfied with my services?

**数羊羔**：……\
**Barbara**: ...

**数羊羔**：无论如何，您都不该按断我的电话。\
**Barbara**: No matter what, you shouldn't have cut the phone off.

侍应生略有歉意地收回了按在电话插簧上的手。\
The maid withdraws her hand from the telephone's hook switch with a hint of apology.

**数羊羔**：也不该隔绝我与外界的联络——尤其是您。\
**Barbara**: Nor should you have isolated me from the outside world.

**数羊羔**：因为您应该知道这意味着什么。\
**Barbara**: Because you should know better than anyone what that means.

**蓝手帕**：……为什么我会需要知道这些？\
**Tuesday**: Why should I?

**蓝手帕**：我只知道，一个这样小的孩子，不应该独自出现在这条公路的附近。\
**Tuesday**: All I know is that a poor, helpless child like you shouldn't be alone on the roadside.

**蓝手帕**：你的母亲呢？她没有告诉你要小心吗？\
**Tuesday**: Where's your mother? Didn't she tell you to be careful?

**数羊羔**：……\
**Barbara**: ...

她叹出了一口气。\
She sighs softly.

**数羊羔**：……您的确什么都不记得了。\
**Barbara**: You really don't remember anything, do you?

**蓝手帕**：在您看来，我应该记得什么？\
**Tuesday**: What do you mean? What do you think I should remember?

**数羊羔**：噢，很显然，现在这已经不重要了——旅馆的陈设很不错，只有您一个人来打扫这些吗？\
**Barbara**: Well, clearly, it doesn't matter now. This motel's well decorated. Did you do all this yourself?

侍应生露出了笑容。\
The maid smiles.

**蓝手帕**：呵呵……我在想，是不是所有的孩子都是这样？总是故意说些颠三倒四的话语，来吸引母亲的注意力……\
**Tuesday**: Heh heh. Are all children like this? Always talking in circles to draw Mama's attention.

**蓝手帕**：虽然总是被人一眼看穿，但那些童稚的话语总是可爱得让人心尖儿打颤……\
**Tuesday**: Ah, but these innocent words make them all the more adorable.

**数羊羔**：……我不是孩子。\
**Barbara**: I am not a child.

**蓝手帕**：哈……这也是孩子们常说的话。\
**Tuesday**: Ha. That's exactly what a child would say.

**数羊羔**：……\
**Barbara**: ...

她无奈地妥协了。\
She yields helplessly.

**蓝手帕**：我总觉得您亲近又熟悉，好像在很久以前见到过似的。\
**Tuesday**: I've always felt a familiarity with you, like I've known you for a long time.

**蓝手帕**：您能和我说说吗？您为什么独自留在了77号公路附近？\
**Tuesday**: Can you tell me about it—why were you out here on Route 77 all alone?

**蓝手帕**：……也许我能帮上您的忙呢？\
**Tuesday**: Maybe I can help you.

**数羊羔**：您听说过《UTTU》这本杂志吗？\
**Barbara**: Have you heard of UTTU?

**蓝手帕**：噢！我知道……\
**Tuesday**: Oh, I have!

**蓝手帕**：这是一本有关于时尚、潮流与先锋的杂志……\
**Tuesday**: It's a magazine about fashion, trends, and the avant-garde.

**蓝手帕**：我的哥哥曾经很喜欢它，但父亲并不能理解这种喜欢——他认为既然是家里的长子，就应该去开农用机械，而不是阅读这种软绵绵的杂志。\
**Tuesday**: My brother loved that magazine, but my father found it unacceptable—to think his eldest son would read those softies' magazines instead of working on the farm!

**蓝手帕**：待在家里看书，研究时尚、潮流、迪斯科。这可不是一个德克萨斯男人应该做的事情。\
**Tuesday**: Fashion, trends, disco ... these aren't things a Texan man should pursue, at least according to my father.

**蓝手帕**：后来，父亲销毁了所有有关于迪斯科的唱片，连同哥哥那张前往洛杉矶的机票。\
**Tuesday**: In the end, my father destroyed all my brother's disco records, along with his plane ticket to Los Angeles.

**数羊羔**：这很好，说明他成功地躲过了那场暴乱。\
**Barbara**: Perhaps that's for the best. He avoided the riots.

**蓝手帕**：……什么？\
**Tuesday**: Huh?

**数羊羔**：没什么，您对此有什么看法或者意见呢？\
**Barbara**: Nothing. So, what do you think?

她将眼前的侍应生视作采访对象——怪谈背后的女主人，这是一次不容错过的机会。\
She's treating the maid as an interview subject—the woman behind the legend, a chance not to be missed.

**蓝手帕**：我？\
**Tuesday**: Me?

侍应生略感惊讶。\
She looks somewhat surprised.

**蓝手帕**：我应该对此有什么见解吗？\
**Tuesday**: Why should I have any opinion?

**数羊羔**：或者说，这对您产生了什么影响？\
**Barbara**: Let me rephrase that. What impact has this had on you?

**蓝手帕**：噢……\
**Tuesday**: Oh.

蓝手帕陷入了思考，随后她摇了摇头。\
Tuesday ponders for a moment, then shakes her head.

**蓝手帕**：这事情与我无关，不是吗？\
**Tuesday**: But what happened between them has nothing to do with me, does it?

**蓝手帕**：这都是他们自己所做的选择……\
**Tuesday**: These were the choices they made.

她抿上了嘴唇，面孔红润。\
She purses her lips, her face flushed.

**数羊羔**：在我刚刚到达这里时，有一位当地的居民说：不要去蓝手帕旅馆居住。\
**Barbara**: When I first arrived, a local resident told me not to stay at Tuesday's Motel.

**数羊羔**：他的婶婶在那个旅店住过，回家后不久便发了疯。\
**Barbara**: He said his aunt went mad soon after she stayed here.

紧锁着的窗户不断地震颤着，发出轻微的响声。\
The windows rattle gently, emitting a faint sound.

**蓝手帕**：哈……我记得那位女士，她的头很大，总让我想起一些有关于畸形的怪谈……\
**Tuesday**: Ha, I remember that lady. Her head was so large. It reminded me of those stories of people with deformities.

**蓝手帕**：所以我让她在深夜里“观看”了一场畸形秀，遗憾的是她似乎并不喜欢这些。\
**Tuesday**: So I had her "watch" a freak show at midnight. Sadly, she didn't seem to enjoy it.

**数羊羔**：……\
**Barbara**: ...

远处的收获机被启动了，柴油发动机的声音传入了室内。\
A harvester starts up in the distance. The sound of the engine fills the room.

**蓝手帕**：这时节的农田，联合收获机一刻也不停地运作着。作物的收获是令人多么高兴的一件事，但与之相伴的噪音却总让孩子担惊受怕。\
**Tuesday**: At this time of year, the farmers run their combine harvesters on the fields nonstop. The harvest is a joyful time of year, but the accompanying noise always frightens the children.

**蓝手帕**：您听过类似的故事吗？贪玩的孩子前往大型机械的附近，结果被卷入机械中，丢失了一只手，或是一个脑袋……哈……\
**Tuesday**: Have you heard the stories? Of how naughty children get too close to harvesters and get caught in them, losing a hand or even a head, haha.

**蓝手帕**：我的旅馆里正好缺了这一类的故事——农田、机械、德克萨斯州、断手或断头的孩子……唔，身临其境的怪谈……\
**Tuesday**: Fields, machinery, children with severed limbs ... Hmm, these stories are exactly what my motel's missing.

窗户的响声愈发焦灼。\
The window rattling grows more frantic.

**蓝手帕**：啊呀，抱歉，孩子在叫我……如果我再不去，它恐怕又要埋怨我了。\
**Tuesday**: Oh, my baby's calling. Please excuse me; I don't want another temper tantrum on my hands.

**蓝手帕**：抱歉了，软绵绵的小客人——我很期待下次与您的谈话……和您说话的时候，总有接连不断的好主意从我的脑子里冒出来。\
**Tuesday**: Apologies, my fluffy little child. I look forward to our next conversation. Talking to you always brings me inspiration.

**蓝手帕**：但旅店最近的客人实在是太多了……多到令我有些讨厌。\
**Tuesday**: But the motel's been too busy lately. It's starting to get on my nerves.

侍应生慢悠悠地说着，面孔上再次浮现了红晕。\
The maid speaks slowly, her face flushed again.

**数羊羔**：咳、咳……\
**Barbara**: *cough*

她虚弱地咳嗽着。\
Her cough is weak, like a sickly child's.

**蓝手帕**：您瞧瞧，这样虚弱的孩子，我怎么忍心让您去别的地方……在您的咳嗽病痊愈之前，你尽可以在这个小房间里居住。\
**Tuesday**: See, this is what I mean. How could I bear to send you out on your own? You'll stay right here in this cozy little room until you're fully recovered.

**数羊羔**：我不需要这样的偏爱，居住在小房间也不能治愈我的病症。\
**Barbara**: I don't need this "special treatment" of yours. Staying here won't cure my illness.

**蓝手帕**：您先睡一觉吧，等精神放松之后，就再也不会有这些胡思乱想了。\
**Tuesday**: Just get some sleep. You'll come to your senses after a good rest.

**蓝手帕**：……再见。\
**Tuesday**: I'll see you soon.

侍应生踩着轻巧的步伐离开了房间。\
The maid lightly steps out of the room.

在她离去之后，羔羊眼看着门扉从房间之中消失了。\
Barbara watches as the door vanishes.

**蓝手帕**：……？\
**Tuesday**: ...?

她望着走廊上残余的血迹，在不久之前，上面还有着一具军官的遗体。\
She looks at the pool of blood in the hallway where the officer's body once was.

**蓝手帕**：我说过很多次，不要再捡地上的东西吃……\
**Tuesday**: How many times have I told you not to eat things off the floor?

**？？？**：呜哇……\
**???**: *cry*

怀中的襁褓忽然发出古怪的哭声。\
The bundle in her arms suddenly lets out a strange cry.

**蓝手帕**：好了，别再哭了……\
**Tuesday**: There, there. Don't cry, sweetheart.

## THH-16 苦目糖 / Picrasma Candy

**维尔汀**：……就是这儿？\
**Vertin**: Is this the spot?

**阿尔古斯**：就是这儿。\
**Argus**: Sure as shooting.

眼前的走廊与他处别无二致。\
The hallway looks identical to any other.

**阿尔古斯**：看这些脚印……\
**Argus**: Look, these footprints.

**阿尔古斯**：这是在十分钟之内留下的脚印。\
**Argus**: They're less than ten minutes old.

**维尔汀**：……可是我们没有看到707的房门。\
**Vertin**: But where's the door to room 707?

**维尔汀**：我能感受到这附近有一些能量的扰动……但这绝不是出于神秘术。\
**Vertin**: I can sense some energy fluctuations nearby, but they're definitely not from arcane skills.

她将掌心贴上了墙壁。\
She presses her palm against the wall.

**维尔汀**：除了神秘术，还有什么能让这些能量如此的焦灼……\
**Vertin**: What else could produce such intense energy?

**蓝手帕**：……噢，两位，请问有什么能够帮助您的吗？\
**Tuesday**: Oh, can I help you with something?

毫无预兆地，侍应生的声音在身后响起。\
The maid's voice comes unexpectedly from behind them.

**阿尔古斯**：……蓝手帕小姐，我有一个问题想问问你。\
**Argus**: Ms. Tuesday, I've got a question for you.

雇佣兵紧紧地盯着侍应生，目光灼灼，如同猎人终于追寻到了猎物的血迹。\
She stares intently at the maid, her gaze sharp as if she's finally caught the scent of her prey.

**阿尔古斯**：你知道那个707房间该怎么走吗？\
**Argus**: Do you know how to get to room 707?

**蓝手帕**：707？\
**Tuesday**: 707?

**阿尔古斯**：……是的——我想，我要找的东西也许就在那个房间里。\
**Argus**: Yup. What I've been looking for might just be in that room.

**蓝手帕**：嗯……我乐于满足客人的要求，客房服务或是更换房间，只要是我能做到的，我一向不吝于帮助。\
**Tuesday**: Hmm. I'm usually more than happy to satisfy the requests of my guests, as long as it's within my power.

**蓝手帕**：但您的要求过界了——那不是您该去的地方。\
**Tuesday**: But this one crosses the line.

**阿尔古斯**：……很可惜，看来我们的谈判破裂了。\
**Argus**: Shame. Looks like negotiations are over.

**阿尔古斯**：瞬息之后，又见星光。\
**Argus**: And thence we came forth to see again the stars.

她的眼睛里再次燃烧起了蓝绿色的辉光。\
After a brief moment, a glimmer of emerald light reignites in her eye.

**蓝手帕**：……这样频繁地施展神秘术，对您的眼睛并不好。\
**Tuesday**: Using arcane skills so frequently is bad for your eyes.

**蓝手帕**：您的长辈没有告诉过您吗？\
**Tuesday**: Didn't your family ever tell you that?

侍应生的声音中不无担忧。\
Her voice carries genuine concern.

**阿尔古斯**：所以你什么都知道。\
**Argus**: So you knew what we were doing all along.

**蓝手帕**：哈，您这样大张旗鼓地动作，当然会让所有人都知道……\
**Tuesday**: Ha, of course. You weren't exactly subtle in your actions. What did you expect?

**蓝手帕**：这就是您的极限……\
**Tuesday**: But you've reached your limit now.

**蓝手帕**：三。\
**Tuesday**: Three.

**阿尔古斯**：……什么？\
**Argus**: What's that supposed to mean?

**蓝手帕**：二。\
**Tuesday**: Two.

**阿尔古斯**：该死的，我知道，故弄玄虚向来是你的拿手好戏……\
**Argus**: Tsk, screw this. Your mind games won't work on me.

**蓝手帕**：一。\
**Tuesday**: One.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

雇佣兵眼中的辉光在一瞬间熄灭。\
The light in the mercenary's eye goes out in an instant.

她的眼睛微微睁大，随后打破了四周如水般的沉默。\
Her eyes widen.

**阿尔古斯**：……灯怎么熄灭了？\
**Argus**: Huh? Who turned the lights off?

**蓝手帕**：……\
**Tuesday**: ...

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

走廊之中的灯光一如往常。\
The hallway lights are as bright as ever.

**蓝手帕**：……灯一直亮着。\
**Tuesday**: The lights are still on, dear.

阿尔古斯并未再说什么，她从口袋中摸出了苦目糖。\
Argus doesn't respond. She pulls a Picrasma candy from her pocket.

她的双手微微颤抖，以致于糖从她的手中滑落，“啪嗒”地掉在了地板上。\
Her hands tremble slightly, causing it to slip from her grasp and fall to the floor with a clack.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

她拾起了糖块，放在了雇佣兵的掌心。\
She picks it up and places it back in Argus's hand.

**维尔汀**：苦目糖不是万能的解药。\
**Vertin**: You rely far too much on Picrasma candy. It can't solve all your problems.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

她吞下糖块，嚼碎，连同其上附着的灰尘。\
She tosses the candy into her mouth and chews it along with the dust from the floor.

**阿尔古斯**：……一般来说，糖块总能很好地发挥它的效用。\
**Argus**: They usually work wonders for me.

**阿尔古斯**：吃一颗，通常能让完全丢失的视野恢复到50%——非常管用。但对于我的工作而言，50%的视野还远远不够用。\
**Argus**: Just one candy restores 50% of my vision. But in my line of work, 50% is never enough.

**阿尔古斯**：所以，这个时候需要再吃下一颗，让视野恢复到100%。\
**Argus**: That's why I take two. I need my vision to be at least 100%.

喉头滚动，口腔传来如预想般的甜蜜。\
She runs the candy along her tongue, and the expected sweetness fills her mouth.

**阿尔古斯**：这可以满足绝大部分的需求，但偶尔也会有些更棘手的任务。\
**Argus**: That'll do the job most of the time, but sometimes I've got an extremely challenging task.

**阿尔古斯**：这个时候需要吃第三颗——需要注意的是，这已经是一个比较危险的数字了……\
**Argus**: That's when I eat a third candy. At that point, it's getting extremely dangerous.

她又往嘴里扔了一颗糖。\
She pops another candy into her mouth.

**阿尔古斯**：按照以往的经验，现在就差不多能够看到东西了。\
**Argus**: I should be able to see now.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

奇迹并没有发生，她的眼睛依旧沉寂，如同星光死尽的夜空。\
No miracle occurs. Her eyes remain still, like a night sky with no stars.

**阿尔古斯**：……是我吃得还不够多吗？\
**Argus**: Sh-Should I take more?

**蓝手帕**：当然——不是。\
**Tuesday**: Absolutely not.

**蓝手帕**：或者说，您正是因为吃得太多了，才会让眼睛在这样关键的时刻派不上用处。\
**Tuesday**: The large amount of candy you've eaten is exactly why your eyes have failed you, and in such a crucial moment, no less.

**蓝手帕**：一切事物都是如此，它们一旦超过合理的限度，反而会引发自身的毁灭——如何掌握这个限度，是值得所有人用一辈子去学习的学问。\
**Tuesday**: Excess leads to destruction. This is true for all things. You'd do well to learn your limits.

**阿尔古斯**：……什么？\
**Argus**: What?

**蓝手帕**：就好像我也总得提防着，不要让那些孩子过于恐惧……\
**Tuesday**: I also had to be careful not to frighten those children too much.

侍应生似乎想起了一些美妙的回忆，雪白的面孔上略带餍足。\
The maid seems to relive some fond memories, a satisfied look on her pale face.

**蓝手帕**：哈……您一直坚定地相信它的作用是吗？\
**Tuesday**: Hmph. You've always put your faith in these candies, haven't you?

**蓝手帕**：一颗糖，50%；两颗糖，100%；三颗糖，用于应付更危险的情况……\
**Tuesday**: One candy, 50% recovery; two candies, 100%; three candies, and you can tackle even the most insurmountable problem.

**蓝手帕**：多么值得信赖呀，这小小的糖果……就像所有人眼中的阿尔古斯，她是那样的伟大，所有的任务只要到了她的手上，保准能够被搞定。\
**Tuesday**: Oh, how dependable they are! Just like the venerable Argus who succeeds in any job she takes on!

侍应生咯咯直笑。\
She chuckles.

**蓝手帕**：哈哈……\
**Tuesday**: Heh heh.

**蓝手帕**：正是因为您一直相信着它……才赢来了如此盛大的毁灭。\
**Tuesday**: It's precisely your excessive confidence in these candies that has led to your marvelous destruction.

**蓝手帕**：就像那些镇民的信任……反而使一个人走向了万劫不复的深渊。噢，真是可怜的家伙。\
**Tuesday**: Just as the people's trust in you as a mercenary has led you to this bottomless abyss. Oh, you poor thing.

**蓝手帕**：他们当然也不会想到……所谓的百眼巨人，竟然是一个盲目的瞎子！\
**Tuesday**: And of course, they'd never have imagined this. Argus, the mercenary named after the hundred-eyed, all-seeing giant, is in fact a blind fool!

**阿尔古斯**：你他*的又是谁？！\
**Argus**: Who the hell are you?!

她向着声音的来源狠狠地扣下了扳机，耳边的枪声振聋发聩。\
She fires in the direction of her voice, the gunshot ringing in their ears.

**？？？**：——！\
**???**: —!

墙壁上出现了深深的弹痕，整座旅馆发出了古怪的嚎叫。\
The bullet pierces the wall, and a strange wail echoes through the halls of the motel.

**阿尔古斯**：该死的，该死的……\
**Argus**: Damn it! Damn it!

**蓝手帕**：哈，没打中呢。\
**Tuesday**: Hahaheh. Missed me.

她极力地压抑着过于活跃的交感神经，颤抖的手指在自己的手背上掐下了一道道红痕。\
She digs her fingers into her hand as she tries to control her trembling.

**蓝手帕**：……嗯。\
**Tuesday**: Uhn.

她轻巧地掂着步子，将心口抵在了枪管上。\
She steps forward, pushing her chest against the barrel of the gun.

**蓝手帕**：这下好啦，一切都对得整整齐齐的。\
**Tuesday**: There you go. Now there's no way you can miss.
