**蓝手帕**：只是您按得下扳机吗？\
**Tuesday**: But do you have the guts to pull the trigger?

她微微侧首，嘴角含笑。\
She tilts her head slightly, smiling.

**蓝手帕**：这一切的决定权在您的手上……不过，我死了以后，您可就再也找不到707了。\
**Tuesday**: The decision's yours to make, but once I'm dead, you'll never find room 707.

**蓝手帕**：数羊羔、凯拉……都在那个房间，不是吗？\
**Tuesday**: Barbara, Kayla, everything you're looking for is all in that room, isn't it?

**阿尔古斯**：——别用你那脏嘴叫她的名字！\
**Argus**: Don't you dare say her name with that filthy mouth!

**蓝手帕**：为什么呢？凯拉小姐是一个很好的住客，我很喜欢她。\
**Tuesday**: But why? Ms. Kayla's such a lovely guest. I've very much enjoyed her company.

侍应生饶有兴味地看着雇佣兵的面孔，后者正因愤怒而变得扭曲。\
The maid looks at the mercenary's face with interest as it twists in rage.

**维尔汀**：……够了。\
**Vertin**: Enough.

**维尔汀**：我想，我们需要好好谈谈。\
**Vertin**: You and I need to have a serious talk.

**蓝手帕**：噢，小姐，没有这个必要了……\
**Tuesday**: Oh, there's no need for that.

**蓝手帕**：我的孩子很想见见您。\
**Tuesday**: Actually, my baby's eager to meet you.

**维尔汀**：……孩子？\
**Vertin**: Your baby?

她的目光投向了侍应生怀中的襁褓。\
She looks at the bundle of swaddling cloth in the maid's arms.

**蓝手帕**：嗯，事实上，它才是这个旅馆的主人……\
**Tuesday**: Yes. In fact, the baby is the master of this motel.

她将襁褓塞入了维尔汀的怀中。\
She holds out the bundle.

**蓝手帕**：所以我想……您应当先和它打个招呼——抱住它。\
**Tuesday**: I think the two of you ought to meet each other first. Here, hold it.

襁褓的分量远比她想象的要轻——这并不是一个孩子的重量。\
She places it in her arms. The bundle is much lighter than she expected—not the weight of a child.

**维尔汀**：这是……\
**Vertin**: This is ...

她恍惚间看见脚下的地毯翻滚为泥沼，而蓝手帕立于泥沼之上，满含微笑地看着她。\
She sees the carpet beneath her feet transform into a quagmire. Tuesday stands on top of the mud, smiling at her.

**阿尔古斯**：维尔汀？维尔汀！\
**Argus**: Vertin? Vertin!

她的双耳仿佛浸入水中，雇佣兵的呼喊如同身处彼岸。\
The mercenary's shouts are dulled. It's as if she's been plunged under water.

急切的脚步声自远处传来，而手中的那个襁褓沉重得如同铅坠。\
She hears hurried footsteps approaching from a distance and feels the once-light bundle become as heavy as lead.

——有什么东西没过了脚踝，她一直在下沉，仿佛要自此坠入一个无明的世界。\
Something engulfs her ankles, pulling her down, down, down into a world of endless darkness.

**阿尔古斯**：放开它，维尔汀！\
**Argus**: Let go of it, Vertin!

一枚青绿色的火焰挣扎着亮起，雇佣兵匍匐在地上，紧紧地拉住了她的手。\
An emerald flame struggles to light up, and the mercenary, lying on the ground, tightly grabs her hand.

**阿尔古斯**：该死的，我从来没有做过这么亏本的买卖——\
**Argus**: I ain't letting our deal end this way! Not while I draw breath!

**维尔汀**：阿尔古斯……\
**Vertin**: Argus ...

**阿尔古斯**：——啊！\
**Argus**: Aaargh!

属于侍应生的皮靴轻轻地碾住了雇佣兵的手指，后者发出了惨痛的叫声。\
The maid presses her foot against Argus's fingers and steps down. Argus screams in pain.

**蓝手帕**：别做多余的事。\
**Tuesday**: Don't you interrupt them.

**蓝手帕**：——维尔汀小姐，无需担忧，这是必要的过程。\
**Tuesday**: There's no need to worry, Ms. Vertin. I've done this countless times.

**蓝手帕**：让我来看看你的梦。\
**Tuesday**: Now, allow me to peer into your dreams.

## THH-17 小水洼 / The Puddle on the Road

世间的响声越来越远，她再次睁开了眼睛，目所能及之处尽为黑夜。\
The sounds of the world fade into total silence, and when she opens her eyes again, there is nothing but darkness.

**维尔汀**：这是……哪里？\
**Vertin**: Where am I?

啪嗒。\
*plop*

一粒冰凉的水珠落到了她的鼻尖。\
A cool drop of water falls on her nose.

**维尔汀**：下雨了？\
**Vertin**: Is that rain?

**“圈环”**：我能用圈环勾住任何东西。\
**"The Ring"**: I can catch anything with a toss.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**伊莎贝拉**：维尔汀，你这次喊我们过来，也是为了这一件事吧？\
**Isabella**: Vertin, that's why you've gathered us here, right?

**维尔汀**：……你们不是属于这里的人。\
**Vertin**: You shouldn't be here.

**伊莎贝拉**：你会理解我们的，对吗，维尔汀？\
**Isabella**: You understand what we desire most, right, Vertin?

四周响起了下雨的淅沥声，孩子们好奇地张望着。\
The falling rain surrounds them. The children watch curiously.

**“圈环”**：维尔汀，我们成功了吗？\
**"The Ring"**: Vertin, we made it, right?

**伊莎贝拉**：可是为什么雨还在下？\
**Isabella**: But why is it still raining?

**“圈环”**：伊莎贝拉，不要大惊小怪，只是下雨，你难道没见过下雨吗？\
**"The Ring"**: Don't be such a baby, Isabella. Haven't you seen rain before?

孩子们伸出了手，企图接住那些坠落的雨珠。\
The children reach out as they try to catch the raindrops in their hands.

**维尔汀**：——不！\
**Vertin**: No!

**蓝手帕**：……您害怕孩子和雨？\
**Tuesday**: Are you afraid of children? Or rain?

熟悉的声音于黑暗之中回荡。\
A familiar voice echoes in the darkness.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：不，我并不害怕这些。\
**Vertin**: No, I'm not afraid of them.

**维尔汀**：雨水是最常见不过的东西——世界上总有一些地方会在下雨。\
**Vertin**: Rain is common. It's always falling somewhere in the world.

**维尔汀**：……只是雨水而已。\
**Vertin**: It's merely an ordinary weather phenomenon.

侍应生微笑着打了一个响指，所有的雨滴自半空停止后，逆流而上。\
The maid snaps her fingers. The raindrops halt, then start to flow upward.

**蓝手帕**：您所害怕的是这样的雨，对吗？\
**Tuesday**: This is the kind of rain you're afraid of, isn't it?

**蓝手帕**：我从来没有见过倒着的雨，这是来自于您的想象力吗？……但我实在想不明白，倒着的雨有什么值得害怕的呢？\
**Tuesday**: Hmm, I've never seen rain fall upwards. Is this some creation of your imagination? Still, I don't see why you'd be afraid of rain falling in reverse.

**蓝手帕**：——好孩子，您能够为我解答吗？\
**Tuesday**: Would you care to enlighten me, dear child?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：蓝手帕小姐，您应当停止这些无谓的尝试，然后告诉我阿尔古斯在哪里。\
**Vertin**: Ms. Tuesday, please. Stop trying to get in my head, and tell me where Argus is.

侍应生置若罔闻，她反而更凑近了些。\
The maid ignores her and steps closer.

**蓝手帕**：……在遇见您之前，我从不相信世界上存在一个没有恐惧的人。\
**Tuesday**: Before I met you, I never thought that a person without fear could exist in the world.

**蓝手帕**：我也从来没有猜错过人们所恐惧的东西……您是如此的特别。\
**Tuesday**: I've never once guessed someone's fear incorrectly, either. You really are something else.

**维尔汀**：您没有猜错。\
**Vertin**: You didn't guess incorrectly.

**维尔汀**：这些逆流而上的雨滴，带来了最紊乱的时代。人们在夹缝中求生，被时代的巨轮碾成微末的灰尘。\
**Vertin**: These reversed raindrops have brought utter chaos to the world, pulverizing people under the crushing wheel of time.

**维尔汀**：您应该庆幸您没有见过这样的雨水。\
**Vertin**: You should be thankful you've never seen it.

**维尔汀**：但是现在，它们不会再是我们前进的阻碍。\
**Vertin**: But it can't stop us anymore.

**维尔汀**：因为伞就在这儿。\
**Vertin**: Because the umbrella's here.

她撑开了伞。\
She opens the umbrella.

**维尔汀**：至少在“暴雨”之中，我能为同伴们撑起这一把伞。\
**Vertin**: At least now, when the "Storm" comes, I can hold up the umbrella and protect my companions.

**维尔汀**：……虽然这个时刻来得太晚了，但好在我们还有未来。\
**Vertin**: And although this ability has come too late for some, we still have a future to protect.

**蓝手帕**：……\
**Tuesday**: ...

**维尔汀**：……您为什么如此执着于人们心中的恐惧？这本来不是什么重要的事，何至于使您双手发抖、战栗不止呢。\
**Vertin**: Why are you so obsessed with people's fears? Your hands have been trembling with excitement this whole time.

侍应生的十指交叉着抵在下巴上，面庞如同花朵般红润娇艳。\
The maid clasps her hands under her chin, her face flushed like a blooming flower.

**蓝手帕**：哈……我果然没有看错您……\
**Tuesday**: Haha. So I wasn't wrong at all.

**蓝手帕**：您为什么要去管那个雇佣兵呢？她的确看起来很厉害，但那始终是个空壳子……您吃过夏威夷果吗？只要能打开外面的硬壳，里面便是一览无余的美味……\
**Tuesday**: Why waste your time with that mercenary? She may look tough, but she's hollow inside. Have you ever eaten a macadamia nut? Crack the hard shell, and you'll find the delicious center.

**蓝手帕**：没有人不喜欢香醇而富含油脂的果肉，而恐惧的美味更甚于此……\
**Tuesday**: Who could resist the soft texture and rich flavor of fear?

**维尔汀**：侍应生小姐，该结束了。\
**Vertin**: Ms. Tuesday, this has to end.

**维尔汀**：您就是一切的罪魁祸首，对吗？\
**Vertin**: You're the one pulling the strings here, aren't you?

红晕漫上了侍应生的脸颊，她单手搅动着裙摆。\
The maid blushes as she twirls her skirt with one hand.

**蓝手帕**：噢，真令人意外，这样的指控……\
**Tuesday**: Oh, what an astounding accusation.

**蓝手帕**：不、不过，我很开心，我想我从来没有这样的开心过……\
**Tuesday**: But, oh, do I feel so, so gratified. I've never felt so satiated in my entire life!

她的灵魂似乎陷入了某种奇异的震颤。\
Her very being seems to be caught in a strange tremor.

**蓝手帕**：您……！您是唯一一个看见了我的人……多么的不可思议……\
**Tuesday**: Oh, you! You're the only one who's ever seen through me! How exhilarating!

**蓝手帕**：但有一点，您说得不对……\
**Tuesday**: However, your accusation missed the mark.

她伸出了自己的双手，那双手在雨幕之下显得格外洁白。\
She stretches out her hands. They look especially pure under the rain.

**蓝手帕**：您看见了吗？它们如此干净，从未沾染上一丝血迹……\
**Tuesday**: You see my hands? They're immaculate—never once tainted by a single drop of blood.

**蓝手帕**：这正是我引以为傲的一点……您瞧瞧，我几乎什么也不用做，那些恐惧就源源不断地产生了……\
**Tuesday**: I take great pride in it. You see, I barely do anything to make people's fears arise.

面前的手掌因为主人的兴奋而略显痉挛。\
Her hands tremble with excitement.

**蓝手帕**：哈，我怎么会去伤害别人呢……通过伤害而产生的恐惧，最为简单，也最为低劣。\
**Tuesday**: Ha, I would never injure anyone. Fear created through physical harm is its crudest and most base form.

**蓝手帕**：我要那恐惧的阴影永远离不开他们的心房……\
**Tuesday**: What I crave is the fear that lingers in their hearts forever.

侍应生的脸颊透出了淡淡的粉色。\
The maid's cheeks flush a faint pink.

**蓝手帕**：即使在多年以后，他们向朋友或亲人讲述其亲身经历的事……每个人的心中都会留下一颗种子……\
**Tuesday**: The kind of fear that, even years later, when they recount their experiences here to their friends and families, a seed of fear is planted in the listeners' hearts.

**蓝手帕**：啊，哈哈……\
**Tuesday**: Ahh, haha.

**蓝手帕**：我将给予他们恐惧，而他们也将成为我可爱的孩子。\
**Tuesday**: I instill fear in my guests, and they become my beloved children.

雨幕之中，她的手指不受控制地颤抖着，被濡湿的脸上露出了无比美丽的笑容。\
In the rain, her fingers tremble uncontrollably, and a beautiful smile spreads across her wet face.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：——阿尔古斯在哪里？\
**Vertin**: Where is she? Where's Argus?

**蓝手帕**：噢……我想，她正在经历自身的恐惧——很难想象吗？这样一位雇佣兵，居然也有害怕的东西……\
**Tuesday**: Well, I suppose she's experiencing her own fears right now. Under that hard mercenary exterior, she's tormented by them. Can you imagine that?

**维尔汀**：蓝手帕小姐，抱歉。\
**Vertin**: Sorry, Ms. Tuesday.

**维尔汀**：……我对这些不感兴趣。\
**Vertin**: But I'm not interested in this vile obsession of yours.

**蓝手帕**：——！\
**Tuesday**: —!

撑着伞的身影，向着更深的黑暗处走去了。\
The one with the umbrella walks deeper into the darkness.

空气中传来了鸟的鸣叫，她看到了熟悉的原野。\
The sound of birds chirping fills the air. Argus is back home—on those familiar plains.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

**阿尔古斯**：这是……\
**Argus**: This is ...

她站在一无所有的荒野中，迎面而来的只有风与草叶的晃动。\
She stands in the field, nothing but the wind and the rustling grass before her.

**镇民Ⅰ**：啊呀，阿尔古斯，太久没有见到你了。大伙儿都以为你不会回来了。\
**Resident I**: Howdy, Argus, long time no see. We thought you'd never come back.

**阿尔古斯**：丹尼斯叔叔……你怎么在这儿？\
**Argus**: Mr. Dennis? Why are you here?

**镇民Ⅰ**：阿尔古斯，你看看你说的是什么话？为什么我不能在这儿？\
**Resident I**: Oh boy, you listening to yourself? Why wouldn't I be here?

**镇民Ⅰ**：尤其是我的女儿还在今天结婚了！\
**Resident I**: It's my daughter's wedding day!

**阿尔古斯**：什么……恭喜……\
**Argus**: Huh? W-Well, congratulations.

她那近乎于木僵的脑袋终于转过了弯。\
She finally catches on.

**阿尔古斯**：可是……你不应该在这里。\
**Argus**: But, you really shouldn't be here.

**阿尔古斯**：你不记得了吗？三年前你的女儿离家出走……\
**Argus**: Don't you remember? Three years ago, your daughter ran away from home.

**阿尔古斯**：她留下了一封书信，和谢弗先生一起去了东部……大概是底特律？我记不太清楚了。\
**Argus**: She left a letter and then went with Mr. Shaffer to a city in the northeast, Detroit, I think? I don't quite remember.

**镇民Ⅰ**：得了吧，别开玩笑了。\
**Resident I**: Oh, come on, quit fooling around.

**阿尔古斯**：……我花了三个月找到了她，她不肯回来，于是我只能把这个消息告诉你……后来，你自己去了底特律……\
**Argus**: After three months of searching, I found her, but she refused to come back with me. So, you went to Detroit yourself.

**阿尔古斯**：然后你……\
**Argus**: And then, you ...

她忽然打住了话头。\
Her words drift off.

丹尼斯为了寻找自己的女儿，死在了底特律——她的记忆这样告诉她。\
Dennis died in Detroit while looking for his daughter. At least, that's what she remembers.

**DENNIS**：(1938–1987)R.I.P.\
**DENNIS**: (1938–1987)R.I.P.

但眼前的事实却与回忆相差甚大。那个被宣告死去的男人正殷切地望着她。\
But, how can that be? He's right here, standing in front of her.

**阿尔古斯**：总之，非常抱歉，我没能把她带回来……\
**Argus**: In any case, I'm sorry I couldn't bring her back.

**镇民Ⅰ**：阿尔古斯，你在说什么呢！\
**Resident I**: What're you talking about, Argus?

**镇民Ⅰ**：看来你真是累着了，说了这么多颠三倒四的话！我早就和其他人说过，不该让你干太多的活！\
**Resident I**: You must be tired from working on all those requests that the townsfolk have pushed upon you. I've told them so many times to go easy on you!

**镇民Ⅰ**：我当然有一个新的委托给你！\
**Resident I**: That said, I have a request for you myself!

**阿尔古斯**：是什么？找寻走失的牛羊，还是……\
**Argus**: What is it? Did you lose some livestock or—

镇民朝她挤了挤眼睛，将一封请柬塞到了她的手心。\
The townsman winks and hands her an invitation.

**镇民Ⅰ**：爱丽丝今天结婚了，如果你有空，欢迎你来！\
**Resident I**: Come to Alice's wedding!

**镇民Ⅰ**：我们准备了足量的麦酒、鹰嘴豆泥，还有礼拜堂的唱诗班——一定得来看看，好姑娘。\
**Resident I**: We've prepared plenty of food and beer. And we've got the chapel choir together. Don't miss out, missy!

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

**阿尔古斯**：抱歉，我不去了。\
**Argus**: Sorry, I won't be there.

**镇民Ⅰ**：为什么？\
**Resident I**: Why?

为什么呢？\
Why, Argus?

**阿尔古斯**：我接到了玛丽姨妈的委托，要去给她的丈夫送信——她腿脚不好，你知道的。\
**Argus**: I-I need to deliver a letter to, to Mrs. Mary's husband. She can't go herself because of her bad legs, you see.

**镇民Ⅱ**：哎呀，阿尔古斯，我可没让你去送信呀。\
**Resident II**: Hey, Argus. I didn't ask you to deliver any letters.

**阿尔古斯**：……玛丽姨妈，您不是……\
**Argus**: Mrs. Mary, didn't you ...?

眼前的人应当在1989年寿终正寝，阿尔古斯记得自己曾亲眼目睹她的灵柩被埋入土中。\
Mary passed away in 1989. Argus saw her coffin being lowered into the ground.

**MARY**：(1945–1989)R.I.P.\
**MARY**: (1945–1989)R.I.P.

另一个被宣告死亡的人，如今正笑意盈盈地立在她的眼前，殷切地望着她。\
Another person declared dead is now standing before her, smiling brightly.

**阿尔古斯**：您还活着……？\
**Argus**: You're still alive?

**镇民Ⅱ**：瞧瞧，这说的是什么话！这孩子真是忙糊涂了。\
**Resident II**: What kind of nonsense are you spouting?! You really ought to take a proper rest.

**镇民Ⅱ**：今天是爱丽丝的好日子，我们都应该去参加她的婚礼，不是吗？\
**Resident II**: Today's Alice's big day. We should all be at her wedding, don't you think?

**镇民Ⅱ**：……好孩子，你的手为什么在抖？\
**Resident II**: Oh, my sweet child, why are your hands shaking?

**阿尔古斯**：我……\
**Argus**: I ...

**镇民Ⅱ**：你为此而害怕吗？可是你为什么会害怕？\
**Resident II**: Are you afraid? Why?

**镇民Ⅱ**：你害怕他们变得幸福？\
**Resident II**: Are you afraid of their happiness?

**镇民Ⅱ**：还是……你害怕自己是个废物？\
**Resident II**: Or are you afraid of your failure?

**阿尔古斯**：……我不是。\
**Argus**: I'm not a failure!

**镇民Ⅱ**：噢，好孩子。\
**Resident II**: Oh, my sweet child.

**镇民Ⅰ**：阿尔古斯，阿尔古斯，如果你要送信，就去找阿尔古斯。\
**Resident I**: Argus! Argus! Got a message to send? Go get Argus, your trusted friend!

**镇民Ⅱ**：阿尔古斯，阿尔古斯，如果你要捉奸，就去找阿尔古斯。\
**Resident II**: Argus! Argus! Got a cheating spouse to catch? Go get Argus; she's got your back!

**？？？**：阿尔古斯，阿尔古斯……\
**???**: Argus ... Argus ...

并不属于镇子的声音在周围响起。\
A foreign voice echoes through their mouths and surrounds her.

**阿尔古斯**：——谁！\
**Argus**: Who's there?!

眼前的一切如潮水般退去，唯有一个少女伫立在她的面前。\
Her surroundings recede like a tide, leaving only a girl in white standing before her.

半裹着胎衣的羔羊卧在她的脚边。她的双手沾满了羊水与血迹，脸上的笑容纯洁如白鸽。\
Wrapped in a half-soiled birth cloth, a lamb lies at her feet. The girl's hands are covered in blood and amniotic fluid. Her smile is as pure as a dove.

**凯拉**：是我呀，阿尔古斯，你忘记我了吗？\
**Kayla**: It's me, Kayla. You haven't forgotten me, have you?

**阿尔古斯**：凯拉……\
**Argus**: Kayla ...

**凯拉**：天要黑了，我们得带着它们回去——在母羊受伤的情况下，它们一定活不过今晚。\
**Kayla**: It's getting dark. We should take them back. Ain't no way they'll make it through the night out here with their mama hurt.

**凯拉**：更何况，天一黑，你的眼睛就什么都看不见了。\
**Kayla**: And you can't see a thing at night.

**阿尔古斯**：是的，我们得回去了——不能再拖延。\
**Argus**: Yeah, we need to go back now. Can't delay any longer.

**凯拉**：噢……\
**Kayla**: Oh.

**阿尔古斯**：怎么了？\
**Argus**: What?

**凯拉**：你还得等等我……\
**Kayla**: Hold on a moment.

羊羔发出了咩咩的叫声。\
The lamb bleats.

**阿尔古斯**：这是要干什么？\
**Argus**: What are you doing?

**凯拉**：别怕，别怕……\
**Kayla**: There, there.

她那双沾满羊水的手轻柔地抚上了小羊的脖颈，羊羔俯下头，舔舐着她冰冷的指尖。\
She kneels down and gently strokes the lamb's neck. The lamb bows its head and licks her fingertips. They're still wet with amniotic fluid.

凯拉微笑着收紧了手掌，羊羔发出了凄厉的惨叫，惊起了远方的候鸟。\
Kayla smiles and tightens her grip around the lamb's neck. It lets out a piercing cry, sending a distant flock of birds into the air.

——这叫声并未持续多久，因为羊羔很快就被那双手扼死在了草地里。\
The cry becomes weaker, more strangled, and then silent as the life is squeezed out of its body.

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

**凯拉**：你看，相比于在荒原中承受豺狼的撕咬，能如此短暂地死去，岂不是一件幸运的事？\
**Kayla**: Isn't it better to die a quick death than end up in the belly of a wolf?

**阿尔古斯**：……你没有资格替它决定这些。\
**Argus**: You've got no right to make that decision.

**阿尔古斯**：没有什么东西是为了死去而降生在这世上的……它原本可以站起来……\
**Argus**: No living thing is born to simply die. It could've stood up. It could've survived.

少女自荒草丛中起身。\
The girl gets to her feet.

**凯拉**：现在我们可以走了。\
**Kayla**: We can go now.

**阿尔古斯**：……你不能走。\
**Argus**: No, don't go.

白衣的女孩面带微笑，田野间的微风吹拂着她的裙摆，发出猎猎的响声。\
The girl smiles as the long grass rustles against her flowing skirt in the breeze.

**凯拉**：……你提醒我了。\
**Kayla**: Oh, you've reminded me.

**凯拉**：还有两个大麻烦没有解决呢……你看看那两个人……\
**Kayla**: There are two problems left unsolved. Those two over there.

雇佣兵向远处望去，丹尼斯叔叔与玛丽姨妈正向着她微笑。\
Argus looks into the distance. Dennis and Mary are standing and smiling at her.

**凯拉**：你得帮我杀了他们，只需要两颗子弹，费不了多少时间……\
**Kayla**: Kill them. It would only take two bullets. Three seconds max.

**凯拉**：人只要活着，就是一件麻烦事——他们会穷追不舍地追着你，就像你对待你的任务目标那样。\
**Kayla**: As long as they're alive, they'll come after you just as hard as you hunt the targets of your missions.

**凯拉**：你应该比我更清楚这些。\
**Kayla**: I'm sure you know that better than I do.

**阿尔古斯**：……为什么？\
**Argus**: Why should I kill them?

**凯拉**：这需要什么理由吗？\
**Kayla**: Do you need a reason?

**凯拉**：就按照以前那样——我说，你做，你什么也不需要思考，这不就是你所引以为傲的东西吗？\
**Kayla**: Just do as we've always done. I say, and you do. No need to think about it. Isn't that what you pride yourself on?

**凯拉**：没有自我意识和选择，成为一个彻头彻尾的工具——这就是一个雇佣兵所需要做的一切。\
**Kayla**: A mindless tool that blindly follows orders. That's all a mercenary needs to be.

**凯拉**：——也是你一直标榜的自我价值……\
**Kayla**: Isn't that the so-called value of a mercenary that you always talk about?

**阿尔古斯**：不，不是的……\
**Argus**: No, it ain't true.

**凯拉**：实际上，你也并没有那么好心，对吗？你才不在乎别人的性命呢。\
**Kayla**: What's with the hesitation, anyway? It's not like you give a damn about other people's lives.

**凯拉**：不肯对叔叔和婶婶下手，也只是因为杀死了他们，你就再也无法听到那些漂亮话了……\
**Kayla**: The only reason you can't bring yourself to kill them is because you enjoy how they always praise you and depend on you.

**阿尔古斯**：你不是凯拉。\
**Argus**: You ain't Kayla.

**凯拉**：只因为不符合你的期待，你就要彻底地否认我的存在吗？\
**Kayla**: Seriously? Are you saying I'm a fraud just because I don't meet your expectations of what I'm supposed to be?

白衣少女露出意味不明的笑容。\
The girl gives an inexplicable smile.

**凯拉**：既然你认为我不是凯拉，那你为什么不杀了我？\
**Kayla**: Fine. If you think I'm not Kayla, then why don't you kill me now?

**凯拉**：只要你对着我的心脏开枪，这些人都会把你当做英雄——他们会在田野里举着火把，高呼你的名字……\
**Kayla**: Just shoot me in the chest, and these people will treat you like a hero. They'll gather in the fields, holding torches, and chant your name.

雇佣兵赫然举起了枪，然而枪管颤抖——她已经丧失了瞄准目标的能力。\
Argus abruptly raises her gun, but her hands are shaking—the barrel trembling.

**凯拉**：阿尔古斯，阿尔古斯，你胆小又懦弱。\
**Kayla**: Argus! Argus! She's spineless!

**凯拉**：阿尔古斯，阿尔古斯……\
**Kayla**: Argus! Argus! She's—

砰——！\
*bang*

阿尔古斯，阿尔古斯……\
Argus! Argus!

**阿尔古斯**：……！\
**Argus**: ...!

子弹贯穿了少女柔软的胸脯，血迹泼洒，如同在原野上燃烧的花朵。\
The bullet pierces the girl's soft chest. Her blood splatters on the field, dotting the grass like a smattering of poppies.

鲜血的份量如此沉重，使簇生的草叶谦卑地弯下了腰。\
It clings to the grass, its weight causing the blades to bend.

**镇民Ⅰ**：噢！阿尔古斯，你是我们的英雄！\
**Resident I**: Oh, Argus! Our great hero!

**镇民Ⅱ**：我们会高呼你的名字，将你的事迹代代相传！\
**Resident II**: The tales of your heroic deeds will be passed down through generations!

**阿尔古斯**：……\
**Argus**: ...

**阿尔古斯**：她不是凯拉。\
**Argus**: She ain't Kayla.

**镇民Ⅰ**：噢！事到如今，您又开始自己骗自己了……她当然是凯拉！\
**Resident I**: Now, now, you're lying to yourself again. Of course she's Kayla!

**阿尔古斯**：不可能。\
**Argus**: It's not possible.

**镇民Ⅱ**：您又在嘴硬了！难道非得把她的心掏给您看，您才愿意相信吗？！\
**Resident II**: Do I need to show you the bullet through her heart for you to believe it, bonehead?!

**阿尔古斯**：——该死的！\
**Argus**: Damn it!

子弹落入枪匣，发出清脆的响声。\
She loads a bullet into the chamber with a crisp click.

**维尔汀**：——别开枪！\
**Vertin**: Don't pull the trigger!

未曾预料的声音从耳边传来。\
An unexpected voice comes from beside her.

**阿尔古斯**：……维尔汀？\
**Argus**: Vertin?

本不该出现在此处的人站在了雇佣兵的身侧，令她产生了轻微的倒错感。\
How did she get all the way out here? Where did she come from?

**维尔汀**：阿尔古斯，冷静。\
**Vertin**: Calm down, Argus.

**维尔汀**：别忘了，你所看见的都不是真实。至少现在，你依然身处于旅馆之中。\
**Vertin**: Remember, what you see isn't real. You're still inside the motel, at least for now.

……\
...

**镇民Ⅰ**：哦，又来了一个小姑娘……\
**Resident I**: Oh, here comes another little lady.

**镇民Ⅱ**：——来得正好，一起来参加我们的聚会吧！\
**Resident II**: Excellent timing. Come join the party!

**阿尔古斯**：……维尔汀？\
**Argus**: Vertin?

**维尔汀**：我是来接你出去的。\
**Vertin**: I'm here to get you out.

**阿尔古斯**：……所以，那不是凯拉。\
**Argus**: So, that wasn't Kayla.

雇佣兵长长地舒了一口气，为这一瞬的犹豫与错乱。\
She lets out a long sigh of relief.

**阿尔古斯**：这很好，再好不过了……\
**Argus**: Couldn't ask for better news than that, really.

**维尔汀**：那不是凯拉。\
**Vertin**: No, it wasn't.

**维尔汀**：我们要离开这儿。\
**Vertin**: Let's get out of here.

她伸出手，如同一个邀请。\
She reaches out her hand in invitation.

**阿尔古斯**：——好。\
**Argus**: Okay.

雇佣兵伸出了手——她总觉得身后有什么可憎的东西正在追逐着她，只要她停下脚步，那片名为迷茫的阴影就会将她吞噬。\
Argus reaches out. She feels like something abominable is chasing after her—that if she stops, the shadow of confusion will come and swallow her whole.

而眼前的那只手，正是迷境中唯一的救赎——于是她不假思索地握紧了它。\
And this hand is her only salvation—her escape from this labyrinth—so she grasps it tightly.

**阿尔古斯**：她不是凯拉。\
**Argus**: She ain't Kayla.

雇佣兵无比肯定地宣布了判决。\
She declares this with absolute certainty.

## THH-18 不眠夜 / Sleepless Night

旅馆的走廊寂静如常，微笑的侍应生静立在旁。\
The motel hallway is as quiet as ever. The maid stands, smiling.

**蓝手帕**：你们见到它了吗？\
**Tuesday**: Did you see it?

**维尔汀**：……它？\
**Vertin**: It?

**蓝手帕**：噢，就是我的孩子……看来它并没有在你们的面前现身，真是一个胆小的家伙。\
**Tuesday**: My baby, of course. Oh, so it didn't show up, then? What a shy little pumpkin!

**阿尔古斯**：……它是什么东西？\
**Argus**: What is it exactly?

**蓝手帕**：它是一个懵懂的超自然存在，一切怪谈的集合体，一颗砰砰直跳的心脏，也是一个胆小又可爱的孩子……\
**Tuesday**: A supernatural being, an amalgam of urban legends, an ever-pounding heart, and a shy little baby—all under one roof.

**蓝手帕**：不过，既然能从那儿出来，就意味着你们已经获得了它的同意——进来吧，我会带你们去看旅馆里最可爱的小房间。\
**Tuesday**: But seeing how you got out of there in one piece, I'm certain you've already earned its approval. Come on in. I'll show you the sweetest little room in the motel.

她的身后赫然出现了一扇鲜红的门扉。\
A red door appears behind her.

**蓝手帕**：别怕，孩子，开门。\
**Tuesday**: Don't be afraid, sweetheart. Go ahead. Open the door.

门扉纹丝不动。\
The door remains motionless.

**蓝手帕**：开门。\
**Tuesday**: Open it. Now.

雇佣兵一言不发，只是沉默地擦拭着枪管。\
The mercenary says nothing. She silently wipes the barrel of her gun.

砰、砰——！\
*bang-bang*

她举起了枪，向着那扇红色的门扉射出了两发子弹。\
She fires two shots at the red door.

整座旅馆发出了剧烈的颤抖。\
The entire motel trembles violently.

**阿尔古斯**：这才是最管用的。\
**Argus**: That'll do it.

她再次为枪支上好了子弹。然而走廊之内，忽然传来了巨大的回响声。\
Before she can reload, the ground starts to shake beneath her feet, and a deafening sound reverberates through the hallway.

侍应生略为惊异地睁大了眼睛。\
The maid's eyes widen in surprise.

**蓝手帕**：是啊，我怎么没有想到呢。\
**Tuesday**: Why didn't I think of that?

**蓝手帕**：您的眼睛还没恢复吧？准头这样的差。\
**Tuesday**: Your eyes haven't recovered yet, have they? Tsk, Tsk. Such poor aim.

**蓝手帕**：让我来帮你吧。\
**Tuesday**: Let me lend you a hand.

**蓝手帕**：要听妈妈的话……\
**Tuesday**: Listen to Mama.

**蓝手帕**：很早就告诉过你，不听话的后果。\
**Tuesday**: I told you long ago about the consequences of disobedience.

**蓝手帕**：哎呀，没子弹了……您能帮我再上一次子弹吗？\
**Tuesday**: Oh, it's out of bullets. Could you help me reload?

**蓝手帕**：噢……乖孩子。\
**Tuesday**: Oh, my sweet child.

**蓝手帕**：您看见了吗？这正是恐惧的魅力……\
**Tuesday**: Can you see it? This is the beauty of fear.

**阿尔古斯**：小心！\
**Argus**: Watch out!

**蓝手帕**：请进吧，客人们。\
**Tuesday**: Please, come in, my dear guests.

**蓝手帕**：——你们会在里面找到你们想要的东西。\
**Tuesday**: You'll find what you seek inside.

**蓝手帕**：嗯，在我捡到它的时候，它的名字还叫做“温馨之家”。\
**Tuesday**: When I found it, it was still called Sweet Home.

**蓝手帕**：没有人看管它，它孤零零地伫立在原野中，多么的可怜……\
**Tuesday**: It was all alone, abandoned in the wilderness. The poor little thing.

**维尔汀**：于是你接手了它——这个未知的、尚在形成中的神秘学意识，它常常表现为一座旅馆，但同时也存在于襁褓之中。\
**Vertin**: So you took it in? Some unknown, growing arcane consciousness that takes the form of a motel yet somehow also exists as a baby?

**蓝手帕**：嗯。\
**Tuesday**: Yes.

侍应生俯下身，抱起了地上的襁褓。\
The maid bends down and picks up the swaddled baby from the crib.

**蓝手帕**：乖……\
**Tuesday**: There, there.

**维尔汀**：它已经严重影响了当地居民的生活。\
**Vertin**: But it's seriously impacted the lives of the locals.

**蓝手帕**：噢，维尔汀，他们是自己选择来到这儿的……我也从未阻止他们离开。\
**Tuesday**: Oh, Ms. Vertin, they chose to come here of their own volition. I never forced them to stay.

**维尔汀**：即使他们在日后或是发疯，或是自杀？\
**Vertin**: But after leaving, some of them went mad or even committed suicide.

**蓝手帕**：那是他们自己选择的路。\
**Tuesday**: Well, they made those decisions themselves.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**蓝手帕**：……现在不是该纠结这种问题的时候了，维尔汀小姐。\
**Tuesday**: Now is not the time to dwell on such trivial matters, Ms. Vertin.

**蓝手帕**：您不是一直想要见到数羊羔吗？\
**Tuesday**: Haven't you been searching for Ms. Barbara?

她伸出手，指向那扇洞开的门扉。\
She points to the open door.

**阿尔古斯**：——慢着。\
**Argus**: Don't get any bright ideas, maid.

她枯竭的眼中再次绽放了蓝绿色的光芒，将枪口顶在了蓝手帕的后心。\
Her eye shines emerald again as she presses the barrel of her shotgun against Tuesday's back.

**阿尔古斯**：侍应生，她出了任何的问题，我都会一枪打爆你的心脏。\
**Argus**: If Vertin gets so much as a scratch, I'll blast your chest open.

**阿尔古斯**：连同你的孩子。\
**Argus**: Along with your baby.

**阿尔古斯**：——进去吧，维尔汀，我会替你看着她。\
**Argus**: Go inside, boss. I'll keep an eye on her.

红色的幕布铺满了房间的每一寸空间，一张洁白的象牙床被摆放在房间的中央。\
Red curtains cover every inch of the room, like flesh clinging to a body. An ivory bed stands in the center.

**数羊羔**：我认得您，维尔汀小姐。\
**Barbara**: Here you are, Ms. Vertin.

**数羊羔**：很高兴我并没有和当前的世界断开联络。\
**Barbara**: I'm so glad. I was beginning to think I'd never regain contact with the outside world.

**蓝手帕**：……阿尔古斯小姐，您可以把枪支放下了。\
**Tuesday**: Ms. Argus, you can put your gun down now.

她品味着心跳的余韵，略带颤抖地开口了。\
She speaks, trembling slightly as she savors every moment of her heightened heartrate.

**蓝手帕**：我之前已经展示过足够的诚意了，不是吗……\
**Tuesday**: I've shown my utmost sincerity, have I not?

**阿尔古斯**：闭嘴！\
**Argus**: Shut your trap!

**维尔汀**：……走吧，数羊羔小姐。\
**Vertin**: Let's get out of here, Ms. Barbara.

**维尔汀**：我想，在其他生物的体内说话，总归不是一个好的选择。\
**Vertin**: I don't think it's the wisest choice to have this conversation while we're still inside a living thing.

**维尔汀**：阿尔古斯，我需要你控制着蓝手帕——直到我们离开这里。\
**Vertin**: Argus, I need you to keep Tuesday in check until we make it out of here.

**阿尔古斯**：哈，当然。\
**Argus**: You ain't gotta tell me twice.

一缕光芒斜穿入户，外面正值金色的黎明。\
A beam of light shines in through the window. Dawn is breaking.

**蓝手帕**：我见过无数次相同的景色，却从来没有像今天一样心潮澎湃……\
**Tuesday**: I've gazed at this scenery countless times, but never have I felt as enthralled as today.

**蓝手帕**：不过……维尔汀小姐，您是不是忘了什么？\
**Tuesday**: But, Ms. Vertin, don't you think you've forgotten something?

**维尔汀**：……什么？\
**Vertin**: Forgotten what?

**蓝手帕**：那名与您一起前来的客人……她刚刚来到旅馆，又急匆匆地要去军备工厂，真是一个急性子的孩子。所幸最后，她没有在道路上迷失，又回到了这儿。\
**Tuesday**: That guest who came with you. Shortly after her arrival, she hurried off to that armament factory. She's such an impatient child. Luckily, she made her way back here.

**蓝手帕**：……她的名字叫做红弩箭。\
**Tuesday**: Her name's Lilya, right?

**维尔汀**：……你把她怎么了？\
**Vertin**: What did you do to her?

侍应生轻轻地笑了。\
The maid laughs softly.

**蓝手帕**：……您别着急，她很好——她正在睡着呢，现在，顶多只是做了一个噩梦。\
**Tuesday**: Relax, she's fine. She's sleeping soundly as we speak, with or without nightmares.

**蓝手帕**：您和我一起去见她，我想，她应该很期望在此刻见到您。\
**Tuesday**: Follow me. I'm sure she's eager to see you.

**蓝手帕**：嗯，就是这个房间。\
**Tuesday**: This is the room.

**阿尔古斯**：开门。\
**Argus**: Open it.

侍应生从钥匙串上取下了一把，拧开了门锁。\
The maid finds the key on her keyring, puts it in the lock, and turns it.

房间内空荡荡的。\
The room is empty.

**蓝手帕**：噢……\
**Tuesday**: Oh.

侍应生懊恼地皱起了眉毛。\
The maid frowns, her annoyance visible on her face.

手提箱的主人冲向了窗户边，向下看去。\
The owner of the suitcase rushes to the window and looks down.

飞行女巫正精疲力竭地坐在下方，她们的视线不期然地交汇。\
Lilya is sitting exhausted below. Their eyes meet.

**红弩箭**：维尔汀，终于找到你了——\
**Lilya**: Vertin! There you are!

**红弩箭**：我得向你汇报——重塑之手已经渗透了附近的小镇，我们不能再去那儿了。\
**Lilya**: Listen, those Manus scum have already wormed their way into the town. We can't go there.

**维尔汀**：你的脸色很差。\
**Vertin**: You look terrible.

**红弩箭**：我一夜没睡——那个房间有鬼，一闭上眼睛就会看到很多怪东西。\
**Lilya**: I couldn't sleep at all in that haunted room. Every time I closed my eyes, I saw all kinds of creepy stuff.

**红弩箭**：头儿，你能下来吗？抬着脖子说话很累。\
**Lilya**: Can you come down here, Captain? Talking like this hurts my neck.

**维尔汀**：……好。\
**Vertin**: Okay.

## THH-19 飘 / Gone in the Wind

**红弩箭**：这是……？\
**Lilya**: What's going on?

旅馆之外，柔和的晨曦拂照着大地，飞行员略带疑惑地望向了眼前的人。\
Outside the motel, the rising dawn paints the earth a deep orange. Lilya looks confused as they approach.

**红弩箭**：头儿，你还好吧？\
**Lilya**: Are you okay, Captain?

**维尔汀**：现在没事了。\
**Vertin**: I'm fine.

**维尔汀**：在你离开的时候，有一个好消息和一个坏消息——\
**Vertin**: I have good news and bad news.

**红弩箭**：别让我选一个了，快说吧。\
**Lilya**: Don't bother with the order; just lay it on me.

**维尔汀**：好消息是，我们找到了数羊羔。\
**Vertin**: The good news is we've found Barbara.

**维尔汀**：坏消息是，我们惹上了一个新的麻烦——这个旅馆是一个充满生命力的意识体，它会源源不断地制造怪谈、散播恐惧，也许以后会成为超自然的神秘学家。\
**Vertin**: The bad news is we've got a new problem. This motel is the manifestation of a living consciousness that constantly generates urban legends and spreads fear. It might turn into a supernatural arcanist in the future.

**维尔汀**：这需要严密的监视和管控。我们需要基金会的帮助，不能任由它在此地发展。\
**Vertin**: We can't let it grow here unchecked. We need the help of the Foundation to keep it under control.

**阿尔古斯**：……老板，我的任务已经结束了。现在，我得去镇子上找凯拉。\
**Argus**: Boss, my job here is done. I'm heading into town for Kayla.

她望向更遥远的地方。\
She looks off into the distance.

**阿尔古斯**：噢……我还答应过一个年轻人，要帮他找到他的母亲……\
**Argus**: Oh, and I promised a young fella that I'd help him find his mother.

**阿尔古斯**：我要先走了。\
**Argus**: I've gotta go now.

**维尔汀**：我该怎么把佣金寄给你呢？\
**Vertin**: How do I pay your fee?

**阿尔古斯**：佣金？\
**Argus**: Fee?

雇佣兵爽朗地笑了。\
She laughs heartily.

**阿尔古斯**：我们是朋友，小姐，不需要您再给些别的了。\
**Argus**: We're friends, Vertin. I don't need no payment.

道别之后，她向着永无终点的路走去。\
She says her goodbyes and sets off on the road ahead.

**红弩箭**：好了，头儿，现在打听到兀尔德的消息了吗？\
**Lilya**: Alright, Captain, any progress on finding Urd?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

羊羔动了动她柔软的耳朵。\
The little sheep's ears twitch.

**数羊羔**：这就是你们来找我的目的吗？\
**Barbara**: That's why you came looking for me, right?

**数羊羔**：当然，我可以帮您询问，这并不是什么难事……\
**Barbara**: I'll ask the wind for you. It's the least I can do.

她说着，闭上了眼睛。\
She closes her eyes.

**红弩箭**：……睡着了？\
**Lilya**: Did she doze off?

自原野而来的微风轻柔地吹拂着她柔软的耳朵，如同一缕无形的蛛丝在她的耳边游移。\
The gentle breeze caresses her ears, like an invisible thread being woven between them.

**数羊羔**：我在听……\
**Barbara**: I'm listening.

**数羊羔**：噢……我听见了。\
**Barbara**: Oh, I heard it. The answer.

羊羔睁开了眼睛。\
She opens her eyes.

**数羊羔**：远方的风告诉我，最近一次收到兀尔德女士的投稿，是来自于圣保罗荣军院。\
**Barbara**: A distant wind told me that Ms. Urd's latest submission came from the São Paulo Veterans' Residence.

**数羊羔**：那的确是一篇优秀的稿件，但除此之外的信息，《UTTU》并不知情。\
**Barbara**: The article she submitted was an excellent piece, but UTTU doesn't know anything beyond that.

**维尔汀**：……好。\
**Vertin**: Okay.

**数羊羔**：今晚。你们或许还能够收获一个不错的梦。\
**Barbara**: I suppose we'll all have restful sleep and sweet dreams tonight.

**数羊羔**：我已经为这次的专题访谈收集到了足够的资料……相信这会是一篇很不错的报道。\
**Barbara**: I've collected the material I needed for the upcoming feature interview. I bet the readers will enjoy it.

**数羊羔**：到时候，我也会在编辑栏里署上您的名字——蓝手帕小姐。\
**Barbara**: I'll be sure to include your name on the byline, Ms. Tuesday.

**蓝手帕**：我？可是我并没有做什么呀。\
**Tuesday**: Me? I don't think I contributed anything.

**数羊羔**：不，您的作用出类拔萃……我想，如果不是您，我也并不明白我内心所埋藏着的，这一份对于“失去联络”的恐惧。\
**Barbara**: Quite the contrary, you played a significant role. If it weren't for you, I wouldn't have realized my inner fear of losing communication with the world.

**数羊羔**：身临其境的体验，对于一位编辑而言是绝佳的资料。\
**Barbara**: First-hand experiences like this are invaluable to an editor.

**蓝手帕**：噢，您再这样说下去，我都有些后悔将您放出来了……\
**Tuesday**: Oh, with the way you put it, I almost regret letting you go.

**数羊羔**：您不会再有那样的机会的，因为——访谈结束了。\
**Barbara**: I won't be returning. The interview's over.

洁白的羊羔合上了红色的笔记本。\
She closes her little red notebook.

**数羊羔**：如果顺利的话，您将会在下一期的《UTTU》上阅读到相关的专栏。\
**Barbara**: If all goes well, you'll be able to read about it in the next issue of UTTU.

**数羊羔**：——我也该走了。\
**Barbara**: I'll take my leave now.

**维尔汀**：……再见。\
**Vertin**: Goodbye.

**红弩箭**：很好，我也想赶紧离开这麻烦透顶的鬼地方。\
**Lilya**: Good, I can't wait to leave this place.

**维尔汀**：还没到时候。\
**Vertin**: We can't leave yet.

**维尔汀**：我在刚刚联络了位于德克萨斯的基金会分部，现在他们正用传送术式赶往此处——必须及时调查这个奇特的超自然存在。\
**Vertin**: I just contacted the Texas branch. Their staff is on their way here. They have to investigate this supernatural being as soon as possible.

**红弩箭**：——他们很快就能到，对吗？\
**Lilya**: And they'll be here soon, I presume?

**维尔汀**：附近有传送术式的波动，应该就是他们……\
**Vertin**: I can feel the energy fluctuations of teleportation rituals. It must be them.

她扭头一看，出现在眼前的是一个陌生的身影。\
She turns her head to see a stranger standing before her.

**维尔汀**：……嗯？\
**Vertin**: Mm?

眼前的女孩有着栗色的头发，手臂上挎着一个藤编的篮子。\
The girl in front of her has chestnut hair and carries a woven basket on her arm.

**红弩箭**：——这应当不是圣洛夫基金会的人，头儿。我在镇子上见过她，她叫凯拉。\
**Lilya**: Looks like you guessed wrong, Captain. I met her in town. Name's Kayla.

**维尔汀**：……凯拉？\
**Vertin**: Kayla?

眼前的少女笑盈盈地望了过来。\
The girl smiles brightly at her.

**维尔汀**：……你认识一个叫阿尔古斯的人吗？\
**Vertin**: Do you know someone called Argus?

挎着篮子的少女甜甜地笑了。\
The girl's smile becomes more gentle.

**凯拉**：我从来没有听过这个名字。真奇怪，怎么有人会给孩子取百眼巨人的名字？\
**Kayla**: The name doesn't ring a bell. How strange! What kind of parent would name their child after a one-hundred-eyed giant?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**凯拉**：我想这只是重名——凯拉是个很常见的名字，就像爱玛、安娜、凯瑟琳，它们略有差异，但本质上并无不同。倒是小姐您……\
**Kayla**: You must've mistaken me for someone else. Kayla is a common name, after all, like Emma, Anna, or Catherine. More importantly, Miss, you look ...

女孩微笑着。\
The girl smiles once more.

**凯拉**：虽然我之前从来没有见过您，但总觉得您很亲切。\
**Kayla**: Although I've never met you before, you seem familiar.

她将手伸进了篮子，片刻后，从中掏出了一支皱巴巴的花朵。\
She reaches into the basket and pulls out a crumpled flower.

一只素色的飞蛾落在了花瓣上，轻轻抖动着它的翅膀，鳞粉扑朔。\
A pale moth lands on a petal, gently fluttering its wings, its scales shimmering in the morning light.

**凯拉**：希望您能拥有一天的好心情。\
**Kayla**: I hope you have a wonderful day.

**维尔汀**：……谢谢。\
**Vertin**: Thank you.

女孩将花朵送入了她的怀中。\
The girl tucks the flower under her arm.

**维尔汀**：您是这儿的住客吗？\
**Vertin**: Are you a guest at this motel?

少女微微地点了点头。\
The girl nods.

**凯拉**：这儿发生了什么事吗？\
**Kayla**: What happened here?

**维尔汀**：圣洛夫基金会已经接管了这座旅馆——这个场所涉及了不少危险案件，我不建议您继续居住在这里。\
**Vertin**: The St. Pavlov Foundation has taken over. I suggest you find alternative accommodation, given the dangerous incidents that have occurred here.

**凯拉**：嗯……那我该怎么办？我的东西还在旅馆里……\
**Kayla**: Hmm. What should I do? All my things are still inside.

**维尔汀**：稍后会有基金会的职员来处理这些问题，您可以相信他们。\
**Vertin**: The Foundation staff will take care of it for you later. You can trust them.

**凯拉**：我能先去拿回我的东西吗？\
**Kayla**: Can't I just go and get my things now?

**维尔汀**：我会建议您在基金会的职员到场后，再进入这个旅馆。\
**Vertin**: I would advise you to wait until the Foundation staff arrive.

**凯拉**：啊呀，好心的小姐，您不用担心这些……我自然有我的办法。\
**Kayla**: Oh, I can look after myself. No need to worry about me, Miss.

女孩眨了眨眼睛，推开了那扇紧闭着的门扉，随即消失在了众人的视野之中。\
The girl winks and pushes open the motel door, promptly disappearing from their view.

**红弩箭**：这个女孩……\
**Lilya**: That girl ...

久未发言的飞行员开口了。\
Lilya breaks her long silence.

**维尔汀**：怎么了？\
**Vertin**: What about her?

**红弩箭**：不，我想应该是我的错觉。\
**Lilya**: Never mind. It's probably nothing.

不远处，传送软盘的辉光一闪而过。\
The light from a teleportation disk flickers nearby.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：抱歉，维尔汀小姐。\
**Foundation Staff I**: Apologies for our delayed arrival, Ms. Vertin.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：在不久之前，我们一直无法定位到这个旅馆的位置，就像是有什么东西在故意干扰我们的判断……\
**Foundation Staff I**: We'd been unable to locate the motel until about ten minutes ago. It's as if something was deliberately interfering with our sense of direction.

正当基金会职员忙于了解情况之时，旅馆的深处忽然再次传出了模糊的回音。\
While the Foundation staff is busy assessing the situation, a faint sound echoes from the depths of the motel.

**蓝手帕**：噢……\
**Tuesday**: Oh.

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

门扉赫然打开，一具青白色的尸体混同着垃圾一并涌出。\
The door suddenly swings open, and a pale, trash-covered corpse is thrown out of it.

**蓝手帕**：它总是不听我的劝告，执意地要吃地上的垃圾——是不是所有的孩子都是这样？\
**Tuesday**: Once again, it insisted on eating garbage off the floor. Is every child this stubborn?

**红弩箭**：……\
**Lilya**: ...

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：……\
**Foundation Staff I**: ...

**维尔汀**：……这是史蒂文，一名隶属于芝诺的军官。\
**Vertin**: It's Stefen, a Zeno officer.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：……史蒂文，耳熟的名字。\
**Foundation Staff I**: Hmm, Stefen. Sounds familiar.

职员熟练地翻动着文件，他很快就找到了想要的内容。\
The staff member flips through his records, quickly finding the information he's looking for.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：的确是个颇有来头的人。资料显示他是芝诺的高级军官，在泄露阿尔卡纳真空弹视频之后就不知所踪。\
**Foundation Staff I**: The records show he was a high-ranking Zeno officer who went missing after the vacuum bomb footage leaked.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：芝诺对此人发布了悬赏令，上面写着一个令人咋舌的数字……看来他的行为彻底地惹怒了伊戈尔将军。\
**Foundation Staff I**: Zeno issued a staggering bounty on him. I guess whatever he did really angered Admiral Igor.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：谁也不会想到他就躲在这个小旅馆中……意外收获。\
**Foundation Staff I**: Who would've thought he'd be hiding in this little motel in the middle of nowhere?

**维尔汀**：显然他的运气不怎么好。\
**Vertin**: Obviously, luck wasn't on his side.

**基金会职员Ⅰ**：很抱歉对您造成了困扰，维尔汀小姐，接下来我们会接管这件事。\
**Foundation Staff I**: Alright, Ms. Vertin, we'll take over from here.

**蓝手帕**：……\
**Tuesday**: ...

**蓝手帕**：眼前的侍应生不为所动，只是轻轻地拍打着襁褓。\
**Tuesday**: The maid remains calm, gently patting the bundle in her arms.

**维尔汀**：……在分部完成他们的流程之后，您会被送往总部，我们将对您做出一个更全面的评估。\
**Vertin**: After the branch completes its procedures, you'll be sent to the headquarters for a more thorough assessment.

**蓝手帕**：……我还能和我的孩子在一起吗？\
**Tuesday**: Will you return my baby to me?

**维尔汀**：现在还不到谈论这些的时候。\
**Vertin**: It's too early to discuss that.

**维尔汀**：走吧，红弩箭。\
**Vertin**: Let's go, Lilya.

她提起了手提箱。\
She picks up the suitcase.

**维尔汀**：我们得回去向Z女士汇报关于兀尔德女士的消息。\
**Vertin**: We must report back to Madam Z about Urd.

## THH-20 往日不再 / Gone Are the Old Days

**凯拉**：……噢，看来我不在的时候，这儿发生了许多故事。\
**Kayla**: Oh dear. It seems a lot transpired while I was away.

**凯拉**：……\
**Kayla**: ...

在思考之后，她拨通了手中的电话。一阵等候音之后，电话被接通了。\
After a moment's thought, she dials a number on her phone. A few rings later, the call is answered.

**金伯利女郎**：……淑女格蕾丝，你终于联系我了！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Ms. Grace, I thought you'd forgotten me!

**金伯利女郎**：我被发现了！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I've been exposed!

不出意料地，电话彼端传来了躁动不安的声音。\
As expected, the voice on the other end is restless.

**淑女格蕾丝**：金伯利，你可以告诉我旅馆里到底发生了什么吗？为什么走廊里会有一摊血迹和少许的脑浆，谁死在了这里？\
**Ms. Grace**: Kimberly, care to tell me what happened in this motel? There's blood and brains splattered in the hallway. Who died and how?

**金伯利女郎**：……是那个芝诺人，他发疯了，对着自己的太阳穴来了一枪。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: It was that Zeno madman! He shot himself in the head!

**金伯利女郎**：他虽然死了，但我还没来得及销毁他床底下的术阵……我也还没来得及找到……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: But I still haven't managed to destroy the ritual sigils under his bed. And I couldn't find the ...

**淑女格蕾丝**：……\
**Ms. Grace**: ...

少女轻轻地叹了一口气。\
She sighs.

**淑女格蕾丝**：据点暴露了，我们得带走所有有关于“仪式”的东西，离开这个地方。\
**Ms. Grace**: Now that our base of operations has been exposed, we'll have to take away everything related to the "ritual" and leave.

**淑女格蕾丝**：基金会的人在不久之后就会对这里进行全面的搜查。\
**Ms. Grace**: The Foundation's rats will thoroughly search this place soon.

**金伯利女郎**：——我可不想和那些灰白格子打交道！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Ugh, the last thing I need right now is to deal with them!

电话彼端传来了短暂的沉默，这不常见。\
There's a brief and unusual silence on the other end of the line.

**金伯利女郎**：不过……您能告诉我，维尔汀是一个怎样的人吗？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: And, uh, could you tell me more about this Vertin?

电话对面，她的语气有些惴惴不安。\
There's a hint of anxiety in her voice.

**金伯利女郎**：我不小心让她知道了一个大秘密——她的记忆力好吗？会把一件事记很久吗？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I might've had a slip of the tongue when she confronted me earlier. How good is her memory?

**淑女格蕾丝**：不用那么忧虑，金伯利。人很少会关心自己以外的事。\
**Ms. Grace**: Fret not, Kimberly. People rarely pay attention to things that don't directly involve them.

少女露出了淡淡的微笑。\
She smiles faintly.

**淑女格蕾丝**：……但我很期待与她的下一次见面。\
**Ms. Grace**: But I do look forward to seeing her again.

数日后。\
Several days later.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：蓝手帕小姐，无需担忧，您大可把这次对谈看作是一次普通的对话。\
**Foundation Staff II**: We're just here to have a conversation, Ms. Tuesday. Relax.

**蓝手帕**：……我是在一个荒原中拾到它的。\
**Tuesday**: I found it in the wilderness.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：它是指那个具备神秘学力量的“旅馆”吗？\
**Foundation Staff II**: You mean, the "motel" with arcane powers?

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：和您确认一下，这个神秘学意识的本体，就是您襁褓中所包裹的……形似心脏的胚胎，对吗？\
**Foundation Staff II**: Just to confirm, the base form of this arcane consciousness is a heart-shaped "fetus," correct?

**蓝手帕**：是的。\
**Tuesday**: Yes.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：它的智力约等于一岁的婴儿，并不具备策划和实施这种行为的能力——而它视您为母亲，对您有着异乎寻常的信任与依赖……\
**Foundation Staff II**: It's about as intelligent as a one-year-old human, and it lacks the ability to deliberately plan or cause the incidents in the motel. Meanwhile, it sees you as its mother, displaying remarkable trust and dependence on you.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：……我们认为您也参与了这些行动。或者说，您才是那个幕后的人。\
**Foundation Staff II**: Therefore, we believe you were a major contributor to these incidents, or rather, the one who pulled the strings.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：也许您并不具备主观上的恶性，但事实如此，因为您而精神崩溃的人在镇子上比比皆是。\
**Foundation Staff II**: You may not have acted with evil intent, but your actions have caused many residents in Chisos to suffer mental breakdowns.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：……所以，他们会寻求一些精神上的解脱——正是因为这个原因，重塑之手对这个镇子进行了史无前例的渗透。\
**Foundation Staff II**: They were seeking some form of relief from their mental anguish, which provided the perfect opportunity for the Manus to entrench themselves so deeply in this town.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：我说得对吗？\
**Foundation Staff II**: Isn't that so, Ms. Tuesday?

**蓝手帕**：噢……我从来没去过那个镇子，不知道那儿的情况……但如果真如您所说的那样。\
**Tuesday**: Well, I've never been to that town. And even if it is as you say ...

**蓝手帕**：这也是他们自己的选择，不是吗？\
**Tuesday**: They made their choices, didn't they?

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：……明白了。\
**Foundation Staff II**: I see.

沙沙的声音响起，职员在笔录上记载了关键的信息。\
She scribbles down the information on her clipboard.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：在不久之前，司辰向基金会提交了另一个关键信息。\
**Foundation Staff II**: The Timekeeper just reported another crucial piece of information to the Foundation.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：在您的旅馆中，是否有自称隶属于“启明会”的信徒活动？\
**Foundation Staff II**: Were there any activities going on in the motel undertaken by the self-proclaimed followers of the Order of Enlightenment?

**蓝手帕**：噢……是的，他们离开得不久，我还能记住他们的脸。\
**Tuesday**: Oh, there indeed were. They left not long ago. I still remember their faces.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：他们做了什么？\
**Foundation Staff II**: What did they do at the motel?

**蓝手帕**：他们在地板上乱涂乱画，发出些奇怪的声音……噢，我想起来了。\
**Tuesday**: They scribbled on the floor and made strange noises. Oh, I remember now.

**蓝手帕**：他们似乎想要尝试什么东西……只是这种尝试并未成功，反而闹出了不少笑话——有一个可怜的女孩被他们关入了镜子里……\
**Tuesday**: Whatever it was they were trying to do, it was a total failure. One poor girl became trapped inside their mirror.

**蓝手帕**：她从未放弃过逃生的尝试。一到深夜，那扇镜子就会发出“砰砰”的响声……哈。\
**Tuesday**: She never stopped trying to escape. The mirror would make banging noises all night long, haha.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：……我们在搜查旅馆的时候，并未发现任何被困在镜子里的人。\
**Foundation Staff II**: We didn't find anyone trapped in a mirror during our search.

**蓝手帕**：噢，那就是……可惜了。\
**Tuesday**: Well, that's sad, I suppose.

侍应生神色平静，一如往昔。\
Her expression remains calm as always.

**基金会职员Ⅱ**：既然您知道他们是具有危险性的神秘学家团体，为何不及时向基金会申报呢？\
**Foundation Staff II**: If you knew they were from a dangerous arcanist organization, why didn't you report them to the Foundation?

**蓝手帕**：啊……\
**Tuesday**: Ah.

**蓝手帕**：这与我有什么关系……？\
**Tuesday**: Why would I?

侍应生舔了舔略有干裂的嘴唇。\
She licks her lips.

**蓝手帕**：我并不会感到害怕。不如说——\
**Tuesday**: Fear doesn't frighten me. No, quite the contrary ...

**蓝手帕**：我一直在期待着这一天。\
**Tuesday**: It excites me. I would embrace fear any day of the week.
